# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Scaling Up Thermodynamic AI Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00170)
*Andrew G. Moore*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可扩展的、基于反向传播（backpropagation）的训练算法，使高温吉布斯采样（Gibbs-sampled）伊辛模型（Ising model）热力学计算设备能够实现深度卷积网络的推理，并在CIFAR-10和CIFAR-100上分别达到94.9%和76.0%的准确率；同时建立了推理成本与精度之间的数学理论，并证明推理成本与性能之间存在可控的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于伊辛模型的热力学计算设备在低功耗人工智能推理（AI inference）和边缘计算（edge computing）方面具有巨大潜力，但缺乏可扩展的方法来训练用于此类硬件的大规模模型。

Method: 将高温吉布斯采样伊辛系统的时间平均行为与前馈神经推理（feed-forward neural inference）之间的理论对应关系转化为一种纯反向传播的训练算法；开发了推理成本与精度之间关系的数学理论，并推导了最优推理调度（inference schedule）的算法。

Result: 图像分类模型在CIFAR-10上达到94.9%的准确率，在CIFAR-100上达到76.0%的准确率（采用二值吉布斯采样）。推理成本与性能之间存在可控的权衡关系，并给出了渐近结果。

Conclusion: 该工作为高温热力学AI模型（thermodynamic AI models）的硬件开发提供了理论依据和算法支撑，指明了未来的发展方向。

Abstract: Thermodynamic computing devices based on the Ising model show great promise for low-power AI inference and edge computing, but scalable methods for training large models for such hardware remain limited. Prior theory shows that the time-averaged behavior of high-temperature Gibbs-sampled Ising systems can implement feed-forward neural inference. We turn this theoretical correspondence into a scalable and purely backpropagation-based algorithm for training deep convolutional networks for thermodynamic inference on Ising machine hardware. Our image classification models achieve accuracies of 94.9% on CIFAR-10 and 76.0% on CIFAR-100 under binary Gibbs sampling. We then develop and experimentally validate a mathematical theory relating inference cost to accuracy and controlling autocorrelation times. Subsequently, we calculate asymptotic results showing that inference cost is bounded by a well-controlled tradeoff with performance and exhibit algorithms for computing optimal inference schedules. Finally, we discuss implications for hardware development and the future of high-temperature thermodynamic AI models.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.str-el'></div>

# cond-mat.str-el [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Dissipation splits the Mott transition in one dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00086)
*Oscar Bouverot-Dupuis,Alberto Rosso,Laura Foini*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文研究了耗散（dissipation）如何改变一维莫特相变（Mott transition）的性质。通过玻色化（bosonisation）和精确积分浴自由度，作者发现耗散会使原本直接的Luttinger液体-莫特绝缘体相变分裂为两个不同的临界现象：先是Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变进入一个中间耗散相（dissipative phase, DP），该相可压缩且无能隙但无超流刚度；随后是一个新的公度-非公度（commensurate-incommensurate）相变进入莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator, MI）。临界指数随浴指数s连续变化，蒙特卡洛模拟定量支持了理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解耗散如何修正量子相变（quantum phase transitions）是多体物理学（many-body physics）中的一个核心挑战。一维莫特相变在孤立系统中分隔了导电的Luttinger液体（Luttinger liquid, LL）和莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator, MI），而该研究旨在揭示局域耦合到密度的耗散浴（dissipative baths）对这一相变命运的影响。

Method: 采用玻色化（bosonisation）方法对系统进行理论处理，并对浴自由度（bath degrees of freedom）进行精确积分，从而将耗散效应纳入有效场论框架。对于公度-非公度相变，推导了有效场论（effective field theory）并刻画了其普适性（universality）。此外，采用最先进的蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）对理论预测进行定量验证。

Result: 耗散在浴指数（bath exponent）$s<3/2$时从根本上重塑了相图（phase diagram）。系统并未发生直接的LL-MI相变，而是出现一个中间耗散相（dissipative phase, DP），该相可压缩（compressible）且无能隙（gapless），但超流刚度（superfluid stiffness）为零。传统的莫特相变分裂为两个不同的临界现象：从LL到DP的BKT相变，以及从DP到MI的新的公度-非公度相变。对于$1<s<3/2$，临界指数随浴指数连续变化：$β=ν=1/z=s-1$；对于$s<1$，$β=ν=1/z=0$，掺杂（doping）以比任何幂律（power law）更快的速度消失。蒙特卡洛模拟定量支持了理论预测。

Conclusion: 耗散能够定性改变莫特相变的性质，并在强关联一维系统中产生新颖的临界行为（novel critical behaviour）。

Abstract: Understanding how dissipation modifies quantum phase transitions is a central challenge in many-body physics. A paradigmatic example is the one-dimensional Mott transition, which in isolated systems separates a conducting Luttinger liquid (LL) from a Mott insulator (MI). Here, we study the fate of this transition in the presence of dissipative baths locally coupled to the density. Using bosonisation and an exact integration of the bath degrees of freedom, we show that dissipation fundamentally reshapes the phase diagram for bath exponents $s<3/2$, where $s$ characterises the low-energy bath spectrum. Rather than undergoing a direct LL-MI transition, the system develops an intermediate dissipative phase (DP) that is compressible and gapless, yet has zero superfluid stiffness. As a result, the conventional Mott transition splits into two distinct critical phenomena: a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition from the LL to the DP, followed by a new commensurate-incommensurate transition from the DP to the MI. We derive an effective field theory for the latter transition and characterize its universality. For $1<s<3/2$, the critical exponents vary continuously with the bath exponent as $β=ν=1/z=s-1$, while for $s<1$ the transition is governed by $β=ν=1/z=0$ and the doping vanishes sharper than any power law. State-of-the-art Monte Carlo simulations quantitatively support our predictions. These results demonstrate that dissipation can qualitatively alter the nature of the Mott transition and generate novel critical behaviour in strongly correlated one-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [3] [Phase distinction of Gibbs states without symmetry breaking: topological invariants of the 3D toric code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00134)
*Haruki Watanabe*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究三维 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 环面码（toric code）在有限温度和一般磁场下的拓扑序（topological order），其中所有更高形式对称性（higher-form symmetry）都被显式破缺。研究表明，拓扑纠缠熵（topological entanglement entropy）在拓扑相中依然保持 $\gamma = \ln 2$ 的量子化值，并在热相变时降为零；该量子化由 Bianchi 恒等式（Bianchi identity）几何保护，而非精确对称性。但该值并非准局域信道不变量；为此引入解码 Wilson 环关联（decoded Wilson-loop correlation）$f_W$，它作为混合态（mixed state）的稳健拓扑不变量（topological invariant），在拓扑相中趋于 $1$，在平凡相中趋于 $0$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有限温度和破缺对称性场下三维 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 环面码（toric code）中拓扑序（topological order）的鲁棒性，并厘清拓扑纠缠熵（topological entanglement entropy）的量子化是否依赖于精确对称性，以及混合态（mixed state）中是否存在更稳健的拓扑不变量（topological invariant）。

Method: 采用微扰分析（perturbative analysis）结合大规模量子蒙特卡洛模拟（large-scale quantum Monte Carlo），通过计算有限温度下的拓扑纠缠熵（topological entanglement entropy）和解码 Wilson 环关联（decoded Wilson-loop correlation）来表征拓扑相变。

Result: 在拓扑相中，拓扑纠缠熵保持 $\gamma = \ln 2$ 的量子化值，直至热相变（thermal transition）时才降为零；该量子化由 Bianchi 恒等式（Bianchi identity）几何保护，而非精确对称性。然而，该值在恒定深度信道下可从平凡乘积态（trivial product state）产生。相比之下，解码 Wilson 环关联 $f_W$ 在热力学极限下于拓扑相中趋于 $1$，于平凡相中趋于 $0$，并且是准局域信道不变量（quasi-local-channel invariant）。

Conclusion: 在三维 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 环面码（toric code）中，有限温度拓扑序（topological order）的拓扑纠缠熵（topological entanglement entropy）虽能保持量子化，但并非混合态拓扑相的稳健判据；解码 Wilson 环关联（decoded Wilson-loop correlation）$f_W$ 作为准局域信道不变量（quasi-local-channel invariant），为表征混合态（mixed state）拓扑相提供了更可靠的拓扑不变量（topological invariant）。

Abstract: We study the finite-temperature topological order of the three-dimensional $\mathbb{Z}_2$ toric code in a generic magnetic field, where every higher-form symmetry is explicitly broken and can at most be emergent. We show perturbatively, and confirm by large-scale quantum Monte Carlo, that the topological entanglement entropy stays quantized at $γ= \ln 2$ throughout the topological phase -- at finite temperature and under the symmetry-breaking field alike -- and collapses to $0$ across the thermal transition, a quantization protected geometrically by the Bianchi identity rather than by any exact symmetry of the system. The plateau $γ= \ln 2$ is, however, not invariant under quasi-local channels: a constant-depth channel can generate this identical quantized value from a trivial product state. We therefore introduce the decoded Wilson-loop correlation $f_W$, which quantizes to $1$ in the topological phase and $0$ in the trivial phase as $L\to\infty$ and, unlike $γ$, is a quasi-local-channel invariant -- a robust topological invariant of the mixed state.

</details>


### [4] [Holographic Quantum Transformer: A Generalist Neuro-Symbolic Architecture for Solving Frustrated Systems via Generative Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00398)
*Xingran Guo,Tiaojie Xiao,Jie Liu,Keqin Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出全息量子变换器（Holographic Quantum Transformer, HQT），一种基于自注意力机制（self-attention）的生成式架构，用于克服阻挫量子多体问题中的符号困难（sign problem）和希尔伯特空间复杂度（Hilbert space complexity）。在方格子J₁-J₂海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）上验证，HQT在8×8阻挫临界点达到高精度基态能量，并提出了“全息转移”（Holographic Transfer）零样本外推协议，实现从小尺寸到大尺寸晶格的高保真初始化与快速收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维阻挫量子物质的模拟面临符号问题和指数级希尔伯特空间复杂度的巨大挑战（grand challenge），亟需一种能够高效处理非局域纠缠（non-local entanglement）模式的可扩展计算范式。

Method: 提出全息量子变换器（HQT），利用全局自注意力（global self-attention）机制解析非局域纠缠结构；并设计了“全息转移”（Holographic Transfer）零样本外推协议，通过连续位置嵌入插值（continuous positional-embedding interpolation）和注意力头重置（head re-initialization），将小尺寸晶格训练好的模型直接投影到更大尺寸晶格上。

Result: 在8×8阻挫临界点（J₂=0.5）处，HQT达到基态能量E/N=-0.5001(1)，符合有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）预期；通过可解释注意力图（interpretable attention maps）自主恢复出J₂相互作用几何。零样本外推至10×10晶格后，能量E/N=-0.49782(3)，与变分最优结果统计一致。

Conclusion: 生成式注意力（generative attention）机制为可迁移量子模拟（transferable quantum simulation）提供了一种可扩展的新范式，有望在更广泛的阻挫量子系统中实现零样本迁移。

Abstract: Simulating two-dimensional frustrated quantum matter is a grand challenge due to the sign problem and exponential Hilbert space complexity. In this work, we introduce the Holographic Quantum Transformer (HQT), a physics-inspired generative architecture that leverages global self-attention to resolve non-local entanglement patterns. We validate HQT on the square lattice $J_1-J_2$ Heisenberg model. On the heavily frustrated $8 \times 8$ lattice at the quantum critical point ($J_2=0.5$), HQT reaches a ground-state energy per site ($E/N$) of $\mathbf{-0.5001(1)}$, consistent with the expected finite-size scaling trend. Beyond numerical accuracy, HQT exhibits intrinsic physical awareness, autonomously recovering the underlying $J_2$ interaction geometry through interpretable attention maps. Our central contribution is ``Holographic Transfer", a zero-shot size-extrapolation protocol with rapid alignment: a model trained on $8 \times 8$ systems is directly projected onto larger $10 \times 10$ lattices via continuous positional-embedding interpolation and head re-initialization, achieving high-fidelity initialization and rapid convergence. This zero-shot protocol yields an energy of $E/N = \mathbf{-0.49782(3)}$, statistically consistent with the variational state of the art while requiring no from-scratch training on the target lattice. Our results establish generative attention as a scalable paradigm for transferable quantum simulation.

</details>


### [5] [Weak Ferromagnetism in NiS$_2$ under Nanocrystallization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00474)
*Hayato Miyazaki,Tomohiko Yoshinaga,Ojiro Miyazaki,Akira Matsuo,Koichi Kindo,Hirofumi Ishii,Tatsuya Kawae,Tetsuya Kida,Masashi Nantoh,Yoichi Ishiwata*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过磁化与热容测量发现，结构有序的NiS₂纳米晶（平均直径27.0±6.5 nm）保持体材料的双步反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）转变，但在低温下表现出大矫顽力、交换偏置（exchange bias）和垂直回线偏移等铁磁（ferromagnetic）响应，这归因于纳米晶表面反铁磁序终止产生的未补偿表面磁矩；同时，未观察到明显的体材料弱铁磁（weak-ferromagnetic）分量，排除了均匀倾斜模型，间接支持了磁畴壁（domain-wall）机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究NiS₂纳米晶是否保留体材料的反铁磁特性，并探索其低温铁磁行为的物理起源，特别是表面未补偿磁矩、均匀倾斜模型（uniform canting model）与畴壁机制（domain-wall mechanism）之间的竞争关系。

Method: 合成了结构有序的NiS₂纳米晶（平均直径27.0±6.5 nm），通过磁化测量（magnetization measurements）和热容测量（heat-capacity measurements）表征其磁性与热力学行为，并在场冷（field cooling）条件下分析磁滞回线特征。

Result: 纳米晶保留了体材料的两步反铁磁转变；低温下表现出具有大矫顽力（coercivity）、交换偏置和垂直回线偏移的铁磁响应，而略高于转变温度时M-H曲线接近线性；未观察到明显的体材料弱铁磁分量。

Conclusion: NiS₂纳米晶的低温铁磁行为最佳解释为纳米晶表面反铁磁序终止产生的未补偿表面磁矩（uncompensated surface moments）；缺乏额外弱铁磁分量的实验事实排除了均匀倾斜模型，间接支持畴壁机制作为体材料弱铁磁性的来源。

Abstract: Structurally well-ordered NiS$_2$ nanocrystals with an average diameter of $27.0 \pm 6.5$ nm retain the bulk-like two-step antiferromagnetic transitions, as shown by magnetization and heat-capacity measurements. Below the lower transition, the nanocrystals exhibit a hysteretic ferromagnetic response with large coercivity, exchange bias, and a vertical loop shift after field cooling, whereas the $M$-$H$ response just above the transition is nearly linear. These features are best explained by uncompensated surface moments generated where the low-temperature antiferromagnetic order terminates at the nanocrystal surface. The absence of a clear additional bulk-like weak-ferromagnetic component constrains homogeneous-canting models and indirectly favors a domain-wall scenario for the weak ferromagnetism of bulk NiS$_2$.

</details>


### [6] [Strongly frustrated 2D magnetism in a 3D hexagonal perovskite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00532)
*Bocheng Yu,Otkur Omar,Songtai Lv,Long Ma,Zhengcai Xia,Jing Meng,Yanran Yang,Jie Ma,Yang Xu,Qingfeng Zhan,Vladimir Yu. Pomjakushin,Haiyuan Zou,Shang Gao,Toni Shiroka,Tian Shang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过核磁共振、中子散射和μ子自旋谱学三种实验手段，发现六方钙钛矿材料Ba₂La₂MnTe₂O₁₂在4.4 K以下表现出理想二维磁性：锰磁矩在ab面内形成120°反铁磁序，c轴方向保持无序，且该体系具有显著强于多数已知磁有序系统的几何阻挫（geometric frustration）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索低维磁性（low-dimensional magnetism）自旋体系中可能出现的奇异量子现象，并寻找强阻挫二维磁性在三维六方钙钛矿中的实际实例。

Method: 联合运用核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance, NMR）、中子散射（neutron scattering）和μ子自旋谱学（muon-spin spectroscopy, μSR）三种互补技术，对Ba₂La₂MnTe₂O₁₂的磁结构、自旋动力学及内部场分布进行综合表征。

Result: 该材料在T_N≈4.4 K进入磁有序态，锰磁矩在ab面内形成120°反铁磁结构，c轴方向无序。零场μSR测量揭示持续强自旋涨落（spin fluctuations）和大的内场分布，阻挫程度远超多数已知磁有序阻挫体系。

Conclusion: Ba₂La₂MnTe₂O₁₂是三维六方钙钛矿中罕见的强阻挫二维磁性实例，该发现挑战了对其他同类材料磁有序的传统解释，并揭示了维度性（dimensionality）对奇异磁态的调控作用。

Abstract: Exotic quantum phenomena are often found to occur in spin systems that exhibit low-dimensional magnetism. By combining nuclear magnetic resonance, neutron scattering, and muon-spin spectroscopy ($μ$SR) techniques, we report a rare instance of strongly frustrated two-dimensional (2D) magnetism in a three-dimensional (3D) hexagonal perovskite. Here, Ba$_2$La$_2$MnTe$_2$O$_{12}$, a triangular-lattice magnet, is shown to undergo a magnetic transition at $T_\mathrm{N} \approx$ 4.4 K, below which the manganese moments form a 120$^{\circ}$ AFM order within the $ab$-plane, while staying disordered along the $c$-axis. This exotic ground state, which exhibits ideal 2D magnetism, is highly consistent with the persistently strong spin fluctuations and the large internal field distributions revealed by zero-field $μ$SR. Further, the 2D magnetism also leads to a significant frustration, much larger than that of most known magnetically-ordered frustrated systems. Our work on Ba$_2$La$_2$MnTe$_2$O$_{12}$ not only challenges the interpretations of magnetic order in other 3D hexagonal perovskites, but it also provides insight into how the dimensionality affects the exotic magnetic states.

</details>


### [7] [Quantum Oscillations of $\mathrm{Sr}_2\mathrm{RuO}_4$ under c-Axis Uniaxial Stress](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00679)
*Fabian Jerzembeck,Maximilian T. Pelly,Helge Rosner,Edgar Abarca Morales,Naoki Kikugawa,Dmitry A. Sokolov,Andrew P. Mackenzie,Andreas W. Rost,Elena Hassinger,Javier F. Landaeta*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过 dHvA 效应测量了在 c 轴单轴应力（uniaxial stress）下非常规超导体 Sr₂RuO₄ 的费米面（Fermi surface）演化，发现空穴型 α 能带面积增大、电子型 β 能带面积减小而 γ 能带面积增大，指出电荷转移（charge transfer）是逼近 Lifshitz 相变（Lifshitz transition）与 Van Hove 奇点（Van Hove singularity）的机制，且有效质量略有增强。结果表明，单轴应力下的量子振荡测量结合能带计算是研究量子材料的有力新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单轴应力已广泛用于关联电子材料研究，但压电施加应力下电子结构演化的费米面分辨实验数据匮乏，且尚无单轴应力下 de Haas-van Alphen（dHvA）效应的报道。本文旨在填补这一空白，并解释电子态密度（density of states）预期增强与 Tc 实际被抑制之间的矛盾行为。

Method: 对非常规超导体 Sr₂RuO₄ 施加 c 轴单轴应力（应力范围至 -1.8 GPa），进行 dHvA 测量以跟踪所有费米面的演化，并结合磁致伸缩（magnetostriction）中的量子振荡及能带结构计算进行对比验证。

Result: 空穴型 α 能带截面积增大，电子型 β 能带截面积减小，电子型 γ 能带截面积增大；所有三个费米面的有效质量在逼近 Lifshitz 相变时均略有增强；dHvA 结果与磁致伸缩量子振荡及能带计算吻合良好。

Conclusion: 与面内单轴应力不同，c 轴应力下电荷转移是逼近电子-空穴 Lifshitz 相变及关联 Van Hove 奇点的主要机制。单轴应力下的量子振荡测量结合能带结构计算，为研究量子材料提供了一种有前景的新途径。

Abstract: Uniaxial stress has now been widely used to study correlated electron materials. However, Fermi surface-resolved experimental data on the evolution of the electronic structure under piezoelectrically applied stress are sparse, with no reports of de Haas-van Alphen (dHvA) effects under uniaxial stress. Here we present dHvA measurements under $c$-axis uniaxial stress on the unconventional superconductor $\mathrm{Sr}_2\mathrm{RuO}_4$. This allows us to study the evolution of the electronic structure directly and to gain insight into the contradicting behavior of the predicted enhancement of the electronic density of states and the observed suppression of $T_\text{c}$. We are able to follow all Fermi surfaces for stress up to $-1.8$~GPa and find that the cross-sectional areas of the hole-like $α$ sheet increase and electron-like $β$ sheet decrease. At the same time, the area of the electron-like $γ$ sheet increases. Therefore, in contrast to in-plane uniaxial stress, charge transfer is the mechanism for approaching the electron-to-hole Lifshitz transition and the associated Van Hove singularity. Additionally, we find that the effective masses on all three Fermi sheets are slightly enhanced as the Lifshitz transition is approached. We compare the dHvA results with quantum oscillations in the magnetostriction and band structure calculations, and find good agreement. At a more general level, our findings show that quantum oscillation measurements under uniaxial stress, combined with band-structure calculations, offer a promising new route for studying quantum materials.

</details>


### [8] [Weak-coupling tensor cross interpolation impurity solver for nonequilibrium dynamical mean-field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00702)
*Shuta Matsuura,Hiroshi Shinaoka,Philipp Werner,Naoto Tsuji*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于弱耦合展开和张量交叉插值（tensor cross interpolation, TCI）的非平衡杂质求解器，用于非平衡动力学平均场理论（DMFT）。该方法将高维积分核近似为张量链（tensor-train）形式，无需随机采样即可高效计算，缓解了连续时间量子蒙特卡洛（CT-QMC）方法中的符号问题（sign problem）。基准测试和半满Hubbard模型计算验证了其准确性；在远离半满情形下，该方法仍可控。该求解器还可用于稳态DMFT，无需解析延拓即可获得金属态的光谱函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模拟非平衡量子多体系统因计算复杂度随实时呈指数增长而极具挑战，传统连续时间量子蒙特卡洛方法在高维积分中面临严重的符号问题（sign problem）。本文旨在开发一种无需随机采样、能够缓解符号问题的新型非平衡杂质求解器。

Method: 基于弱耦合展开（weak-coupling expansion）和张量交叉插值（tensor cross interpolation, TCI），将高维积分中的被积函数近似为张量链（tensor-train）形式，实现高效数值求积，避免蒙特卡洛随机采样。

Result: 对精确可解的非平衡杂质模型的基准测试与精确解高度一致，并揭示被积函数具有低秩结构。在半满Hubbard模型的相互作用淬火问题中，该方法以与CT-QMC相当的精度重现了临界相互作用强度下的快速热化（fast thermalization）。在3/4填充情形下，该方法仍保持可控，揭示出连续性交叉（crossover）而非尖锐定义的快速热化点。应用于稳态DMFT时，无需解析延拓即可在金属态区域获得准确的光谱函数。

Conclusion: 该基于TCI的非平衡杂质求解器在弱耦合展开框架下有效缓解了符号问题，在远离半满等困难条件下仍表现稳健，并能直接应用于稳态DMFT问题，是非平衡量子多体模拟的一种有前景的新方法。

Abstract: Simulating nonequilibrium quantum many-body systems remains a major challenge due to the exponential growth of the computational complexity with real time. Here we implement a nonequilibrium impurity solver based on the weak-coupling expansion and the tensor cross interpolation (TCI), and apply it to nonequilibrium dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT). The method approximates the integrands of the high-dimensional integrals arising in the weak-coupling expansion in a tensor-train form, enabling efficient evaluations without stochastic sampling and thereby mitigating the sign problem affecting continuous-time quantum Monte Carlo (CT-QMC) methods. Benchmark calculations for an exactly solvable nonequilibrium impurity model agree well with the exact results and reveal a low-rank structure of the integrands. When applied to interaction-quench problems in the half-filled Hubbard model, the method reproduces fast thermalization at a critical interaction strength with accuracy comparable to CT-QMC. Away from half filling, where the sign problem becomes even more severe, the present approach remains well controlled, revealing a crossover instead of a sharply defined fast thermalization point in the 3/4-filled case. The solver can also be applied to steady-state DMFT problems, yielding accurate spectral functions in the metallic regime without analytic continuation.

### [9] [Deconfined criticality between an antiferromagnetic insulator and a nodal d-wave superconductor: a quantum Monte Carlo study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00762)
*Chuang Chen,Subir Sachdev,Zi Yang Meng*

TL;DR: 该论文通过量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）方法，在π-flux背景和SU(2)晶格规范场（lattice gauge field）耦合下，利用部分子表示（parton representation）研究平方晶格半填充时绝缘性Néel态与节线d波超导体（nodal d-wave superconductor）之间的相变。研究发现了二阶退禁闭量子相变（second-order deconfined quantum phase transition），并分析了电子及自旋子-荷子复合体的色散关系。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统直接基于电子自由度的研究对Néel态与d波超导态之间相变的性质（如一阶还是二阶、是否存在退禁闭行为）尚未给出统一结论。本研究引入部分子表示和规范场框架，试图从新的微观视角澄清该相变的临界行为。

Method: 采用量子蒙特卡洛方法，引入费米型自旋子（fermionic spinons）和玻色型荷子（bosonic chargons）的部分子表示，两者都在π-flux背景（电子净磁通为零）中运动，并与量子涨落的SU(2)晶格规范场耦合。通过测量自旋子-荷子复合体（与电子具有相同量子数）的关联函数，分析其色散关系。

Result: 发现了二阶退禁闭量子相变，在该相变点Néel序和d波超导序均连续消失。在d波超导相内部，自旋子-荷子复合体具有无能隙的狄拉克色散（gapless Dirac dispersion）；在反铁磁相中则变为有能隙色散（gapped dispersion）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在部分子-规范场描述下，Néel态到d波超导态的相变为二阶退禁闭量子相变，这不同于此前基于电子直接计算的结果，暗示规范场涨落在该相变中起关键作用。

Abstract: We present a quantum Monte Carlo study of the transition between the insulating Néel state and the nodal $d$-wave superconductor on the square lattice at half-filling. We access a regime of frustrated magnetic order without a sign problem using a parton representation of the electron in terms of fermionic spinons and bosonic chargons. Both partons move in a background $π$-flux (so the electron experiences no net flux) and are coupled to a quantum fluctuating SU(2) lattice gauge field. In contrast to earlier studies directly on the electronic degrees of freedom, we find evidence for a second-order deconfined quantum phase transition at which both the Néel and $d$-wave superconductivity orders vanish continuously. We compute correlators of the spinon-chargon composite with the same quantum numbers as the electron: we find a gapless Dirac dispersion inside the $d$-wave superconductor, turning into a gapped dispersion in the antiferromagnet.

### [10] [Tensor Network Solvers for Ultra-large Tight-binding Hamiltonians: Algorithms and Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00991)
*Tiago V. C. Antão,Anouar Moustaj,Yitao Sun,Jose L. Lado*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种统一的张量网络（tensor network）方法，通过将 $N=2^L$ 个格点映射为 $L$ 个赝自旋（pseudospin）格点的多体问题，并结合张量网络算法，实现对极致大尺度紧束缚（tight-binding）问题的高效求解。该方法无需显式矩阵存储或对角化，可常规处理数十亿格点系统，并在多种量子材料问题中展示应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在介观乃至宏观尺度理解量子材料（quantum materials）需要针对极大系统进行紧束缚计算，但传统显式矩阵表示在此规模下计算成本过高，成为摩尔（moiré）、超摩尔异质结和准晶（quasicrystals）等体系研究的主要瓶颈。

Method: 将 $N=2^L$ 个格点的紧束缚系统映射为一个 $L$ 个赝自旋格点的多体问题，随后使用张量网络算法求解。对于具有可压缩实空间结构（compressible real-space structure）的哈密顿量，张量网络键维（bond dimension）保持较小（通常数十量级）且与 $N$ 无关。任意跳跃函数（hopping functions）的张量网络表示通过量子张量交叉插值（quantics tensor cross interpolation）构建，所有物理可观测量完全通过张量网络代数计算，无需显式矩阵存储或对角化。

Result: 展示了该方法在谱函数（spectral functions）、动量空间谱（通过张量网络量子傅里叶变换）、实空间拓扑不变量（topological invariants）、实时动力学、自洽平均场下的关联诱导对称性破缺、非厄米现象（non-Hermitian phenomena）以及激子多体物理（excitonic many-body physics）等广泛应用。该方法可常规求解数十亿格点系统。

Conclusion: 该张量网络方法利用实空间结构的可压缩性，建立了一个灵活的计算框架，能够在超大尺度上研究量子物质。该方法已在开源 Julia 包 TensorBinding.jl 中实现。

Abstract: Understanding quantum materials at meso and even macroscopic scales requires tight-binding calculations on system sizes where explicit matrix representations become prohibitively costly. This represents a major bottleneck to rationalize phenomena in moiré and super-moiré heterostructures and quasicrystals. Here, we present a unified tensor-network methodology to solve tight-binding problems at exceptionally large scales, by mapping a system of $N = 2^L$ sites onto a many-body problem of $L$ pseudospin sites, which is subsequently solved with tensor network algorithms. For Hamiltonians with compressible real-space structure, the tensor network bond dimension remains modest, typically of order a few tens, independent of $N$.Tensor network representations of arbitrary hopping functions including long-range, spatially modulated, and twisted-layer couplings are built with quantics tensor cross interpolation, and all physical observables are evaluated entirely with tensor network algebra without explicit matrix storage or diagonalization. We demonstrate applications to spectral functions, momentum-space spectra via the tensor-network quantum Fourier transform, real-space topological invariants, real-time dynamics, correlation induced symmetry breaking with self-consistent mean-field calculations, non-Hermitian phenomena, and excitonic many-body physics. Our methodology enables routinely solving systems with billions of sites, by leveraging the tensor network compressibility of real-space structures, and establishing a flexible framework to study quantum matter at ultra-large length scales. The methodology is implemented in the open-source Julia package TensorBinding.jl.

</details>


### [11] [Exact interlayer triplet-pairing eigenstates in the extended Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01038)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统η-配对对称性在层间相互作用下会被破坏，如何推广三重态配对机制并在强关联系统中构建精确的凝聚配对态是待解决的问题。

Method: 针对多层扩展Hubbard模型（multi-layer extended Hubbard model），提出层间三重态配对算符，借助受限谱生成代数构造精确的凝聚对本征态；采用量子淬火动力学（quench dynamics）进行数值模拟验证。

Conclusion: 该研究为强关联系统中精确凝聚配对态的研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: $η$-pairing symmetry generalizes the pairing mechanisms in superconductivity but is broken in the presence of interlayer interactions. In this work, we extend this approach to triplet pairs. We propose interlayer triplet-pairing operators for the multi-layer extended Hubbard model. We find that a set of exact condensate-pair eigenstates can be constructed, which exhibit off-diagonal long-range order. In contrast to the $η$-pairing mechanism, this originates from restricted spectrum generating algebra and is only available for bilayer and trilayer systems in the presence of interlayer Hubbard interactions. Nevertheless, the system also retains the original on-site $η$-pairing symmetry in the absence of interlayer interactions. Consequently, both singlet and triplet pairs coexist in the eigenstates of the multi-layer Hubbard model. We employ quench dynamics to demonstrate the results through numerical simulations. Our findings open avenues for the study of exact condensate-pair states in strongly correlated systems.

### [12] [Chiral enhancement of two-magnon bound states in an $S=1/2$ triangular-lattice magnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01062)
*László Rudner,Karlo Penc*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在自旋-1/2三角晶格J1-J2-J3海森堡模型中加入均匀标量手性（scalar chirality）相互作用，发现该手性项在单磁子（one-magnon）扇区精确抵消，不改变单磁子色散与不稳定性；但在双磁子（two-magnon）扇区作为相邻翻转自旋之间的定向相互作用存在，通过对称性适配的三角晶格谐函数（triangular-lattice harmonics）推导出Γ点的有限维能隙方程，手性耦合分裂E2型通道中两个相反相对运动手性（relative-motion chirality），选择性地增强其中一个双磁子束缚态通道。精确对角化确认了该机制，并揭示了增强的束缚以及M点和不可约总动量处的额外束缚态。结果表明标量手性是一种高效的微观机制，可在不移动单磁子谱的情况下增强双磁子束缚，并为高场自旋向列（spin-nematic）和多极不稳定性提供路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于自旋-1/2三角晶格J1-J2-J3海森堡模型，加入均匀标量手性相互作用项。在单磁子扇区通过完全平方形式重写色散以识别极小流形；在双磁子扇区引入对称性适配的三角晶格谐波函数，在Γ点对A1和E2型分波通道（partial-wave channels）推导有限维能隙方程（gap equations），并辅以精确对角化（exact diagonalization）验证

Result: 标量手性在单磁子扇区精确抵消，不改变单磁子色散与不稳定性；但在双磁子扇区作为相邻翻转自旋间的定向相互作用，分裂E2型扇区中两个相反相对运动手性，选择性增强其中一个双磁子束缚态通道。精确对角化证实了该机制，并观察到增强的束缚，以及在M点和不可约总动量处出现额外束缚态

Conclusion: 标量手性是一种高效的微观机制，可在不移动单磁子谱的情况下选择性地增强双磁子束缚。该发现为理解高磁场下自旋向列序及多极不稳定性（multipolar instabilities）提供了新的理论路径。

Abstract: We study one- and two-magnon excitations above the fully polarized state of the spin-$1/2$ triangular-lattice $J_1$-$J_2$-$J_3$ Heisenberg model with an additional uniform scalar-chirality interaction. In the one-magnon sector of the Heisenberg model, we identify two special minimum manifolds by rewriting the dispersion in complete-square form. The scalar-chirality term cancels exactly in this sector, leaving the one-magnon dispersion and the single-magnon instability unchanged. In contrast, it survives in the two-magnon sector as an oriented interaction between neighboring flipped spins. Using symmetry-adapted triangular-lattice harmonics, we derive finite-dimensional gap equations at the $Γ$ point in the symmetry-resolved $\mathsf{A_1}$ and $\mathsf{E_2}$-type partial-wave channels. The chirality coupling splits the two opposite relative-motion chiralities in the $\mathsf{E_2}$-type sector, thereby selectively enhancing one two-magnon bound-state channel. Exact diagonalization confirms this mechanism and reveals enhanced binding, as well as additional bound states at $M$ and at incommensurate total momenta. Our results identify scalar chirality as an efficient microscopic mechanism for strengthening two-magnon binding without shifting the one-magnon spectrum, and provide a route toward high-field spin-nematic and multipolar instabilities.

### [14] [Strange Luttinger liquids in a cavity-embedded one-dimensional electronic chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01146)

Motivation: 探索一维电子系统在光-物质耦合（light-matter coupling）与电子-电子相互作用共同作用下的低能物理行为，特别是相图结构和马约拉纳零模的稳定性，以理解量子化腔场对强关联电子体系的调控机制。

Method: 无相互作用情形下，推导低能有效理论并识别为奇异Luttinger液体；有限相互作用时，采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）计算可观测量以表征相边界。

Result: 光-物质耦合定性修改了低能能区，打破了Luttinger液体普适性中的标准速度关系；相图中存在马约拉纳零模相；腔场显著移动了相边界并影响了马约拉纳态的性质。

Conclusion: 奇异Luttinger液体描述在非相互作用情形下成立，但其在引入电子-电子相互作用后的适用性仍需进一步验证。腔场的存在为调控一维电子体系的相图和拓扑态提供了新机制。

Abstract: We study a one-dimensional electronic chain coupled to a homogeneous quantized vacuum field and electron-electron interactions. In the absence of the latter, we derive a low-energy effective description in the presence of light-matter coupling, which we identify as a strange Luttinger liquid. Although it retains a formal resemblance to conventional Luttinger liquid theory, the coupling to the quantum field qualitatively modifies the low-energy sector and breaks the standard velocity relation underlying Luttinger universality. For finite electron-electron interactions, we recover a phase diagram featuring several phases as a function of interaction strength and hopping amplitude, including a phase hosting Majorana-like zero modes. Using exact diagonalization, we compute observables that characterize the phase boundaries and show that the cavity field significantly shifts them. We also study the fate of Majorana-like states under the influence of the cavity field, highlighting their modification by light-matter coupling. Finally, we investigate whether the strange Luttinger liquid description identified in the noninteracting regime continues to hold when electron-electron interactions are introduced.

</details>


<div id='hep-lat'></div>

# hep-lat [[Back]](#toc)

### [15] [Monte Carlo reconstruction of symmetry-twisted partition function ratios: the critical 3D Ising](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00106)
*José Matos*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出一种蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）策略，通过扩展构型空间并采用平直直方图（flat histogram）方法直接估计晶格理论中不同全局扇区之间的配分函数比，并以此计算三维伊辛模型（Ising model）在薄板几何上的对称性扭转热力学卡西米尔差（thermodynamic Casimir difference），无需晶格导数或体相扣除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接估计不同全局扇区（global sectors）之间的配分函数比在晶格理论中具有挑战性，常规方法通常需要复杂的数值导数或体相扣除。本文旨在开发一种无需上述步骤、可直接获取自由能差的数值方法。

Method: 该方法通过扩展构型空间，对端点分别为目标扇区的插值族（interpolating family）进行抽样，并结合平直直方图方法重建对应的自由能差。具体应用在薄板几何 $\mathbb{R}^{2}\times S^{1}_{L_{z}}$ 上的三维伊辛模型，在体相临界点比较未扭转周期扇区与 $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ 扭转反周期扇区。

Result: 通过大体积和长宽比外推，直接得到对称性扭转热力学卡西米尔差 $\Delta_{\mathbb{Z}_{2}}=0.327(2)$，无需晶格导数或体相扣除。该结果提供了对周期扇区热力学卡西米尔观测量中所观测张力的独立扭转扇区探测。此外，方法还给出共形场论（CFT）紧致化数据的直接数值估计，包括有效热屏蔽尺度和 $T^{2}$ 上的 $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ 奇扇区能隙。

Conclusion: 本文提出的蒙特卡洛方法能够直接且选择性地获得共形场论的紧致化数据，并独立验证了扭转扇区与周期扇区之间热力学观测量的内在关联，为晶格理论中的扇区自由能差计算提供了一种通用的数值框架。

Abstract: We introduce a Monte Carlo strategy for directly estimating partition function ratios between distinct global sectors of a lattice theory. It enlarges the configuration space to sample an interpolating family whose endpoints are the desired sectors, and uses flat histogram methods to reconstruct the corresponding free energy difference. Although the construction is more general, we focus here on the three-dimensional Ising model on the slab $\mathbb{R}^{2}\times S^{1}_{L_{z}}$ at the bulk critical point, comparing the untwisted periodic sector with the $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$-twisted antiperiodic sector. A large-volume and aspect ratio extrapolation gives the symmetry-twisted thermodynamic Casimir difference $Δ_{\mathbb{Z}_{2}}=0.327(2)$ directly, without lattice derivatives or bulk subtractions. This provides an independent twisted sector probe of tensions observed in periodic sector thermodynamic Casimir observables. More generally, the method gives direct but selective numerical access to CFT compactification data, including estimates of the effective thermal screening scale and the $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$-odd sector energy gap on $T^{2}$.

</details>

### [16] [A bilayer cellular Potts model of epithelial docking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00400)
*Troy Singletary,Andrea James,Tyler A. Engstrom*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种双层细胞Potts模型（bilayer cellular Potts model），用于模拟动物形态发生中上皮细胞双层融合的“对接（docking）”阶段。模型通过短程面外交联耦合两个标准2D面积-周长弹性模型，预测边缘匹配（edge matching）在单层处于流体态且耦合强度适当时达到最优，并揭示了协调T1转变（coordinated T1 transitions）和“畴壁（domain walls）”等涌现特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 上皮细胞双层融合是动物形态发生（morphogenesis）中的常见步骤，但与单层伤口愈合等上皮融合过程不同，双层融合尚未成为建模研究的重点。实验观察表明，在对接过程中细胞倾向于重塑以跨双层共定位双侧连接（匹配边缘），这为建模提供了生物学动机。

Method: 引入双层细胞Potts模型，通过短程离面（out-of-plane）相互作用耦合两个标准的二维面积-周长弹性模型。该耦合通过单一可调参数最小化地模拟动态细胞骨架突起、钙粘蛋白（cadherins）及其他边缘相关粘附分子的组合效应。模型随后被扩展以粗略考虑双层弯曲。

Result: 模型预测：当两个单层处于流体态（平均细胞形状指数>4.6）且双层耦合强度在面内与离面能量标度间取得平衡时，边缘匹配最大；耦合强度过高时系统易陷入亚稳态；协调T1转变的配对和四重态（quadruplets）对边缘匹配起关键作用；涌现出跨越系统且长寿命的“畴壁”（domain walls）结构；扩展模型可研究对接前沿速度分布。

Conclusion: 该双层Potts模型成功捕捉了上皮双层对接中边缘匹配的核心行为，揭示了耦合强度与单层流体性对匹配效率的影响，以及T1转变和畴壁在动力学中的作用。模型为理解形态发生中的双层融合提供了可扩展的计算框架。

Abstract: Fusion of two epithelial cell sheets brought together in a bilayer configuration is a common step in animal morphogenesis, yet, in contrast to other epithelial fusion processes such as wound healing in a monolayer of cells, it has not been a strong focus of modeling efforts. Here we consider a preliminary stage of bilayer fusion, recently termed "docking." In multiple instances of docking that span apical and basal varieties, cells appear to have a tendency to remodel so as to co-localize their bilateral junctions (match their edges) across the bilayer. Motivated by this observation, we introduce a bilayer cellular Potts model that couples two standard 2D area- and perimeter-elasticity models via short-range, out-of-plane interactions between cell edges. The new coupling involves a single adjustable parameter that minimally models the combined effect of dynamic cytoskeletal protrusions, cadherins, and other potential edge-associated adhesion molecules. Our model predicts that bilayer edge matching is maximized when the two monolayers are in their fluid-like regimes (average cell shape index greater than 4.6 in our implementation), and when the bilayer coupling strength strikes a balance between in-plane and out-of-plane energy scales. At higher coupling strengths, the system tends to get stuck in metastable states with sub-optimal edge matching. Exploration of the mechanisms of edge matching reveals that pairs and quadruplets of coordinated T1 transitions play a particularly important role. We also find numerous examples of emergent features we term "domain walls" - branching or unbranching curves that cross no matched edges, but that separate regions of nearly complete matching. These domain walls can be both system spanning and long lived. Finally, we extend our model to crudely account for bending of the two sheets, and study the distributions of docking front speeds that result.

</details>

### [17] [Yangian Doubles and off-Shell Bethe Vectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00594)
*A. Liashyk,S. Pakuliak,E. Ragoucy*

TL;DR: 本文为经典系列的 Yangian 对偶（Yangian double）构造了通用 $\fg$ 不变可积模型（integrable model）的离壳 Bethe 向量（off-shell Bethe vector），并证明其满足定义性质，这些性质曾被用于证明 $\ggo$ 不变可积模型中的矩形递推关系（rectangular recurrence relation）及验证在壳 Bethe 向量（on-shell Bethe vector）的本征值性质。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过经典系列 Yangian 对偶的流（current）构造离壳 Bethe 向量，并系统验证其满足文献 [LPR-RR] 中用于证明矩形递推关系和本征值性质的关键定义性质。

Result: 成功构造了适用于一般 $\fg$ 不变可积模型的离壳 Bethe 向量，并证明其满足所需的定义性质。

Conclusion: 本文的构造为 $\fg$ 不变可积模型中 Bethe 向量的理论提供了统一框架，并为进一步研究其与本征值性质和递推关系的关联奠定了基础。

Abstract: Off-shell Bethe vectors for a generic $\fg$ invariant integrable model are constructed through the currents of the Yangian doubles of the classical series. These off-shell Bethe vectors are shown to satisfy the defining properties which were used in \cite{LPR-RR} to prove the rectangular recurrence relations and verify the eigenvalue property of the on-shell Bethe vectors in $\ggo$-invariant integrable models.

### [18] [An Analytical Toy Equation of State for Neutron Stars Consistent with Current Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00070)
*Tian-Shun Chen,Xiao-Ding Zhou,Kilar Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过扫描双多方（double polytropic）关系构建了一个紧凑的解析状态方程（equation of state, EOS），该方程能够生成满足当前多信使天文观测约束（如GW170817潮汐形变、NICER质量-半径测量）的相对论性中子星序列，为快速解析与半解析研究提供了基准模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星的快速解析与半解析研究通常需要一个便于计算且能产生相对论性星体序列的状态方程，同时该序列还需符合当前多信使约束。现有单多方基线扫描无法通过全部观测过滤器，因此需要构建更复杂的双多方模型来弥补这一不足。

Method: 采用光滑的双多方关系 $\hatε(\hat p)=a_1\hat p^{Γ_1}+a_2\hat p^{Γ_2}$ 对能量密度作为压力的函数进行参数化扫描。参数选择基于大质量脉冲星、GW170817双中子星事件的潮汐形变（tidal deformability）以及NICER质量-半径测量等过滤条件。随后利用曲线积分评分（curve-integral score）对公开的NICER和GW170817后验数据集进行评估，从可行区域中挑选基准状态方程。

Result: 单多方基线扫描未发现通过所有过滤器的模型，而双多方扫描识别出了可行区域。选中的基准状态方程支持最大质量 $M_{\max}=2.44$--$2.49\,M_\odot$，在1.4倍太阳质量处半径 $R_{1.4}\simeq 11.3$ km，潮汐形变 $Λ_{1.4}=485$--$512$，且在稳定分支上保持因果性（causal）。

Conclusion: 该紧凑的解析状态方程族为当前观测尺度下的相对论性星体结构测试提供了参考基准，尤其适用于需要兼顾计算效率与多信使约束一致性的快速数据分析场景。

Abstract: Fast analytic and semi-analytic studies of neutron stars often require an equation of state that is convenient to evaluate while producing relativistic stellar sequences compatible with current multimessenger constraints. We construct such a benchmark by scanning a smooth double polytropic relation for the energy density as a function of pressure, $\hatε(\hat p)=a_1\hat p^{Γ_1}+a_2\hat p^{Γ_2}$. The parameters are selected with filters based on massive pulsars, tidal deformability from the binary-neutron-star event GW170817, and NICER mass-radius measurements. A single polytropic baseline scan finds no model passing all filters, whereas a double-polytrope scan identifies a viable region. A curve-integral score, evaluated against public NICER and GW170817 posterior data sets, is then used to choose benchmark equations of state within this region. The selected representatives support $M_{\max}=2.44$--$2.49\,M_\odot$, with $R_{1.4}\simeq 11.3$ km and $Λ_{1.4}=485$--$512$, and remain causal on the stable branch. This compact analytic family provides reference cases for relativistic stellar-structure tests at current observational scales.

</details>


### [19] [Smoking-gun evidence for hierarchical black-hole mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01121)
*Yin-Jie Li,Yuan-Zhu Wang,Shao-Peng Tang,Yi-Zhong Fan*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究利用GWTC-5中259个双黑洞并合事件，通过灵活混合族群模型证明高自旋黑洞的子质量函数与低自旋恒星塌缩起源子族的剩余质量分布呈峰对峰对应（Bhattacharyya系数~0.95），为层级并合（hierarchical mergers）提供了确凿证据；同时，低自旋子族的质量上限约束了12C(α,γ)16O核反应的天体物理S因子，表明观测到的黑洞族群可完全由恒星塌缩后经动力学层级组装解释，无需引入原初黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 恒星质量黑洞形成后如何增长是天体物理学的一个核心未解问题。引力波观测已发现具有高质量和高自旋的黑洞子族群，但其起源——究竟来自致密恒星环境中的层级并合（hierarchical mergers）还是孤立黑洞的吸积——此前尚未明确。

Method: 采用灵活的混合族群模型（flexible mixture population model），应用于GWTC-5目录中的259个双黑洞并合样本。通过分析高自旋子族与低自旋恒星塌缩起源子族的质量函数形态对应关系，并计算Bhattacharyya系数量化匹配程度。

Result: 高自旋子族的质量函数与低自旋子族的预言剩余质量分布呈峰对峰对应，Bhattacharyya系数高达~0.95。低自旋子族的质量上限为mmax,1=54.2+7.7-7.2 M⊙，据此推算12C(α,γ)16O反应的天体物理S因子为S300=151+30-26 keV·b，与理论基准值一致。

Conclusion: 高自旋黑洞是早期并合的产物，提供了层级并合的"冒烟枪证据"（smoking-gun evidence）；整个观测到的黑洞族群可由恒星塌缩后经动力学层级组装完整解释，无需诉诸原初黑洞（primordial black holes）的存在。

Abstract: How stellar-mass black holes grow after their birth is a central open question in astrophysics. Gravitational-wave observations have revealed a subpopulation of coalescing black holes with both high masses and high spins, but whether these properties arise from hierarchical mergers in dense stellar environments or from accretion onto isolated black holes has remained unresolved. Here, using a flexible mixture population model applied to the 259 binary black hole mergers in GWTC-5, we show that the mass function of the high-spin subpopulation traces, peak by peak, the predicted remnant-mass distribution of the low-spin, stellar-collapse-origin subpopulation up to $\sim80\,M_\odot$. This morphological match, quantified by a Bhattacharyya coefficient as high as $\sim0.95$, is naturally expected if the high-spin black holes are themselves the products of earlier mergers, whereas any alternative scenario would require fine-tuning, thereby providing smoking-gun evidence for hierarchical mergers. In addition, the sharp upper-mass cutoff of the low-spin subpopulation at $m_{\rm max,1}=54.2^{+7.7}_{-7.2}\,M_\odot$ yields an astrophysical $S$-factor of $S_{300}=151^{+30}_{-26}$~keV~b (68\% credible interval) for the $^{12}{\rm C}(α,γ)^{16}{\rm O}$ reaction, in agreement with the benchmark theoretical value. These results establish that the entire observed black-hole population can be accounted for by stellar collapse followed by dynamical hierarchical assembly, without invoking primordial black holes.

</details>

### [20] [Evanescent absorption spectroscopy of transition metal dichalcogenide materials using guided photoluminescence in Si$_3$N$_4$ photonic waveguides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00615)
*Victor Gonzalez-Morote,Marianna Sledzinska,Arkadiusz P. Gertych,Syed Hassan Abbas Jaffery,Mariusz Zdrojek,Daniel Navarro-Urrios*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于芯片集成的无源倏逝波吸收光谱技术，利用Si₃N₄波导自身的缺陷相关光致发光作为内源探针，实现了MoS₂和WS₂等二维过渡金属硫属化物（TMD）在集成光子环境中的光学吸收测量，无需外部照明即可表征2D材料的光学性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维过渡金属硫属化物（TMD）与光子波导的片上集成是实现紧凑型光电子和传感器件的关键，然而这类器件的性能高度依赖于2D材料在集成环境中的光学吸收特性。现有方法需要外部光源，无法在真实集成条件下直接表征吸收，因此亟需一种片上无源的原位吸收光谱方法。

Method: 利用Si₃N₄波导核心自身的宽带缺陷相关光致发光作为内部探针，光在波导内传播经过TMD薄片下方，通过倏逝波（evanescent wave）与2D材料发生光谱衰减。将TMD覆盖波导的透射光谱与无TMD的参考波导归一化，即可提取能量依赖的吸收响应。同时设计了顶部泵浦方案以收集波导传播的WS₂光致发光信号。

Result: 提取的导波吸收结果与拉曼光谱（Raman）和局部微光致发光（micro-photoluminescence）表征结果一致，并能区分空间均匀与非均匀TMD薄片之间的吸收差异。顶部泵浦方案恢复的WS₂光致发光在传播过程中的光谱重塑可由测得的吸收响应进行定量复现。

Conclusion: 该无源片上平台可在集成光子环境中直接表征2D材料的光学特性，为基于波导集成的TMD光电探测器和传感器提供了一条直接的技术路径。

Abstract: On-chip integration of two-dimensional transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) with photonic waveguides underpins a growing class of compact optoelectronic and sensing devices, whose performance depends on the optical absorption of the 2D material in this integrated environment. We demonstrate source-free, on-chip evanescent absorption spectroscopy of MoS$_2$ and WS$_2$ flakes integrated on Si$_3$N$_4$ waveguides, in which the broadband defect-related photoluminescence of the Si$_3$N$_4$ core itself acts as the internal probe. Light generated inside the core propagates under the TMD flake and is spectrally attenuated by evanescent interaction with the 2D material, and normalizing the transmitted spectrum to a reference waveguide without TMD yields the energy-dependent absorption response without any external illumination. The extracted guided absorption agrees with Raman and local micro-photoluminescence characterization and resolves differences between spatially uniform and non-uniform flakes. A complementary top-pumping scheme recovers guided WS$_2$ photoluminescence, whose spectral reshaping during propagation is quantitatively reproduced by the measured absorption. This source-free platform qualifies 2D materials in their integrated photonic environment and provides a direct route toward waveguide-integrated TMD photodetectors and sensors.

</details>


### [21] [Self-selected phase-matched second harmonic generation in nonlinear optical materials: from phenomenon to applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00657)
*Niklas Dömer,Tobias Hehemann,Felix Sauerwein,Sebastian Inckemann,Steffen Ganschow,Mirco Imlau*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自选择相位匹配二次谐波产生（self-selected phase-matched second harmonic generation）方法，将其作为一种全光学探针，用于测量双折射非线性光学材料中的折射率色散（refractive-index dispersion）。该方法无需波长或角度调谐，利用宽光谱超短脉冲使材料自动选择满足I类非临界相位匹配条件的基频分量，从而通过二次谐波光谱中的窄峰位置灵敏地反映材料参数。研究在铌酸锂（lithium niobate）和铌酸锂-钽酸锂固溶体（lithium niobate-tantalate solid solutions）中验证了该方法对化学计量比、温度梯度和成分不均匀性的检测能力，表明该技术可用于非线性光学材料的快速非接触式检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统二次谐波相位匹配方法需要波长调谐或角度调谐，操作复杂且效率较低；而针对非线性光学材料（如铌酸锂）的化学计量比、温度梯度和成分均匀性等关键参数，目前尚缺乏快速、非接触式的光学检测手段。

Method: 利用宽光谱、强超短脉冲照射双折射非线性光学材料，使其自动选择满足I类非临界相位匹配条件（type-I noncritical phase-matching condition）的基频光谱分量，从而在二次谐波光谱中产生一个窄峰。该峰的位置由折射率决定，因而对影响光学色散（optical dispersion）的材料参数高度敏感。

Result: 成功将该方法应用于铌酸锂中化学计量比（stoichiometry）和温度梯度（temperature gradients）的光学检测，以及新生长铌酸锂-钽酸锂固溶体中成分不均匀性（composition inhomogeneities）的检测。

Conclusion: 自选择相位匹配二次谐波产生方法可作为一种快速、非接触式的非线性光学材料检测手段，适用于块状晶体（bulk crystals）、晶圆（wafers）和薄膜平台（thin-film platforms）。

Abstract: Self-selected phase-matched second harmonic generation is introduced as an all-optical probe of refractive-index dispersion in birefringent nonlinear optical materials. Rather than requiring wavelength or angular tuning, the exposure with a spectrally broad, intense ultrashort pulse allows the material to self-select the fundamental spectral component that satisfies the type-I noncritical phase-matching condition. This produces a narrow peak in the second harmonic spectrum whose position is governed by the refractive indices and is therefore highly sensitive to material parameters that affect the optical dispersion. We demonstrate the application of this phenomenon for the optical inspection of stoichiometry and temperature gradients in technologically relevant lithium niobate, as well as composition inhomogeneities in newly grown lithium niobate-tantalate solid solutions. These results establish self-selected phase-matched second harmonic generation as a rapid, non-contact method for inspecting nonlinear optical materials, with potential relevance for bulk crystals, wafers, and thin-film platforms.

</details>


### [22] [Near-Field Characterisation of Guided Modes in WS2 Nanobeams and Quasi-Bulk Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00694)
*Zara S. Taylor,Luke M. Hallacy,Xuerong Hu,Oliver T. Williams,Simone Strohmair,Fabian Felixberger,Alexander J. Knight,Timothy Chester-Parsons,Luke R. Wilson,Alexander I. Tartakovskii*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本研究通过超光谱腔增强成像（hyperspectral cavity-enhanced imaging）确定了WS₂在可见光-近红外（visible-NIR）边界区域消光系数（extinction coefficient）的高分辨率上下界，并利用散射型扫描近场光学显微镜（s-SNOM）在800–1400 nm范围内探测了WS₂波导中的TE₀、TM₀及高阶模式，识别了波矢色散（wavevector dispersion）和损耗的模式特异性趋势，同时发现近场测量中结构尺寸接近激发波长时会产生显著伪影。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: WS₂具有高面内折射率（in-plane refractive index）、低亚带隙吸收（sub-bandgap absorption）和强光学各向异性（optical anisotropy），是极具前景的纳米光子学（nanophotonics）集成平台。然而，目前对WS₂波导随波长变化的模式限制（modal confinement）和衰减（attenuation）的实验研究仍十分有限，且其消光系数报告值跨数量级差异，导致模态衰变长度（modal decay length）预测存在巨大不确定性，阻碍了晶圆级集成可行性的评估。

Method: 采用超光谱腔增强成像技术测定WS₂在可见光-近红外边界区域消光系数的高分辨率上下界；进一步运用散射型扫描近场光学显微镜（s-SNOM）在800–1400 nm光谱范围内探测准体（quasi-bulk）和纳米束（nanobeam）WS₂波导中的TE₀、TM₀及高阶模式，分析波矢色散和损耗的模式特异性趋势。

Result: 绝对损耗值依赖于测量几何结构，但s-SNOM能可靠捕获相对模态趋势，并给出传播损耗（propagation loss）的上界。在纳米束测量中，当结构尺寸接近激发波长时，横向干涉（transverse interference）和空间采样效应（spatial sampling effects）会产生显著伪影，使提取的有效折射率（effective index）偏移高达0.25。

Conclusion: 本工作同时评估了s-SNOM作为波导性能探针的能力，表明其可作为各向异性波导（anisotropic waveguides）的诊断工具。同时揭示了纳米尺度波导近场测量中需警惕的结构尺寸相关的伪影问题。

Abstract: The exceptionally high in-plane refractive index, low sub-bandgap absorption, and strong optical anisotropy of WS2 make it a promising material platform for next-generation integrated circuits for nanophotonics. Its layered van der Waals structure further enables heterogeneous integration with silicon photonics and emerging two-dimensional optoelectronic materials. However, despite increasing interest in the waveguiding properties of WS2, experimental studies of wavelength-dependent modal confinement and attenuation remain limited. Additionally, though the extinction coefficient of WS2 is expected to be near-negligible beneath the bandgap, reported values span orders of magnitude, leading to large uncertainty in predicted modal decay lengths and wafer-scale integration feasibility. To resolve these ambiguities we perform hyperspectral cavity-enhanced imaging, determining high-resolution upper and lower bounds on the extinction coefficient of WS2 within the visible-NIR edge. We further employ scattering-type scanning near-field optical microscopy (s-SNOM) to probe TE0, TM0, and higher-order modes in both quasi-bulk and nanobeam WS2 waveguides across the 800-1400 nm spectral range, enabling identification of mode-specific trends in wavevector dispersion and loss. This work simultaneously assesses s-SNOM as a probe of waveguide performance, and we find that while absolute loss values depend on measurement geometry, s-SNOM reliably captures relative modal trends and provides upper bounds on propagation loss, supporting its use as a diagnostic tool for anisotropic waveguides. We further identify significant artefacts in nanobeam measurements arising from transverse interference and spatial sampling effects when the structure size approaches the excitation wavelength, which can shift extracted effective indices by up to 0.25.

### [23] [Lanczos Method for QRPA Strength Functions in Atomic Nuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01114)
*Dong Min Roh,Chao Yang,Jonathan Engel,Matthew L. Dai*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种对称Lanczos方法，用于计算原子核中电荷改变QRPA（charge-changing QRPA）强度函数。该方法基于有限振幅法（finite-amplitude method, FAM）的QRPA线性响应公式，导出等效谱表示及简化本征值问题，通过一次Krylov迭代即可在宽能量区间内近似计算洛伦兹展宽的强度函数，避免了传统逐频点响应计算。数值测试表明，对称Lanczos投影在扩展频率范围内比GMRES参考结果更具计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统电荷改变QRPA强度函数计算需要逐频点求解线性响应问题（frequency-by-frequency response calculations），计算成本高昂。本文旨在开发一种矩阵自由的Lanczos算法，通过单次Krylov迭代在宽频率区间内高效获得强度函数，降低整体计算开销。

Method: 从有限振幅法（FAM）的QRPA线性响应问题出发，推导出等价谱表示，并在实情况下导出涉及矩阵乘积$MK$和$KM$的简化本征值问题（reduced eigenvalue problem），其中$M \equiv A+B$、$K \equiv A-B$。利用该公式构造矩阵自由的对称Lanczos近似（matrix-free symmetric Lanczos approximation），通过单次Krylov迭代计算洛伦兹展宽的强度函数。

Result: 对$^{112}$Sn和$^{150}$Nd的数值测试显示：(1) GMRES迭代法能够复现收敛的迭代FAM强度曲线，且所需迭代次数更少；(2) 以GMRES作为逐频点参考，Lanczos近似能以更低的整体计算成本复现相同的强度曲线。

Conclusion: 对称Lanczos投影法为QRPA强度函数计算提供了一种高效且准确的手段，尤其适用于需要在扩展频率范围（extended frequency range）内获取谱信息的场景。

Abstract: We present a symmetric Lanczos method for computing charge-changing QRPA strength functions in atomic nuclei. Starting from the finite-amplitude-method formulation of the QRPA linear-response problem, we derive equivalent spectral representations and, in the real case, a reduced eigenvalue problem involving the matrix products $MK$ and $KM$, where $M\equiv A+B$ and $K\equiv A-B$ are formed from the usual QRPA matrices $A$ and $B$. The resulting formulation enables a matrix-free Lanczos approximation of the Lorentzian-smeared strength function over a broad energy interval from a single Krylov run, in contrast to conventional frequency-by-frequency response calculations. Numerical tests for $^{112}$Sn and $^{150}$Nd first show that GMRES reproduces the converged iterative FAM strength profiles while requiring fewer iterations. Using GMRES as the frequency-by-frequency reference, we then show that the Lanczos approximation reproduces the same strength profiles with reduced overall cost. These results indicate that symmetric Lanczos projection provides an efficient and accurate approach for QRPA strength-function calculations when spectral information is required over an extended frequency range.

</details>

### [24] [Spin Femtoscopy: A Framework for Revealing Genuine Spin Correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00413)
*Kehao Zhang,Xuan Wang,Xiaofeng Luo*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文提出自旋费米显微镜（spin femtoscopy）框架，利用自旋分辨的费米显微测量提取强相互作用物质中真实的两粒子自旋关联（two-particle spin correlations），以ΛΛ对为原理验证，通过弱衰变构建自旋敏感费米显微关联函数，并分离量子统计与末态相互作用引起的自旋混合效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重离子碰撞实验中的自旋测量（如超子极化与矢量介子自旋排列）仅揭示了单粒子自旋现象，而产生的强子系统中真实的两粒子自旋关联仍基本未被实验探测。

Method: 提出自旋费米显微镜框架，利用Λ超子的自分析弱衰变构建不同单态（singlet）与三重态（triplet）混合比例的自旋敏感费米显微关联函数，提取自旋态布居数，并区分量子统计与自旋依赖末态相互作用带来的费米显微混合效应。

Result: 证明所提可观测量能够实验获取两粒子自旋态布居数，并实现真实自旋关联与由量子统计及末态相互作用引起的自旋依赖费米显微混合的分离。

Conclusion: 该工作将费米显微镜从源几何与末态相互作用的探针扩展为一个揭示强相互作用物质量子自旋结构的框架。

Abstract: Spin correlations are among the most fundamental quantum observables in many-body systems, yet they remain difficult to access experimentally in relativistic heavy-ion collisions. Existing spin measurements, including hyperon polarization and vector-meson spin alignment, have revealed important single-particle spin phenomena, but genuine two-particle spin correlations in the produced hadronic system remain largely unexplored. Here we propose spin femtoscopy, a framework for accessing genuine two-particle spin correlations through spin-resolved femtoscopic measurements. The key principle is that different two-particle spin configurations can give rise to different femtoscopic correlation functions because of quantum statistics, spin-dependent final-state interactions. Using $ΛΛ$ pairs as a proof of principle, we exploit the self-analyzing weak decay of $Λ$ hyperons to construct spin-sensitive femtoscopic correlation functions with different singlet and triplet admixtures. We show that these observables provide experimental access to the spin-state populations of the pair and allow genuine spin correlations to be separated from spin-dependent femtoscopic mixing caused by quantum statistics and final-state interactions. This work extends femtoscopy from a probe of source geometry and final-state interactions to a framework for revealing the quantum spin structure of strongly interacting matter.

### [25] [Valley-dependent electron optics using quantum dots in bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00271)
*Fereshte Ildarabadi,Stephen R. Power*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出在Bernal堆叠双层石墨烯（BLG）中利用静电定义的量子点（QDs）与层反对称门控（layer-antisymmetric gating）构建可调控的谷电子光学平台。通过连续模型与广义多重散射形式，系统分析了单点与多点结构对高斯电子束的谷依赖散射，实现谷分离与谷滤波功能，并指出该方案在实验上可行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双层石墨烯中实现无需磁场、应变或自旋-轨道耦合的强谷依赖散射机制，并基于此设计可调控的谷电子光学平台。

Method: 采用四能带连续模型（four-band continuum model）和广义多重散射形式（generalized multiple-scattering formalism），分析高斯电子束（Gaussian electron beams）在单点与多点结构中的散射，计算谷分辨电流（valley-resolved currents）与角分布（angular profiles）。

Result: 单个量子点产生显著的谷依赖偏转；相同极性量子点阵列作为谷分离器（valley splitter），相反门控量子点对作为谷滤波器（valley filter）。组合结构可实现可调的高谷极化电流生成、导向与滤波，并有效抑制前向透射。

Conclusion: 所需的能量尺度、门控不对称性与器件尺寸均在双门控双层石墨烯的实验可及范围内，表明量子点阵列可作为可控谷分辨电子光学的现实平台。

Abstract: Electrostatically defined quantum dots (QDs) with layer-antisymmetric gating in Bernal-stacked bilayer graphene (BLG) open a local gap and generate a mass-like term with opposite sign in the two valleys, producing strongly valley-dependent scattering without magnetic fields, strain, or spin-orbit coupling. Building on this mechanism, we propose a tunable platform based on such QDs for valley-dependent electron optics in BLG. Using a four-band continuum model and a generalized multiple-scattering formalism, we analyze scattering of Gaussian electron beams from single- and multi-dot architectures and compute valley-resolved currents and angular profiles. A single dot produces distinct valley-dependent deflection, while multi-dot configurations enable enhanced control: identical-dot arrays act as valley splitters, whereas oppositely gated pairs function as valley filters. Combining these elements yields tunable generation, steering, and filtering of highly valley-polarized currents with strong suppression of forward transmission. The required energy scales, gate asymmetries, and device dimensions are within experimentally accessible regimes for dual-gated BLG, establishing quantum-dot arrays as a realistic platform for controllable valley-resolved electron optics.

### [26] [Madelung hydrodynamics and Poisson geometry of wave functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01024)
*Boris Khesin,Klas Modin*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子力学与流体力学之间Madelung变换的泊松几何（Poisson geometry），证明该变换可作为动量映射（momentum map），为微分同胚群半直扩张的余伴随轨道（coadjoint orbits）定义预量子丛（prequantum bundles），并揭示了无限维Fubini–Study与Fisher–Rao几何之间的Kähler映射、带Morse–Bott密度的辛同构（symplectomorphism）以及Wallstrom量子化条件的新动量映射观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓展Madelung变换的几何框架至一般波函数（包含零点与不连通流形），并回应Atiyah关于哈密顿环面作用凸性结果在无限维情形的提问。

Method: 利用泊松几何与动量映射理论，在任意定向流形上分析Madelung变换的几何性质，并分类处理无零点波函数与带非临界零点波函数两种情况。

Result: (1) Madelung变换作为动量映射自然定义出预量子丛；(2) 对于无零点波函数，建立无限维Fubini–Study与Fisher–Rao几何间的Kähler映射，推广至非单连通流形；(3) 对于非临界零点波函数，证明Madelung变换是到带Morse–Bott密度的余伴随轨道的辛同构，并提供Wallstrom量子化条件的动量映射解释。

Conclusion: Madelung框架给出了无限维版本哈密顿环面作用凸性结果的部分回答，并建立了Madelung变换与Marsden–Weinstein辛结构在纽结与膜上的联系。

Abstract: We describe the Poisson geometry of the Madelung transform between quantum mechanics and hydrodynamics for generic wave functions. We prove that for arbitrary oriented manifolds this transform, being regarded as a momentum map, naturally defines prequantum bundles for coadjoint orbits of semidirect extensions of diffeomorphism groups. Furthermore, we show that the Madelung framework provides a natural infinite-dimensional version of the convexity results for Hamiltonian torus actions, thus giving a partial answer to Atiyah's question.
  In particular, for wave functions without zeros our results provide a Kähler map between the infinite-dimensional Fubini--Study and Fisher--Rao geometries, thus extending previous results to non-simply-connected manifolds. Furthermore, for wave functions with noncritical zeros, the Madelung transform is shown to be a symplectomorphism to the coadjoint orbits with Morse--Bott densities. The latter, in turn, furnishes a novel momentum map point of view on the Wallstrom quantization condition for the hydrodynamical form of quantum mechanics. We also comment on the relation between the Madelung setting and the Marsden--Weinstein symplectic structures on knots and membranes.

### [27] [Surface Platinum Alloying for Passivation of Oxide Interfaces on Superconducting Niobium Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00429)
*Ananya Chattaraj,Conan Weiland,Bruce Ravel,Kim Kisslinger,Sooyeon Hwang,Xiao Tong,Ajith Pattammattel,Andrew M. Kiss,Steven L. Hulbert,Aswin kumar Anbalagan,Andrew L. Walter,Peter V. Sushko,Mingzhao Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种可扩展的 fabrication 策略，通过在铌（Niobium, Nb）表面沉积薄层铂（Pt）并经热退火形成 Nb-Pt 合金，有效抑制表面和侧壁区域的进一步氧化，从而降低双能级系统（two-level systems, TLS）引起的介电损耗，提升超导 transmon 量子比特的相干性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导 transmon 量子比特的相干性受限于表面和界面上双能级系统（TLS）引起的介电损耗。铌（Nb）在环境条件下易形成原生氧化物，引入有损介电界面，降低器件性能，因此亟需一种化学稳定且可扩展的表面钝化方案。

Method: 在高纯度铌薄膜上沉积薄层铂（Pt），随后进行热退火处理，使 Pt 与表面氧化铌反应形成 Nb-Pt 合金层；结合光谱学和显微学分析表征合金层的化学稳定性及其抑制氧化生长的能力，并利用第一性原理（ab initio）模拟揭示原子尺度的结构重排与电子结构演化。

Result: 制备的高纯度 Nb 薄膜具有体超导转变温度（$T_c = 9.30\pm0.10$ K）；Pt 封装层经热退火后形成化学稳定的 Nb-Pt 金属合金层，能够有效抑制进一步氧化；模拟结果阐明了 Pt 掺入原生氧化铌后的原子尺度机制。

Conclusion: 该策略提供了一条材料工程路径，可制备化学鲁棒的 Nb 界面（包括侧壁），有望用于构建更高相干性的超导量子比特架构。

Abstract: Dielectric loss arising from two-level systems (TLS) at surfaces and interfaces remains a primary limitation to coherence in superconducting transmon qubits. Niobium (Nb), a widely used material in superconducting quantum circuits, readily forms native oxides under ambient conditions, leading to lossy dielectric interfaces that degrade device performance. Here, a robust and scalable fabrication strategy is demonstrated for chemically stabilizing Nb surfaces and mitigating further oxidation, including protection of both surface and sidewall regions. High-purity Nb films were fabricated with bulk-like superconducting transition temperatures ($T_c = 9.30\pm0.10$) K. We demonstrate that a thin Pt encapsulation layer, deposited after native oxide formation, can be transformed via thermal annealing into a Nb-Pt alloy at the surface. Spectroscopic and microscopic analyses confirm the formation of a chemically stable metallic alloy layer and its ability to suppress further oxide growth. Ab initio simulations elucidate the atomic-scale rearrangement and electronic structure evolution associated with Pt incorporation on native niobium oxide, providing insight into the stabilization mechanism of the alloyed surface. This approach offers a materials pathway for engineering chemically robust Nb interfaces, including sidewalls, toward higher-coherence superconducting qubit architectures."

### [28] [Quench of chiral superconductivity by quantum phase fluctuations in twisted cuprate bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00630)
*Yin Shi,Mengxian Zhao,Fei Yang,Miao Liu,Sheng Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文论证量子相位涨落（quantum phase fluctuations）从根本上重塑了扭曲铜氧双层中手性 $d+id'$ 超导态的相图，将手性相限制在极窄的扭转角窗口和极低温度范围内，并揭示了手性破缺导致的一级相变、共存亚稳性以及时间反演对称性破缺（TRSB）量子临界点处的约瑟夫森相位锁定弱化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对扭曲铜氧双层（twisted cuprate bilayers）中手性 $d+id'$ 超导态的理论预言与时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal symmetry breaking, TRSB）实验信号之间的争议，作者试图探究量子相位涨落对该手性态的相图所产生的影响。

Method: 通过引入量子相位涨落（quantum phase fluctuations）分析，考察其对层间相位自由度长程相干性的破坏作用，并据此重新构建手性 $d+id'$ 态的相图。

Result: 量子相位涨落几乎消除了相图大部分区域的手性相，仅将其限制在极窄的扭转角窗口和超低温度范围内；手性破坏通过一级相变（first-order transition）进入 $d$-波态，产生共存与亚稳性（metastability）；在超导区域内部，TRSB 量子临界点（quantum critical point）处的约瑟夫森相位锁定（Josephson phase locking）被显著削弱。

Conclusion: 量子相位涨落是低维层状量子材料中时间反演对称性破缺相涌现的一个基本约束因素，为理解相关实验争议提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Following theoretical proposals of chiral $d+id'$ superconductivity in twisted cuprate bilayers, experimental signatures of time-reversal symmetry breaking (TRSB) remain highly controversial. Here we demonstrate that quantum phase fluctuations fundamentally reshape the phase diagram of this proposed chiral state. Unlike regular superconducting orders, the chiral $d+id'$ state requires long-range coherence of an interlayer phase degree of freedom and is therefore intrinsically vulnerable to phase fluctuations. Incorporating these fluctuations nearly eliminates the chiral phase over most parts of the phase diagram, restricting it to a narrow twist-angle window and ultra-low temperatures. The fluctuation-driven destruction of chirality produces a first-order transition into the $d$-wave state, giving rise to coexistence and metastability. Meanwhile, Josephson phase locking is strongly weakened at the TRSB quantum critical point, which sits well within the superconducting regime. More broadly, our work establishes quantum phase fluctuations as a fundamental constraint on the emergence of TRSB phases in low-dimensional layered quantum materials.

</details>


### [29] [Collective phase modes in twisted $d$-wave superconducting bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00662)
*Yin Shi,Mengxian Zhao,Fei Yang,Miao Liu,Sheng Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文理论分析了扭转双层铜氧化物超导体中低能相位涨落的动力学，发现高阶约瑟夫森耦合会显著改变相位行为：相对相位刚度在正常态即为有限值，且相对相位涨落获得有限激发能隙，该能隙在趋近手性量子临界点时被强烈抑制，揭示了超导态内约瑟夫森相位锁定的失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭转双层铜氧化物被预言可通过高阶约瑟夫森耦合（higher-order Josephson coupling）实现高温手性 $d+id'$ 超导。在二维超导系统中，超导序参量相位的长波涨落构成无能隙（gapless）集体模，即使在零温下也不可忽略。因此，有必要系统分析低能相位涨落对这类系统的影响。

Method: 作者对扭转 $d$ 波超导双层体系中的低能相位涨落进行理论分析，系统保留所有阶次的约瑟夫森耦合（Josephson coupling）效应。

Result: 高阶约瑟夫森耦合导致相位动力学的非平庸修正：两层之间的相对相位刚度（relative-phase stiffness）在正常态即为有限值，这是层内 U(1) 对称性被层间隧穿显式破缺的直接结果。相位涨落会抑制相对相位刚度但增强 $d+id'$ 相中的整体相位刚度。相对相位涨落获得一个小而有限的激发能隙，该能隙不再等于约瑟夫森等离子体频率（Josephson plasma frequency），并在趋近手性量子临界点（chiral quantum critical point）时被强烈抑制，表明超导态内约瑟夫森相位锁定的失效。

Conclusion: 研究表明，高阶约瑟夫森耦合在扭转 $d$ 波超导双层中主导了低能相位动力学，其引发的相位刚度变化和有限能隙行为对于理解该体系中的手性超导态及其量子临界现象具有关键意义。

Abstract: Twisted cuprate bilayers have been predicted to host high-temperature chiral $d+id'$ superconductivity, originating from higher-order Josephson coupling processes. In such two-dimensional superconducting systems, long-wavelength fluctuations in the phase of the superconducting order parameter constitute gapless collective modes and therefore remain significant even at zero temperature. Here, we perform a theoretical analysis of the low-energy phase fluctuations in twisted $d$-wave superconducting bilayers, systematically retaining Josephson coupling to all orders. We demonstrate that higher-order Josephson coupling processes lead to nontrivial modifications of the phase dynamics. In particular, the stiffness of the relative phase between the two layers is finite even in the normal state, which is a direct consequence of the intralayer U(1) symmetry breaking explicitly induced by interlayer tunneling. Phase fluctuations suppress the relative-phase stiffness but enhance the overall-phase stiffness in the $d+id'$ phase. Furthermore, the relative-phase fluctuations acquire a small but finite excitation gap, which is no longer equal to the Josephson plasma frequency and is strongly suppressed upon approaching the chiral quantum critical point, indicating the breakdown of Josephson phase locking within the superconducting state.

### [30] [Resilient $j$=3/2 superconductivity in topological semimetal YPtBi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00765)
*Prathum Saraf,Nicholas A. Crombie,Rahul Sharma,Jared Z. Dans,Danila Sokratov,Carsyn L. Mueller,Ram Kumar,Hyunsoo Kim,Connor Roncaioli,Winslow Weiss,David Graf,Chandra Shekhar,Claudia Felser,Johnpierre Paglione*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过系统调控无序程度（nearly two orders of magnitude）和载流子密度（nearly three orders of magnitude），实验测量并比较YPtBi超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature）随这些参数的变化。

Result: 超导临界温度在两到三个数量级的无序与载流子密度变化范围内几乎保持不变，表现出显著的鲁棒性（remarkable robustness）。

Conclusion: YPtBi的超导转变可能由相位刚度（phase stiffness）而非配对形成（pair formation）主导；库珀配对（Cooper pairing）对剧烈的准粒子环境变化不敏感，这揭示了拓扑高自旋超导体中一种新的保护形式。

Abstract: Cooper pairing in most of the known fermionic superfluids occurs via spin-1/2 quasiparticle interactions that lead to spin-singlet or spin-triplet pairing. In the topological semimetal YPtBi, strong spin-orbit coupling results in a band inversion between highly symmetric $s$- and $p$-like electronic bands and a degeneracy at the $Γ$ point that ensures the manifold of $j$=3/2 quasiparticle states thrive near the Fermi level, where superconducting pairing occurs. Here we study the effects of magnetic and nonmagnetic disorder and carrier density on this exotic superconducting pairing state. By varying levels of disorder and carrier densities by nearly two and three orders of magnitude, respectively, we show that the superconducting critical temperature of YPtBi has a remarkable robustness, with little variation across this span. Our results suggest that superconductivity in YPtBi may reside in a regime where phase stiffness, rather than pair formation, governs the transition temperature. The insensitivity of Cooper pairing to dramatic changes in quasiparticle environment in a $j$=3/2 superconductor highlights a new form of protection realized in topological high-spin superconductors.

### [31] [Characterization of Hydroxyls in Surface Oxide of Superconducting Tantalum and Their Mitigation in Quantum Circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00903)
*Ekta Bhatia,Nicholas Pieniazek,Aleksandra Biedron,Sandra Schujman,Hunter Frost,Zhihao Xiao,Jakub Nalaskowski,Kevin Musick,Thomas Murray,Satyavolu Papa Rao*

TL;DR: 本研究首次通过二次离子质谱（SIMS）等方法证明，α相钽（alpha-Ta）薄膜表面的亚氧化物区域中羟基（hydroxyls）的积累是导致超导量子电路中两能级系统（TLS）缺陷及退相干（decoherence）的关键分子起源。通过化学机械平坦化（CMP）形成的氧化物替代原生氧化物，以及等离子体氮化处理，均可有效抑制羟基掺入，为制造更高相干性的超导量子电路提供了路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钽（Ta）在超导量子电路中因替代铌（Nb）作电容极板时可实现更长相干时间而受到关注。此前研究已确认表面氧化物中的两能级系统（TLS）缺陷是微波损耗和退相干的主要来源，但钽氧化物的性质尚不明确。因此，本文旨在系统表征钽表面氧化物的化学结构，并寻找TLS缺陷的分子起源及其调控方法。

Method: 采用300毫米晶圆级α相钽薄膜，使用二次离子质谱（secondary ion mass spectrometry, SIMS）检测羟基分布；利用角分辨X射线光电子能谱（angle-resolved X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy, ARXPS）分析表面化学态；通过透射电子显微镜（transmission electron microscopy, TEM）确认氧化物厚度。并通过化学机械平坦化（chemical mechanical planarization, CMP）及等离子体氮化处理调控表面羟基含量。

Result: 首次发现羟基在钽的亚氧化物（suboxide）区域积累。表面区域以Ta2O5为主，Ta2O5与底层钽之间存在亚化学计量比的TaOx层。通过CMP形成的氧化物可抑制羟基掺入；等离子体氮化处理也可降低α相钽表面的羟基负载。

Conclusion: 研究结果支持TLS缺陷在氧化物厚度内非均匀分布的观点，并提出羟基是这些损耗通道可能的分子起源。通过表面工程调控羟基含量，有望从根源上降低TLS缺陷，从而制造更鲁棒、更高相干性的超导量子电路。

Abstract: Recently, tantalum (Ta) has gained attention in superconducting quantum circuits due to the longer coherence times achieved when replacing niobium (Nb) in capacitor pads. Previous literature shows that surface oxides that form upon ambient exposure on superconducting metals such as Ta, Al, and Nb host two-level system (TLS) defects, which are a leading source of microwave loss and decoherence. While the surface oxides of Nb and Al have been extensively studied, Ta oxides remain less well understood. Using secondary ion mass spectrometry of alpha-Ta films deposited at 300 mm wafer scale, we show for the first time that hydroxyls accumulate in the Ta suboxide region above the underlying Ta. Angle-resolved X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy shows that the surface region is dominated by Ta2O5, with sub-stoichiometric TaOx present in between the Ta2O5 and underlying Ta. The thickness of the tantalum oxide is confirmed by transmission electron microscopy. We demonstrate that [OH] incorporation can be suppressed by replacing the native oxide with an oxide formed during chemical mechanical planarization of alpha-Ta films. Our findings support the hypothesis that TLS defects are non-uniform within the oxide thickness and suggest hydroxyls as a probable molecular origin of these loss channels. Furthermore, we show the feasibility of plasma nitridization as a method to decrease hydroxyl loading on alpha-Ta surfaces. The modulation of hydroxyl content through surface engineering of alpha-Ta can enable the fabrication of more robust, high-coherence superconducting quantum circuits by addressing a potential TLS source.

### [32] [Imaging superconducting weak spots through vortex-assisted THz near-field photovoltage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00914)
*Sergio J. Salvía-Fernández,Ekaterina Khestanova,Zoe Velluire-Pellat,Leonardo R. Cadorim,Sergi Batlle-Porro,David A. Czaplewski,Johann Osmond,Sebastian Castilla,Adrian Bachtold,Milorad V. Milošević,Aharon Kapitulnik,Frank H. L. Koppens*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文首次将太赫兹近场光电压纳米成像技术应用于超导体，实现了2.52 THz下300 nm的空间分辨率，揭示了NbN薄膜中由超流密度降低的纳米级缺陷产生的光电压峰，并归因于涡旋-反涡旋对在缺陷处的 nucleation 增强，为探测超导体中材料不均匀性对光-物质相互作用的影响提供了直接途径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文演示了太赫兹近场光电压纳米成像（THz near-field photovoltage nanoscopy）在超导体中的首次应用，对载流偏置的NbN薄膜条带进行扫描成像，在2.52 THz频率下实现了300 nm的空间分辨率。

Result: 在NbN薄膜体内观测到与超流密度（superfluid density）降低的纳米级缺陷（nanoscopic defects）相关的光电压峰（photovoltage peaks）；该光电压信号随涡旋耗散态（vortex-dissipative state）的演化而变化，归因于缺陷位点处增强的涡旋-反涡旋对成核（vortex-antivortex pair nucleation）。

Conclusion: 该结果为探测超导体中材料不均匀性如何影响光-物质相互作用（light-matter interactions）提供了直接实验途径，对超导器件以及高Tc超导体（high-Tc）和莫尔材料（moiré materials）等强不均匀体系具有重要启示。

Abstract: Nanoscale inhomogeneities are a defining feature of many superconducting materials, yet their local electromagnetic response has remained difficult to access experimentally. This is because their relevant energy scale lies in the terahertz range, where wavelengths -- on the order of hundreds of microns -- are too large to spatially resolve nanoscopic variations. Here, we demonstrate the first application of THz near-field photovoltage nanoscopy in a superconductor, achieving 300 nm spatial resolution at 2.52 THz. Scanning a current-biased NbN strip, we reveal photovoltage peaks within the bulk associated with nanoscopic defects of reduced superfluid density. The observed photovoltage follows the evolution of the vortex-dissipative state and is attributed to enhanced vortex-antivortex pair nucleation at defect sites. Together, these results open a direct route to probing how material inhomogeneities influence light-matter interactions in superconductors, with implications for superconducting devices and strongly inhomogeneous systems such as high-Tc and moiré materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究对Kagome超导体中的超导对称性进行了完整分类（full classification），并通过理论分析展示了呼吸模式驱动下奇频动力学库珀对的出现机制。

Conclusion: 由于奇频配对在时间上本质上是非局域的（nonlocal in time），该结果将呼吸模式作为在Kagome材料中设计动力学库珀对的关键手段。

Abstract: The breathing mode in Kagome materials is a structural modulation that breaks inversion symmetry and has been shown to be a crucial source for intriguing phases in the normal state. We then show that odd-frequency spin-singlet Cooper pairs can be realized by controlling the breathing mode in kagome lattices with conventional spin-singlet $s$-wave superconductivity. Since odd-frequency pairing is intrinsically nonlocal in time, our results put forward the breathing mode for designing dynamical Cooper pairs in kagome materials.

### [34] [Thermal Concentration and Poisson--Dirichlet Edge Statistics for Random--Lattice Gibbs Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00311)
*Masahiro Kaminaga*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究高维Haar随机幺模晶格上的吉布斯测度（Gibbs measure），分析了边缘窗口与原始方向吉布斯系综的极限行为，并建立了固定因子的可见性曲线（visibility curve）c=γ^{-2}，为近似最短向量问题提供了随机晶格热力学参考模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维随机晶格（random lattice）中，理解向量能量（即欧几里得范数的平方）的吉布斯分布对于统计力学（statistical mechanics）和计算数论中的最短向量问题（shortest vector problem, SVP）均具有重要意义。本文旨在建立随机晶格热力学参考模型，探索吉布斯权重在淬火几何无序（quenched geometric disorder）下的极限行为，并刻画近似最短方向的可见性（visibility）条件。

Method: 研究采用概率极限理论分析，分别考虑全符号类吉布斯系综（full sign-class Gibbs ensemble）和原始方向吉布斯系综（primitive-direction Gibbs ensemble）。对于前者，证明边缘窗口（edge window）内的吉布斯质量（Gibbs mass）依分布收敛到泊松点过程（Poisson point process）；对于后者，推导加权矩公式（weighted moment formula）并利用淬火热浓度（quenched thermal concentration）结果，得到固定因子窗口的可见性曲线。

Result: 对于全符号类吉布斯系综：当0<c≤1时，边缘窗口的吉布斯质量依概率趋于零；当c>1时，该质量具有非平凡的泊松极限，且排序后的吉布斯权重收敛到参数为1/c的泊松-狄利克雷分布（Poisson-Dirichlet distribution）。对于原始方向吉布斯系综：在高温区间0<c<1内，固定因子γ>1的原始吉布斯质量在c<γ^{-2}时趋于0，在γ^{-2}<c<1时趋于1，在临界边界c=γ^{-2}处趋于1/2。

Conclusion: 固定因子定理（fixed-factor theorem）是关于原始目标测度（primitive target measure）的可见性陈述，而非原始全晶格吉布斯测度（original full lattice Gibbs measure）。该结果为与近似最短向量相关的吉布斯目标提供了随机晶格热力学参考模型，但并不意味着对最短向量问题存在高效算法。

Abstract: We study Gibbs measures on high--dimensional Haar--random unimodular lattices, where the energy of a lattice vector is its squared Euclidean norm. The random lattice is viewed as quenched geometric disorder, and $c>0$ denotes the scaled inverse temperature. We first analyze the edge window of vectors whose length is within the factor $e^{a/n}$ of the shortest length, with fixed $a$ as $n\to\infty$. For the full sign--class Gibbs ensemble, we prove a Poisson point process limit theorem for the Gibbs mass of this window. The mass vanishes in probability for $0<c\le1$, while for $c>1$ it has a nontrivial Poisson limit, and the ranked Gibbs weights converge to the Poisson--Dirichlet distribution with parameter $1/c$. We then pass to a primitive--direction Gibbs ensemble and consider a fixed approximation factor $γ>1$. For this modified ensemble, we prove a weighted moment formula and a quenched thermal concentration result in the high--temperature range $0<c<1$. This yields the primitive fixed--factor visibility curve $c=γ^{-2}$ for approximate shortest directions. More precisely, the primitive Gibbs mass of the fixed--factor window tends to zero for $c<γ^{-2}$, to one for $γ^{-2}<c<1$, and to $1/2$ at the critical boundary $c=γ^{-2}$. Thus the fixed--factor theorem is a visibility statement for an idealized primitive target measure, not for the original full lattice Gibbs measure. The results provide a random--lattice thermodynamic reference model for Gibbs targets related to approximate shortest vectors, without implying an efficient algorithm for the shortest vector problem.

</details>


### [35] [(Non-)Hyperuniformity of Second Order Statistics of Point Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00587)
*Fabio Frommer,Martin Hanke*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了两类平稳点过程——投影核行列式点过程（determinantal processes with projection kernels）和超稳定对相互作用吉布斯点过程（Gibbs point processes with superstable pair interactions）的二阶统计量（second order statistics）的方差渐近行为，发现其方差均与球体体积成正比，即表现出非超均匀（non-hyperuniform）行为，并对统计力学中的逆Henderson问题有重要应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨行列式点过程与吉布斯点过程这两类典型平稳点过程的二阶统计量方差的渐近增长行为，并考察其超均匀（hyperuniform）性质的有无。

Method: 采用渐近分析方法，研究原点周围球体内二阶统计量（second order statistics）的方差，并分析结构因子（structure factor）及巴特利特谱测度（Bartlett spectral measure）的符号性质。

Result: 两类过程二阶统计量的方差渐近均与球体体积成正比，即呈现非超均匀（non-hyperuniform）行为；吉布斯过程的结构因子严格正定，而行列式过程的结构因子仅在原点处有简单零点（simple zero）。

Conclusion: 对于超稳定相互作用的吉布斯过程，上述结果可应用于统计力学中的逆Henderson问题（inverse Henderson problem）。

Abstract: We investigate statistical properties of certain stationary point processes, namely determinantal processes with projection kernels and Gibbs point processes with superstable pair interactions. These are examples of hyperuniform and non-hyperuniform stationary point processes, respectively. We are interested in the variance of their second order statistics within a ball around the origin, and we study the asymptotic growth of this variance as the radius of the ball goes to infinity. It is shown that, generically, for both types of processes the variance is asymptotically proportional to the volume of the ball. In other words: the second order statistics of these point processes behave non-hyperuniform. For Gibbs processes with superstable interactions these results have an interesting application to the so-called inverse Henderson problem of statistical mechanics.
  We also show that the structure factor (respectively the Bartlett spectral measure) of these Gibbs processes is strictly positive, while it is positive except for a simple zero at the origin for the determinantal processes.

</details>
