### [36] [Topological Hall plateau in quasi-2D kagome magnet YMn$_6$Sn$_6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00150)
*Sambit Jena,Nastaran Salehi,Manuel Pereiro Lopez,Olle Eriksson,Narayan Mohanta,Karthik V Raman,Tanay Nag,Banasree Sadhukhan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理（ab initio）计算和自旋动力学（spin-dynamics）模拟，研究了Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）在kagome磁体YMn₆Sn₆中的作用，发现平面DMI与铁磁交换共同稳定了准二维中的无序斯格明子（skyrmion）相，并揭示了该相中的拓扑霍尔平台（topological Hall plateau）和拓扑磁振子激发（topological magnon excitations）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）在kagome磁体中对自旋织构（spin texture）的调控作用，特别是无序斯格明子（skyrmion）相的形成条件及其物理响应。

Method: 结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）与自旋动力学（spin-dynamics）模拟的第一性原理（ab initio）框架，生成无序斯格明子的真实自旋织构（spin texture）。

Result: 无序斯格明子相在外磁场B_ext < 0.5 T的范围内持续存在，且斯格明子尺寸随磁场增大而减小；在-0.5 ≤ B_ext < 0.5 T区间内出现拓扑霍尔平台（topological Hall plateau），该响应关于磁场呈反对称，其幅值和符号由Hund耦合强度与化学势的复杂相互作用决定，体现了狄拉克点（Dirac points）和范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities）的作用；此外，在无序斯格明子相中发现了拓扑磁振子激发（topological magnon excitations）。

Conclusion: 在准二维YMn₆Sn₆中，平面DMI与铁磁交换可稳定无序斯格明子相，该相表现出由近均匀标量自旋手性（scalar spin chirality）驱动的拓扑霍尔平台，并支持拓扑磁振子激发，为理解kagome磁体中的拓扑自旋现象提供了新视角。

Abstract: We examine the impact of the Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (DMI) in kagome magnets and show that a predominantly planar DMI together with ferromagnetic exchange stabilizes a disordered skyrmion phase in quasi-two-dimensional (2D) YMn$_6$Sn$_6$. Within an ab initio framework combining density functional theory and spin-dynamics simulations, we generate realistic spin textures of disordered skyrmion and find that this phase persists for $B_{ext} < 0.5$ T, with a decreasing skyrmion size as magnetic field increases. We demonstrate the emergence of topological Hall plateau in the range $-0.5 \leq B_{ext} < 0.5$ T, driven by nearly uniform scalar spin chirality and the resulting constant real-space Berry curvature. This response is anti-symmetric with magnetic field while magnitude and sign of these plateau are determined by a complex interplay between Hund's coupling strength and chemical potential signifying the role of Dirac points and van Hove singularities. In addition, we reveal topological magnon excitations in the disordered skyrmion phase of quasi-2D YMn$_6$Sn$_6$.

</details>


### [37] [Structure-Dependent Chemical Order Modification in Strained Alloy Nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00195)
*Yue Wang,Zibo Chen,Evropi Toulkeridou,Joseph Kioseoglou,Panagiotis Grammatikopoulos*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过原子尺度分子动力学（molecular dynamics）和蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，系统探究了应变作为控制参数对双金属纳米合金（nanoalloy）化学有序性（chemical ordering）的影响，发现应变效应强烈依赖于纳米颗粒的具体结构构型：截角八面体（truncated octahedral）颗粒的化学有序性对应变不敏感，而二十面体（icosahedral）颗粒在拉伸应变下表面Ni浓度显著增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米合金（nanoalloy）的物理化学性质对原子排列高度敏感，而实际应用中的纳米颗粒通常负载于基底之上，基底与颗粒间的强相互作用会引入显著的晶格应变（lattice strain），因此需要系统理解应变作为一种外部控制参数如何影响纳米合金的化学有序性（chemical ordering）。

Method: 采用原子尺度分子动力学（molecular dynamics）和蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，通过隐式锚定界面（implicit anchored interface）施加可控的拉伸应变（tensile strain）和压缩应变（compressive strain），系统探测具有不同结构构型（structural motif）的NiPt纳米颗粒的响应。

Result: 对于截角八面体（truncated octahedral）颗粒，即使在较大应变下，化学有序性和偏析（segregation）行为仍保持高度稳健，表明内在热力学偏好占主导。对于二十面体（icosahedral）颗粒，则观察到显著的应变诱导化学再分布，拉伸应变下表面Ni浓度显著上升。

Conclusion: 应变能以结构依赖的方式选择性地调控纳米合金的化学有序性——该效应在二十面体结构中的产生归因于其固有的几何挫败（geometric frustration）与高比例低配位（undercoordinated）位点的共同作用。这项工作为理解应变诱导的纳米合金化学有序性提供了通用框架（general framework）。

Abstract: Alloy nanoparticles (nanoalloys) exhibit tuneable physicochemical properties that depend sensitively on their atomic arrangement, making control over chemical ordering a central challenge in nanomaterials design. While most theoretical studies consider nanoalloys in vacuum, practical systems are typically supported, where strong cluster-substrate interactions can introduce significant lattice strain. Here, we investigate strain as a control parameter for chemical ordering in bimetallic nanoalloys using atomistic molecular dynamics and Monte Carlo simulations. By imposing controlled tensile and compressive strain through an implicit anchored interface, we systematically probe the response of NiPt nanoparticles with distinct structural motifs. For truncated octahedral particles, we find that chemical ordering and segregation behaviour remain remarkably robust even under large strains, indicating that intrinsic thermodynamic preferences dominate. In contrast, icosahedral nanoparticles exhibit pronounced strain-induced chemical redistribution, with a significant increase in surface Ni concentration under tensile strain. This behaviour is attributed to the combined effects of intrinsic geometric frustration and a high fraction of undercoordinated sites in icosahedral structures. Our results demonstrate that strain can selectively modulate chemical ordering in nanoalloys in a structure-dependent manner, establishing a general framework for understanding strain-induced chemical ordering in nanoalloys.

</details>


### [38] [Dominant-pair free energies predict phase selection in high-entropy alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00203)
*Dennis Boakye,Chuang Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于半经验宏观原子模型和Dinsdale晶格稳定性数据库的热力学框架，通过主导对机制将复杂多组元B2有序化问题简化为有效伪二元系统，并结合布拉格-威廉姆斯自由能与最低自由能分类器，实现多组元合金相稳定性的连续预测，在269个高熵合金样本上优于传统相选择判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有相选择标准（phase-selection criteria）多将多组元合金中的相选择简化为单一标量参数，无法显式表达任何竞争有序相的自由能，缺乏热力学基础。

Method: 基于半经验宏观原子模型（semi-empirical macroscopic atom model）和Dinsdale晶格稳定性数据库（Dinsdale lattice stability database）构建热力学框架；提出主导对机制（dominant-pair mechanism），将多组元B2有序化问题简化为有效伪二元系统（effective pseudo-binary system），并解析求解布拉格-威廉姆斯自由能（Bragg-Williams free energy）；结合最低自由能分类器（minimum-free-energy classifier）进行相预测。

Result: 在269个实验表征的高熵合金样本上，该模型在类平衡宏F1指标（class-balanced macro-F1 metric）上优于传统相选择判据，在三分类任务中达到77.9%的准确率，优于价电子浓度判据（valence electron concentration criterion）。

Conclusion: 该模型具有通用性和计算高效性，能够在大范围组分和温度下预测多组元合金的相稳定性，输出连续相稳定性图谱而非单一标量值。

Abstract: Phase selection in multicomponent alloys is governed by the competition between entropic stabilization of disordered solutions and enthalpic driving forces for chemical ordering. However, widely used parametric criteria reduce it to a single scalar, carrying no explicit free energy for any competing ordered phase. Herein, we develop a thermodynamic framework based on the semi-empirical macroscopic atom model and the Dinsdale lattice stability database to fill this gap. We show that a dominant-pair mechanism, in which the Al-transition-metal interaction family dominates the ordering enthalpy, enables the complex multicomponent B2-ordering problem to be reduced to an effective pseudo-binary system with an analytically evaluated Bragg-Williams free energy. Combined with a minimum-free-energy classifier, the framework predicts the lowest-energy phase as a function of composition and temperature. This provides continuous phase stability maps rather than the single-value predictions of conventional descriptors. Demonstrated on high-entropy alloys using a dataset of 269 experimentally characterized samples, the model outperforms widely used phase-selection criteria in the class-balanced macro-F1 metric and achieves 77.9% on the well-posed three-class task, outperforming the valence electron concentration criterion. The model is general by construction and computationally efficient for predicting phase stability in multicomponent alloys over a broad range of compositions and temperatures.

</details>


### [39] [Anomalous bulk dealloying below the parting limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00246)
*Weiyue Zhou,Hooman Gholamzadeh,Lei Ding,Kevin Daub,Mehdi Mosayebi,Travis Casagrande,Yingxin Zhu,Miaomiao Jin,Mark R. Daymond,Yang Yang,Michael P. Short,Suraj Y. Persaud*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示了熔盐环境中低于经典临界浓度（parting limit）的异常块体脱合金（bulk dealloying）机制，提出晶界辅助脱合金理论——扩散诱导再结晶（DIR）生成高密度晶界网络，促进熔盐渗透，从而驱动远低于传统报告阈值的块体脱合金，并产生类似不连续沉淀（discontinuous precipitation, DP）的独特形貌。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 熔盐环境中存在低于经典脱合金理论临界浓度（约50–60 at.%）的异常块体脱合金现象，但其根本机制尚不明确。阐明这一机制对于核能、航空航天等能源系统及电化学应用中脱合金行为的预测与控制至关重要。

Method: 采用脱合金区域的三维（3D）重构，并结合晶体学（crystallographic）与元素分析（elemental analyses），直接绘制三维晶界-空位（GB-void）结构。

Result: 发现扩散诱导再结晶（DIR）形成高密度晶界网络，该网络促进熔盐渗透，可在远低于传统报告的脱合金极限（parting limit）下驱动块体脱合金，并产生类似不连续沉淀（DP）的独特形貌。

Conclusion: 晶界-空位（GB-void）的动态相互作用是理解并在复杂电化学环境中预测和控制脱合金行为的关键。

Abstract: Dealloying has been extensively studied both as a corrosion degradation mechanism in structural materials, including those used in nuclear, aerospace, or marine environments, and as a versatile method to fabricate porous materials for catalysts and other functional applications. Classical dealloying theory in aqueous environments predicts a critical reactive-element concentration (parting limit) for continuous selective dissolution at temperatures where bulk diffusion does not dominate; this threshold is commonly reported around 50~60 at.%. Yet recent studies show that molten salt environments can generate extensive bulk dealloying below this threshold. Despite the importance of this anomalous dealloying behavior in many energy systems and electrochemical applications, its fundamental origin remains elusive. Here, we address this critical gap, revealing a grain boundary (GB)-assisted bulk dealloying mechanism. Using three-dimensional (3D) reconstruction of the dealloyed regions correlated with crystallographic and elemental analyses, we directly map the 3D GB-void architecture and reveal that diffusion-induced recrystallization (DIR) generates a high-density GB network, which then promotes molten-salt infiltration and can drive bulk dealloying far-below the conventionally reported parting limit, producing a distinctive morphology reminiscent of discontinuous precipitation (DP). Understanding this dynamic GB-void interplay is crucial for the prediction and control of dealloying in complex electrochemical environments.

</details>


### [40] [Modulation of the Nernst Thermoelectrics by Regulating the Anomalous Hall and Nernst Angles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00401)
*Meng Lyu,Junyan Liu,Jianlei Shen,Shen Zhang,Yang Liu,Jinying Yang,Yibo Wang,Yiting Feng,Binbin Wang,Hongxiang Wei,Enke Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示了磁性Weyl半金属中反常能斯特电导率（ANC）的大小与反常能斯特角和反常霍尔角之和直接相关，通过调控两者协同作用可有效优化ANC；在铁掺杂Co3Sn2S2中实验验证了该机制，并观察到40–140 K温度范围内稳固的TlnT标度律，暗示其内在起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性Weyl半金属（magnetic Weyl semimetals）中的大反常能斯特效应在拓扑热电（topological thermoelectrics）领域具有重要应用前景，但目前优化能斯特热电性能的方法仍然有限，亟需提出有效的调控策略。

Method: 通过理论分析建立反常能斯特电导率（anomalous Nernst conductivity, ANC）与反常能斯特角（anomalous Nernst angle）和反常霍尔角（anomalous Hall angle）之和的直接关系，并利用铁掺杂磁性拓扑材料Co3Sn2S2进行实验调控验证。

Result: 发现反常霍尔角符号在特定材料中相对稳定，而反常能斯特角符号可被内在调控，通过使两者协同作用可有效优化ANC；在所有样品中观察到40–140 K温度范围内ANC呈现稳健的TlnT标度律（scaling law）。

Conclusion: 该研究为优化磁性拓扑材料中的能斯特热电性能提供了一种普适性方案，尤其适用于反常能斯特角与反常霍尔角符号相反的常见情形。

Abstract: The large anomalous Nernst effect in magnetic Weyl semimetals is one of the most intriguing transport phenomena, which draws significant attention for its potential applications in topological thermoelectrics. Despite frequent reports of substantial anomalous Nernst conductivity (ANC), methods to optimize Nernst thermoelectrics remain limited. Our research reveals that the magnitude of the ANC is directly related to the sum of the anomalous Nernst and Hall angles. While the sign of the anomalous Hall angle is relatively stable in a certain material, the sign of the anomalous Nernst angle can be intrinsically tuned. Therefore, the ANC can be effectively optimized by regulating these angles to work in concert. This finding is verified by experimental modulation from iron-doped magnetic topological material Co3Sn2S2. Additionally, we observed a robust TlnT scaling law of the ANC over the temperature range of 40 to 140 K in all studied samples, suggesting an intrinsic origin of the ANC. Considering the common opposite sign of the anomalous Nernst and Hall angles in many magnetic topological materials, our research offers an applicable scheme for optimizing the Nernst thermoelectrics.

</details>


### [41] [Atom-selective spin-polarized transport in a charge-ordered altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00506)
*Liu Yang,Yuan-Yuan Jiang,Xiao-Yan Guo,Yi-Dong Liu,Xian-Zhe Chen,Wen-Jian Lu,Yu-Ping Sun,Ming Li,Ding-Fu Shao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算和量子输运模拟，发现电荷有序的交替磁体α-Fe₂PO₅在费米能级附近交替磁自旋分裂较弱的情况下，仍表现出显著实空间自旋选择性——电荷序在子晶格内产生不等价Fe²⁺和Fe³⁺位点，电子/空穴掺杂分别激活以Fe³⁺和Fe²⁺为主的自旋极化通道，且通道在反铁磁子晶格上携带相反自旋极化，形成具有隐藏Néel自旋特征的全局补偿电荷流；此外，提出一种全集成α-Fe₂PO₅隧道结，通过匹配/失配原子选择通道实现数量级的电导调制，建立了原子级自旋功能与自旋电子器件的实空间设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交替磁体（altermagnets）无需净磁化即可实现自旋极化输运，是自旋电子学的重要平台；然而，其输运特性通常仅在动量空间自旋分裂（momentum-space spin splitting）框架下讨论，对实空间（real-space）自旋选择性的机制理解不足。本文旨在探索电荷有序（charge order）能否在交替磁体中引入额外的实空间自旋选择性，并为原子级自旋功能器件提供新的设计原则。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与量子输运模拟（quantum transport simulations），以电荷有序交替磁体α-Fe₂PO₅为研究对象，分析其电子结构、自旋极化通道及输运特性，并构建全集成隧道结（all-in-one tunnel junction）模型。

Result: 电荷序在每个子晶格（sublattice）内产生了不等价的Fe²⁺和Fe³⁺位点；褶皱C型反铁磁堆垛（puckered C-type antiferromagnetic stacking）抑制了子晶格间输运。电子掺杂和空穴掺杂分别激活以Fe³⁺和Fe²⁺位点为主导的自旋极化通道，且两个反铁磁子晶格上的通道携带相反自旋极化，形成全局补偿但具有隐藏Néel自旋特征（hidden Néel spin character）的电荷流。在隧道结中，原子选择通道的匹配与失配可导致数量级（orders-of-magnitude）的电导调制。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了电荷序驱动的实空间自旋选择新机制，证明即使在交替磁自旋分裂较弱的体系中也能实现显著的自旋极化输运；提出了基于原子选择通道（atom-selective channels）匹配的实空间设计原则，为开发新型原子级自旋电子学器件（spintronic devices）提供了理论依据和材料平台。

Abstract: Altermagnets provide a promising platform for spin-polarized transport without net magnetization, but their transport properties are usually discussed in terms of momentum-space spin splitting. Here, using first-principles calculations and quantum transport simulations, we show that the charge-ordered altermagnet $α$-Fe$_2$PO$_5$ exhibits a distinct form of real-space spin selectivity despite weak altermagnetic spin splitting near the Fermi level. The charge order creates inequivalent Fe$^{2+}$ and Fe$^{3+}$ sites within each sublattice, while the puckered C-type antiferromagnetic stacking suppresses inter-sublattice transport. As a result, electron and hole doping activate spin-polarized transport predominantly through Fe$^{3+}$- and Fe$^{2+}$-based channels, respectively. These atom-selective channels carry opposite spin polarizations on the two antiferromagnetic sublattices, giving rise to a globally compensated charge current with hidden Néel spin character. We further propose an all-in-one $α$-Fe$_2$PO$_5$ tunnel junction, where matching or mismatching atom-selective conduction channels yields orders-of-magnitude conductance modulation. Our findings establish a real-space design principle for atomically controlled spin functionality and spintronic devices.

</details>


### [42] [Effect of granules anisotropy on "double quantum" magnetic resonance excitation in nanogranular composites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00526)
*A. B. Drovosekov,M. Yu. Dmitrieva,A. V. Sitnikov,S. N. Nikolaev,V. V. Rylkov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用电子自旋共振（ESR）方法，在宽频（7–80 GHz）和宽温（4.2–300 K）范围内研究了金属-绝缘体纳米颗粒复合膜 (CoFeB)x(Al2O3)100-x，发现除常规的铁磁共振信号外，还存在一个有效g因子约为4的额外吸收峰。该峰被用量子力学“巨自旋（giant spin）”模型解释为铁磁颗粒中“双量子（double quantum）”跃迁的激发。研究还考察了金属相含量x和热退火对ESR谱参数的影响，揭示了纳米复合物中铁磁颗粒尺寸与其各向异性之间的相关性，表明该各向异性具有表面起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究金属-绝缘体纳米颗粒复合膜中除常规铁磁共振信号之外的额外吸收峰的物理机制，并系统研究金属相含量和热退火对该谱峰行为的影响，以及铁磁颗粒尺寸与各向异性之间的关联。

Method: 采用电子自旋共振（electron spin resonance, ESR）方法，在频率7–80 GHz和温度4.2–300 K范围内测量(CoFeB)x(Al2O3)100-x薄膜；通过改变名义金属相含量x（约15–50 at.%）以及不同温度的热退火来调控铁磁颗粒的尺寸与各向异性；利用量子力学“巨自旋（giant spin）”模型解释“双量子（double quantum）”跃迁产生的吸收峰。

Result: 实验观察到有效g因子约为4的额外吸收峰，其行为可用“巨自旋”模型很好地解释；该峰强度是频率和温度的复杂函数，与颗粒磁矩和各向异性相关；铁磁颗粒尺寸与各向异性之间存在相关性，表明各向异性源于表面效应。

Conclusion: 纳米复合膜中出现的g≈4吸收峰源于铁磁颗粒中“双量子”跃迁的激发；铁磁颗粒的各向异性具有表面起源，且可以通过改变金属相含量和热退火进行调控。

Abstract: Films of metal-insulator nanogranular composites (CoFeB)x(Al2O3)100-x with different contents of the metal ferromagnetic (FM) phase CoFeB (x ~ 15-50 at.%) are investigated by the method of electron spin resonance (ESR) in a wide range of frequencies (f = 7-80 GHz) and temperatures (T = 4.2-300 K). Besides the conventional FM resonance signal, the experimental spectra demonstrate an additional absorption peak with a double effective g-factor g ~ 4 which is explained within the quantum mechanical "giant spin" model by excitation of "double quantum" transitions in FM granules CoFeB. According to the theory, the intensity of this "double quantum" peak is a complex function of frequency and temperature, including as parameters the granule magnetic moment and anisotropy. Experimentally, the size and anisotropy of the granules can be varied either changing the nominal FM phase content x in the composites or annealing the samples at different temperatures. Here we study the effects of concentration x and thermal annealing of (CoFeB)x(Al2O3)100-x films on their ESR spectral parameters. The observed behavior of the "double quantum" peak intensity is well explained within the considered "giant spin" theoretical concept. In conclusion, we demonstrate the correlation between the size of FM granules in nanocomposites and their anisotropy, indicating the surface origin of this anisotropy.

</details>


### [43] [A general-purpose atomic cluster expansion interatomic potential for niobium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00540)
*Aleksei Egorov,Ralf Drautz,Thomas Hammerschmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

Method: 采用原子团簇展开（atomic cluster expansion, ACE）方法构建通用势函数，在数千个密度泛函理论（DFT）结构上训练，训练数据涵盖广泛的局域环境（local environments）。

Result: 所构建的ACE势函数在精度、效率和鲁棒性之间取得了平衡，在近百万原子的断裂分子动力学模拟中表现出色，达到了接近DFT精度的水平。

Conclusion: ACE势函数能够以接近DFT的精度对铌进行大规模原子尺度模拟，优于现有的经验势和机器学习势，包括一种新型的通用机器学习（ML）势。

Abstract: Niobium, a body-centered cubic transition metal, poses a challenge for interatomic potentials, which struggle to capture its properties, such as phonons, high-pressure behavior, energy barriers to dislocation glide, and others. To tackle this challenge, we constructed a general-purpose atomic cluster expansion (ACE) potential for niobium. We trained our ACE on thousands of density functional theory (DFT) structures spanning a diversity of local environments. We validated it across a range of properties and compared it with existing empirical and machine learning (ML) potentials, including a novel universal ML potential. The resulting ACE balances accuracy, efficiency, and robustness, enabling large-scale exploration of niobium with near-DFT precision. Finally, our ACE held its own in a stringent test: a near-million-atom molecular dynamics simulation of fracture

### [44] [Entropy-Driven Structural Phase Transition in Nb$_3$Cl$_8$ via Density Functional Theory and an Effective Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00599)
*Chenjie Zhu,Shuai Zhang,Zhong Fang,Zhijun Wang,Quansheng Wu,Hongming Weng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算与扩展哈伯德模型（extended Hubbard model）构建统一自由能框架，揭示了Nb₃Cl₈中α→β结构相变由声子与自旋熵共同驱动，并解释了c轴单轴压力抑制相变的热力学机制，为在低温下探索α相中候选量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid, QSL）态提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Nb₃Cl₈作为一种在有效三角晶格上形成的平带簇莫特绝缘体（flat-band cluster Mott insulator），被认为是潜在承载量子自旋液体（QSL）态的候选材料。然而，约90K处的一级结构相变将高温顺磁α相转变为低温非磁性β相，抑制了α相中候选QSL区域的研究。为澄清该相变的微观起源，本研究结合第一性原理与扩展哈伯德模型构建统一自由能框架。

Method: 将第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）与扩展哈伯德模型（extended Hubbard model）相结合，构建描述α相与β相的统一自由能框架（unified free-energy framework）；进一步通过评估与压力相关的广义焓（generalized enthalpy）分析c轴单轴压力对相变的影响。

Result: 相变由声子熵和自旋熵联合驱动：α相因较软的声子（softer phonons）和更大的顺磁自旋熵而稳定，β相则通过层间二聚化（interlayer dimerization）硬化声子并通过单态形成（singlet formation）淬灭自旋熵而获得稳定。c轴单轴压力可抑制相变，使α相在低温下得以稳定存在，从而为探索其候选QSL态创造条件。

Conclusion: 该工作从热力学角度揭示了Nb₃Cl₈中α→β相变由声子与自旋熵竞争驱动的本质，并提供了c轴压力抑制相变、稳定α相进而可能实现低温QSL探索的理论解释。

Abstract: As a prototypical flat-band cluster Mott insulator on an effective triangular lattice, Nb$_3$Cl$_8$ is a potential candidate for hosting a quantum spin liquid (QSL) state. Nevertheless, a first-order structural phase transition around 90K transforms the high-temperature paramagnetic $α$ phase into the low-temperature nonmagnetic $β$ phase, suppressing the candidate QSL regime of the $α$ phase. To clarify the microscopic origin of this transition, we combine first-principles calculations with an extended Hubbard model to construct a unified free-energy framework. This framework reveals that the transition is jointly driven by phonon and spin entropy: the $α$ phase is stabilized by softer phonons and larger paramagnetic spin entropy, whereas the $β$ phase is favored by interlayer dimerization, which hardens the phonons and quenches the spin entropy through singlet formation. Furthermore, by evaluating the pressure-dependent generalized enthalpy, we provide a thermodynamic explanation for the suppression of the transition under c-axis uniaxial pressure, where stabilizing the $α$ phase may allow the candidate QSL regime of the $α$ phase to be explored at low temperatures.

### [47] [Atomic Cluster Expansion Potentials for Screw Dislocations in BCC Refractory Metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00717)
*Lei Zhang,Francesco Maresca*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究开发了针对第5族（V、Nb、Ta）和第6族（Mo、W）难熔金属（refractory metals）的原子簇展开（atomic cluster expansion, ACE）势函数，显著改善了体心立方（bcc）金属中螺位错（screw dislocation）性质的描述，实现了对Mo和W的近密度泛函理论（DFT）精度，并对V、Nb、Ta取得了实质性改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过扩展现有密度泛函理论（DFT）数据库，为V、Nb、Ta、Mo、W这五种难熔金属开发了一系列原子簇展开（ACE）势函数。

Conclusion: ACE势函数为难熔金属中螺位错行为提供了重要的模拟工具，尤其是对Mo和W达到了接近第一性原理的精度，并揭示了数据库构成与元素特异性对势函数可迁移性的关键影响。

Abstract: Accurate atomistic modeling of screw dislocations in body-centered cubic (bcc) metals remains challenging because their plasticity is governed by a complex dislocation glide behavior due to their compact three-fold symmetric core structure and a strongly temperature-dependent flow stress induced by the large Peierls barrier. In the context of group 6 (V, Nb, Ta) and group 5 (Mo, W) refractory metals (RMs), both classical interatomic potentials and some machine learning potentials consistently fail to reproduce density functional theory (DFT) Peierls barriers and the glide plane. Here, we developed an array of atomic cluster expansion (ACE) potentials for these RMs by extending an existing DFT database. The developed ACE potentials significantly improve the description of screw dislocation properties, achieving near-DFT accuracy for Mo and W and substantial improvement for V, Nb, and Ta. The results show that transferability to screw dislocation behavior depends sensitively on both database composition and element-specific energetics, and that achieving a single-humped Peierls barrier alone is not a sufficient validation metric for accurate prediction of dislocation glide. For Nb, Mo, and W, the developed ACE models also enable reliable calculation of kink-pair activation enthalpies, which are well described by both Kocks' law and a line-tension model.

### [48] [The BiP-PRISM algorithm for fast and scalable core-loss STEM-EELS simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00756)
*Philipp Pelz*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出BiP-PRISM算法，通过对探针形成和探测器传播两个PRISM矩阵分别进行束划分（beam partitioning）与自然邻域插值（natural-neighbor interpolation）重构，在保证高精度的前提下大幅降低原子分辨STEM-EELS模拟的计算与内存开销，首次实现消费级GPU上的全分辨率元素映射（elemental mapping）、4D数据立方体（4D cubes）与动量分辨qEELS模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原子分辨扫描透射电子显微镜-电子能量损失谱（STEM-EELS）的定量解释需要对电子探针在芯损失跃迁（core-loss transitions）前后进行动力学模拟，计算成本极高。现有PRISM算法虽通过复用散射矩阵（scattering matrices）加速了这一过程，但计算与内存需求仍限制了其在消费级硬件上的应用。

Method: 将PRISM算法中的两个散射矩阵——探针形成矩阵（probe-forming matrix，$\mathcal{S}_1$）与探测器传播矩阵（detector-propagating matrix，$\mathcal{S}_2$）——分别进行束划分（beam partitioning），每个矩阵仅在稀疏的父束（parent beams）集合上计算，再通过自然邻域插值（natural-neighbor interpolation）在电离原子（ionized atom）位置进行局域重构。

Result: 理论证明总误差完全由电离原子处的重构误差决定（locality result）。算法消除了逐扫描点出射波传播（per-scan exit wave propagation）的步骤，大幅降低了内存需求。在消费级GPU上实现了全分辨率元素映射、4D数据立方体与动量分辨qEELS模拟。多模态五边氧化物界面图谱与FePt纳米颗粒Fe-L边图谱的模拟验证表明，在5倍内存缩减下仍能达到高精度。

Conclusion: BiP-PRISM算法在显著降低计算与内存开销的同时保持了高精度，将原子分辨STEM-EELS的定量模拟从专业集群扩展至消费级GPU，为更广泛的材料科学定量分析提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Quantitative interpretation of atomic-resolution STEM-EELS requires dynamical simulation of the electron probe before and after core-loss transitions, which is computationally expensive. While the PRISM algorithm accelerates this by reusing scattering matrices, we introduce beam partitioning for both the probe-forming ($\mathcal{S}_1$) and detector-propagating ($\mathcal{S}_2$) PRISM matrices to further reduce computational and memory costs. Each matrix is calculated on a sparse set of parent beams and reconstructed via natural-neighbor interpolation locally at the ionized atom. A locality result demonstrates that the total error is governed entirely by this on-atom reconstruction error. The resulting BiP-PRISM algorithm removes per-scan exit wave propagation and significantly reduces memory requirements, enabling full-resolution elemental mapping, 4D cubes, and momentum-resolved qEELS on consumer-grade GPUs. We characterize the approximation's validity regime and demonstrate the simulation of a multimodal five-edge oxide-interface map and an FePt nanoparticle Fe-L map at 5x memory reduction, showing that the algorithm achieves high accuracy with significantly lower computational demands.

</details>

### [50] [Vanadium superconducting microwave resonators on silicon wafers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00809)
*Y. Fujita,Y. Urade,Y. Hibino,M. Tsujimoto,K. Inomata,G. Fujii,W. Mizubayashi*

TL;DR: 本研究以钒（vanadium, V）作为超导量子器件的新型材料，通过溅射法在硅衬底上生长四种V膜结构，并借助共面波导谐振器分析其微波损耗与结构性质之间的关联。研究发现V表面损耗主要由与平均光子数无关的非二能级系统（non-TLS）损耗主导，Ta覆盖层可缓解该损耗；尽管Nb缓冲层能提高V膜的晶格取向均匀性，但反而导致更高的非TLS损耗，其来源可能与V氧化物或氢化物有关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解超导薄膜中材料性质与微波损耗之间的关联，是开发用于量子电路的低损耗材料的关键课题。本研究聚焦于钒（V）这一新型超导量子器件材料，探讨其结构性质与微波损耗之间的关系。

Method: 采用溅射法在(001)取向硅片上生长四种V膜结构（Nb/V/Ta、Nb/V、V/Ta、V），以Nb和Ta分别作为缓冲层和覆盖层材料；利用X射线衍射（XRD）和原子力显微镜（AFM）表征膜结构；制备共面波导谐振器并进行微波测量，获得内部品质因子（$Q_{\rm int}$）随平均光子数（$\langle n_{\rm ph} \rangle$）的变化关系；使用能量色散X射线光谱（EDS）和X射线光电子能谱（XPS）分析元素组成。

Result: 生长在Nb缓冲层上的V膜比直接生长在硅片上的V膜具有更高的晶格取向均匀性和更小的晶粒尺寸；V表面的损耗由与$\langle n_{\rm ph} \rangle$无关的非二能级系统（non-TLS）损耗主导，Ta覆盖层可缓解该损耗；Nb缓冲层上的V膜在$\langle n_{\rm ph} \rangle = 10^{0}$至$10^{6}$范围内表现出更低的$Q_{\rm int}$和更高的非TLS损耗，尽管其晶格取向均匀性更高。

Conclusion: V膜中的微波损耗主要来自非TLS损耗，Ta覆盖层可有效降低表面损耗；但更高的晶格取向均匀性并未带来更低的损耗，V氧化物和/或V氢化物可能是导致这一反常趋势的原因。

Abstract: Understanding the correlation between material properties and microwave losses in superconducting films is a crucial subject for developing low-loss materials for quantum circuits. We focus on vanadium (V) as a novel material for superconducting quantum devices and discuss loss in V films in relation to their structural properties. Using a sputtering method, we grow four V-film structures on (001)-oriented Si wafers, employing Nb and Ta as the buffer and capping layer materials, respectively: Nb/V/Ta, Nb/V, V/Ta, and V. X-ray diffraction and atomic force microscopy reveal that the V films grown on the Nb buffer layers have higher uniformity of lattice orientation and smaller grain size than that directly grown on the Si wafer. Coplanar waveguide resonators are fabricated from the four V-film structures, and averaged photon number ($\langle n_{\rm ph} \rangle$) dependences of internal quality factor ($Q_{\rm int}$) are obtained by performing microwave measurements. By analyzing the obtained $Q_{\rm int}$ vs $\langle n_{\rm ph} \rangle$, it is found that loss at the V surface is dominated by $\langle n_{\rm ph} \rangle$-independent non-two-level-system (non-TLS) losses, which can be mitigated by introducing the Ta capping layer. Furthermore, the V films on the Nb buffer layers exhibit lower $Q_{\rm int}$ in the $\langle n_{\rm ph} \rangle$ range from 10$^{0}$ to 10$^{6}$ and higher non-TLS loss than that directly grown on Si wafers, even though the former has higher lattice-orientation uniformity than the latter. Origins of these trends might be relevant to V oxides, of which presence at surfaces and grain boundaries in bulk regions in the V resonators is suggested by energy dispersive X-ray spectroscopy and X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy, and/or V hydrides.

### [52] [Strengthening and interface-mediated plastic co-deformation in an ultrafine Cr-Ni eutectic: A nanomechanical investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00906)
*Arkajit Ghosh,Mustafa Tobah,Jianing Zhou,Jian Wang,Amit Misra*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超细共晶异质结构为高强度材料的塑性提供了严格检验，变形需通过界面和应变梯度来容纳。室温延展性通常受限于硬质相的过早断裂，界面间距、原子结构和局部化学如何实现塑性共变形这一基本问题尚不明确。本研究旨在回答该问题。

Method: 以Cr-Ni二元合金为模型体系，通过电子束粉末床熔融（electron-beam powder bed fusion）制备层状共晶组织（Cr-rich BCC相与Ni-rich FCC相，平均层间距~450 nm）。采用原子分辨率扫描透射电镜（atomic-resolution STEM）表征界面结构；开展扫描电镜内原位微尺度压缩与拉伸实验；结合透射电镜/高分辨扫描透射电镜进行变形序列关联分析；并运用原子尺度建模（atomistic modeling）研究界面影响。

Result: 原子级STEM显示阶梯状半共格（semi-coherent）FCC/BCC界面，具有Kurdjumov-Sachs取向关系，BCC侧数个原子面内存在Ni富集。原位微尺度力学测试表明高流动应力伴随大塑性应变、无开裂。变形序列：初始阶段塑性以FCC片层内与界面相邻区域的应变梯度驱动位错累积为主导，随后发生FCC变形孪晶及局部界面剪切与再取向，BCC相随后出现高密度可移动位错。原子模拟揭示了界面结构与化学对硬质相滑移激活的作用。

Conclusion: 纳米限域（nanoscale confinement）、阶梯状K-S界面结构以及界面化学共同促进了硬质相在单体韧脆转变温度（brittle to ductile transition temperature）以下的位错滑移启动，实现了高流动强度下的塑性共变形。

Abstract: Ultrafine eutectic heterostructures provide a stringent test of plasticity in high-strength materials, where deformation must be accommodated through interfaces and strain gradients. Room temperature ductility is typically limited by premature fracture of the hard phase, leaving open the fundamental questions regarding the interface spacing, atomic structure and local chemistry that enable plastic co-deformation. Here we address this question using a model system of Cr-Ni binary alloy, processed via electron-beam powder bed fusion that produces a lamellar eutectic microstructure of Cr-rich BCC and Ni-rich FCC phases, with an average interlamellar spacing of ~450 nm. Atomic-resolution STEM revealed a stepped semi-coherent FCC/BCC interface with the Kurdjumov-Sachs orientation relationship and Ni-enrichment confined to a few atomic planes on the BCC side. In situ micro-scale compression and tension tests in SEM demonstrate high flow stresses coupled with large plastic strains without cracking, indicating stable accommodation of plastic incompatibility. Correlative TEM/HR-STEM establishes a deformation sequence: initial plasticity is dominated by strain-gradient driven dislocation accumulation in the FCC lamellae adjacent to interfaces, followed by deformation twinning in FCC and local interfacial shear and reorientation. The BCC phase subsequently develops a high density of mobile dislocations. Atomistic modeling has been employed to understand the influence of the FCC/BCC interface atomic structure and chemistry on the slip activation in the hard phase. These findings show that nanoscale confinement, stepped K-S interfacial structure, and interfacial chemistry collectively promote dislocation glide in a hard phase below its monolithic brittle to ductile transition temperature, and plastic codeformation at high flow strengths.

### [53] [First-principles calculations of spin-split bands in chiral hybrid organic-inorganic perovskites ($R$/$S$-PEA)PbI$_3$ and ($R$/$S$-NEA)PbI$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00933)
*Tetsuya Furukawa,Kazushi Nakano,Youta Suzuki,Takumi Kaneko,Ayumi Ishii,Tetsuaki Itou*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，系统比较了两种手性杂化有机-无机钙钛矿（(R/S-PEA)PbI₃和(R/S-NEA)PbI₃）的自旋劈裂能带结构，揭示了NEA基化合物中更强的价带有效自旋劈裂源于自旋-轨道耦合引起的大能隙和多能带交叉效应，并通过群论分析解释了非对称空间群下的能带简并和自旋极化消失行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性杂化有机-无机钙钛矿（chiral hybrid organic-inorganic perovskites）结合了分子手性（molecular chirality）与重无机离子中的强自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling），为研究手性驱动自旋劈裂能带（chirality-driven spin-split bands）的物理机制提供了理想平台，但不同手性分子对自旋劈裂行为的影响机制尚不清晰。

Method: 采用包含自旋-轨道耦合的第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），对一维手性钙钛矿(R/S-PEA)PbI₃和(R/S-NEA)PbI₃进行能带结构计算，并结合群论分析（group-theoretical analysis）对非对称空间群P2₁2₁2₁下的能带简并和自旋极化特性进行对称性分析。

Result: (R/S-PEA)PbI₃中最低导带以Pb轨道为主，而(R/S-NEA)PbI₃中则为Pb轨道与NEA最低未占分子轨道（LUMO）的杂化。两种化合物在价带顶和导带底附近均呈现显著自旋劈裂；尽管在相关高对称点附近具有相似的线性k劈裂系数，但(R/S-NEA)PbI₃的价带有效自旋劈裂更强，其源自高对称点处自旋-轨道耦合诱导的更大能隙以及多能带结构中的能带（反）交叉效应。此外，对给定分子手性，PEA与NEA基化合物表现出相反的自旋织构（spin texture），与[PbI₆]⁴⁻八面体的相反手性畸变以及此前观测到的相反圆二色性（circular dichroism）符号一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解手性杂化有机-无机钙钛矿中手性依赖的电磁响应（包括圆二色性）提供了坚实的理论基础，并揭示了有机分子轨道参与杂化、多能带交叉效应以及晶格手性畸变共同调控自旋劈裂行为的关键机制。

Abstract: Chiral hybrid organic-inorganic perovskites provide a promising platform for investigating the physics of chirality-driven spin-split bands because they combine robust molecular chirality with strong spin-orbit coupling from heavy inorganic ions. First-principles calculations including spin-orbit coupling are performed for the one-dimensional chiral perovskites ($R$/$S$-PEA)PbI$_3$ and ($R$/$S$-NEA)PbI$_3$ to compare their spin-split band structures and to identify the factors controlling their differences. In ($R$/$S$-PEA)PbI$_3$, the lowest conduction bands predominantly consist of Pb orbitals, whereas in ($R$/$S$-NEA)PbI$_3$, they are formed by hybridization between Pb orbitals and the lowest unoccupied molecular orbital of NEA. Both compounds exhibit pronounced spin splitting near the valence-band maximum and conduction-band minimum. The effective spin splitting of the edges of the valence bands is stronger in ($R$/$S$-NEA)PbI$_3$, despite similar linear-in-$k$ splitting coefficients near the relevant high-symmetry points. This enhancement originates from larger gaps induced by spin-orbit coupling at high-symmetry points and band (anti)crossings in the multiband structure. For a given molecular handedness, the PEA- and NEA-based compounds exhibit opposite spin textures, consistent with the opposite chiral distortions of the [PbI$_6$]$^{4-}$ octahedra and with the previously observed opposite signs of circular dichroism. Group-theoretical analysis for the nonsymmorphic space group $P2_12_12_1$ further accounts for band sticking, symmetry-enforced degeneracies, and the disappearance of spin polarization at specific Brillouin-zone-boundary points. These results provide a solid foundation for future studies of chirality-dependent electromagnetic responses, including circular dichroism, in chiral hybrid organic-inorganic perovskites.

### [54] [Substrate-dependent electrical transport in individual single-walled carbon nanotubes grown across SiO$_2$ and hexagonal boron nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00985)
*Yuanjia Liu,Taiki Inoue,Yoshihiro Kobayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碳纳米管（carbon nanotubes, CNTs）的电子输运性质受周围环境影响显著，衬底是决定器件性能的关键因素。以往研究中不同碳纳米管之间存在手性、直径和缺陷密度的差异，难以可靠地评估衬底的独立作用。

Method: 采用气流导向生长法合成长且对齐的单壁碳纳米管（single-walled CNTs），无需转移处理即可使同一根纳米管跨越不同衬底区域；沿单根碳纳米管制作多通道场效应晶体管（field-effect transistors），直接比较同在SiO₂和hBN上的输运特性。

Result: hBN衬底上的碳纳米管通道始终表现出比SiO₂衬底上更高的场效应迁移率（field-effect mobility）；但在电荷中性点附近的温度依赖输运中，两种衬底均呈现热激活行为，激活能（activation energy）相近，均为15-20 meV。

Conclusion: 结果为hBN增强碳纳米管低场载流子输运提供了直接证据，并表明碳纳米管的本征小带隙基本不受衬底影响，为基于hBN衬底的高性能碳纳米管电子器件奠定了实验基础。

Abstract: The electronic transport properties of carbon nanotubes (CNTs) are strongly affected by their surrounding environment, making the underlying substrate a critical factor for device performance. Here, we demonstrate enhanced carrier transport of individual single-walled CNTs on hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) by directly comparing CNT channels on SiO$_2$ and hBN within the same nanotube. This within-tube comparison removes tube-to-tube variability in chirality, diameter, and defect density, allowing the intrinsic substrate effect to be evaluated more reliably. The CNTs were synthesized using gas flow-directed growth, which yields long, well-aligned CNTs without transfer processes, allowing a single nanotube to extend across different substrate regions. Multichannel field-effect transistors fabricated along an individual CNT exhibit clear ambipolar characteristics. CNT channels on hBN consistently exhibit higher field-effect mobility than those on SiO$_2$. In contrast, temperature-dependent transport near the charge neutrality point exhibits thermally activated behavior with similar activation energies (15-20 meV) on both substrates, indicating that the intrinsic small bandgap of CNTs is largely unaffected by the substrate. These results provide direct evidence that hBN enhances low-field carrier transport in CNTs and establish a foundation for the fabrication of high-performance electronics based on hBN-supported CNTs.

Here, based on a symmetry-decoupled analysis of magnetoelectric coupling in compensated magnets, we establish a geometry-driven spin-ferroelectric coupling mechanism in bilayer breathing kagome lattices. Within this geometric framework interlocking the out-of-plane electric polarization with cooperative intralayer structural distortions, we demonstrate that polarization switching drives a deterministic reversal of the global spin splitting. First-principles calculations on a prototype bilayer Nb3Cl8 successfully validate this mechanism, demonstrating the switching of spin-splitting states through an energetically feasible, asynchronous layer-by-layer transition pathway. ### [56] [Complex crystal structure prediction using ML-enhanced multi-minima iterative genetic algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01004)

Abstract: Current machine learning (ML) approaches for materials discovery rely heavily on known structural databases, limiting their ability to identify entirely novel structure types. In this work, we develop a multi-minima iterative genetic algorithm (MMIGA) that integrates an artificial-neural-network machine learning (ANN-ML) interatomic potential with an iterative, metadynamics-inspired penalty scheme. We demonstrate the robustness of this method on a complex ternary La-Co-Pb system, characterized by Co-Pb immiscibility and an intricate energy landscape. The ML-enhanced MMIGA successfully predicts the ground-state Pbam structure of the recently synthesized La4Co4Pb antagonistic-pair-phase, a novel structure missed by previous database-reliant ML predictions, while also identifying multiple metastable competing phases. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在电子阻止（electronic stopping）能区，高能重离子（swift heavy ion）穿过绝缘体会导致电子系统激发并随后将能量传递给晶格，从而产生损伤。然而，离子轨迹周围的电子能带结构（electronic band structure）会发生径向不均匀的塌缩，这一异质性对能量传递和最终损伤的影响尚不明确。本文旨在量化这种径向异质性效应，改进对Al2O3中辐照损伤的预测。

Method: 采用两步模拟方法：首先使用蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）代码TREKIS描述离子通过后电子与离子系统的初始激发过程；随后利用基于密度泛函理论（DFT）的分子动力学（molecular dynamics）追踪离子径迹（ion track）中能带结构的变化。两者结合，在考虑能带结构空间不均匀性的前提下，计算电子激发弛豫（relaxation）时间内传递给晶格的能量剖面。

Result: 700 MeV Bi离子撞击Al2O3后，在距离子轨迹约2 nm半径内发生瞬态金属-半导体异质结（metal-semiconductor heterojunction），即能带塌缩（band gap collapse）导致金属化（metallization）；在约3–5 nm处能带收缩；半径大于5 nm时能带几乎不变。基于此数据，估算了不同径迹半径处的原子加热（atomic heating）程度，发现损伤图案沿离子路径呈现更明显的不连续特征。

Conclusion: 径向能带异质性（radial band gap heterogeneity）显著影响了能量向晶格传递的剖面，使损伤建模比假设所有电子-空穴（electron-hole）能量均匀传递给原子的传统模型更为精确，预测出更突出的不连续损伤图案。

Abstract: We estimate the effects of radial heterogeneity in the collapse of the electronic band gap on the damage in Al2O3 after impact of a swift heavy ion decelerated in the electronic stopping regime. The Monte Carlo code TREKIS describes the initial excitation of the electronic and ionic systems following the ion passage, while the density functional theory based molecular dynamics traces changes in the band structure in the ion track. This combination of methods enables us to compute the profile of energy transferred to the lattice by the time of relaxation of the electronic excitation, accounting for the induced spatial inhomogeneity of the band structure around the ion trajectory. We demonstrate that impact of a 700 MeV Bi ion induces a transient metal-semiconductor heterojunction in Al2O3: the metallization (the band gap collapse) occurs within a radius of about 2 nm from the ion trajectory. The band gap shrinks at distances of about 3-5 nm, while it remains almost unaffected at radii larger than 5 nm. Using this data, we estimate the atomic heating depending on the degree of band gap reduction at different radii from the ion trajectory. This approach refines the damage modeling, producing more pronounced discontinuous damage patterns along the ion path for all crystallographic directions compared to the model that assumes all the energy accumulated in the electron-hole ensemble is delivered to the atoms.

</details>


### [58] [Diamond Diode for Extreme Venus Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01093)
*Harshad Surdi,Gabriel Munro-Ludders,Mohamadali Malakoutian,Srabanti Chowdhury,Savannah Eisner,Mohamed Fadil Isamotu,Mengyang Yuan,Stephen Goodnick,Franz Koeck,James Lyons,Trevor Thornton,Robert Nemanich*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种具有迄今最高电流密度（约116 kA/cm²）的金刚石肖特基PIN二极管（SPIND），并建立了包含热电子发射（thermionic emission）和空间电荷限制电流（space charge limited current, SCLC）的分析模型，结合Silvaco ATLAS TCAD仿真准确复现了实验J-V特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金刚石因其高击穿电场和优异热导率而成为功率半导体器件的理想候选材料，但现有金刚石肖特基二极管仍受限于缺陷密度和接触电阻，导致器件性能未能达到理论极限。本工作旨在通过器件结构优化与模型分析，实现更高电流密度和功率处理能力，并探索进一步提升性能的路径。

Method: 采用伪垂直（pseudo-vertical）二极管结构，制作了50微米宽的金刚石肖特基PIN二极管（SPIND）。建立包含热电子发射和空间电荷限制电流的分析模型，并利用Silvaco ATLAS TCAD仿真，通过多单陷阱能级（multiple single trap levels）及其他物理模型来模拟真实器件，以再现实验J-V特性。

Result: 该二极管实现了迄今报道的最高电流密度约116 kA/cm²，总电流约1.3 A，最大功率处理容量1.85 MW/cm²，正向偏压约16 V时比导通电阻（specific on-resistance, Ron,S）低至0.05 mOhm-cm²，电流开关比约6×10¹²，具有优异的整流特性。

Conclusion: 分析模型与ATLAS仿真结果表明，通过降低缺陷密度（defect density）和接触电阻（contact resistance），可进一步改善器件的开启电压（turn-on voltage）和比导通电阻，使器件性能逼近Mott-Gurney空间电荷限制电流机制下的理论极限。

Abstract: A diamond Schottky PIN diode (SPIND) with the highest reported current density to date of ~116 kA/cm2 is demonstrated carrying a total current of ~1.3 A through a 50 micron wide pseudo-vertical diode structure. The diamond SPIND also provides a maximum power handling capacity of 1.85 MW/cm2 and a low specific on-resistance Ron,S of 0.05 mOhm-cm2 at a forward bias of ~16 V. The diamond SPIN diode also shows excellent rectification characteristics with a current on-off ratio of ~6e12. An analytical model including thermionic emission and space charge limited current is presented together with Silvaco ATLAS TCAD simulations, to accurately reproduce the experimental J-V characteristics using multiple single trap levels and other physical models emulating a real device. Theoretical analysis from the analytical models in conjunction with ATLAS simulations shows that further improvement in the device turn on voltage and Ron,S can be achieved by reducing the defect density and contact resistance in order to approach the ultimate performance in the Mott-Gurney space charge limited current regime

</details>


### [59] [Topological Hall effect due to electron-skyrmion scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01149)
*Arijit Mandal,Hareram Swain,B. R. K. Nanda,S. Satpathy*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用Lippmann-Schwinger方程和格林函数形式，研究了从弱耦合到强耦合全范围内电子在手性自旋纹理（如斯格明子（skyrmion））上的散射，发现了Ramsauer-Townsend极小、中间耦合共振以及大缠绕数斯格明子的朗道能级共振等新特征，并揭示了这些特征对拓扑霍尔电导和自旋霍尔电导的显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前关于电子在手性自旋纹理（如斯格明子（skyrmion））上散射的研究大多集中在交换相互作用远小于电子能量的弱耦合（weak-coupling）区域；然而实际材料往往处于定性行为截然不同的强耦合（strong-coupling）区域，因此有必要对所有耦合强度下电子散射的完整物理图像进行系统研究。

Method: 采用Lippmann-Schwinger方程和格林函数（Green's function）形式，该方法对所有耦合强度均有效，从而能够统一描述从弱耦合到强耦合区域的电子散射过程。

Result: 发现了散射截面中的若干新特征：Ramsauer-Townsend极小（Ramsauer-Townsend minima）、显著的中间耦合共振（intermediate-coupling resonances），以及大缠绕数斯格明子的朗道能级共振（Landau-level resonances）。这些特征强烈影响拓扑霍尔电导（topological Hall conductivity）和自旋霍尔电导（spin Hall conductivity），且后者对入射电子能量高度敏感。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解集体手性自旋纹理（如斯格明子晶体（skyrmion crystal））中的霍尔输运提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Electron scattering from chiral spin textures such as skyrmions is fundamental to the understanding of transport in more complex systems, including skyrmion crystals. Most of the previous studies have focused on the weak-coupling regime, where the exchange interaction is small compared with the electron energy. Real materials, however, often lie in the strong-coupling regime, which exhibits qualitatively different behavior. Using the Lippmann-Schwinger equation and Green's function formalism, valid for all coupling strengths, we uncover several new features in the scattering cross section, including Ramsauer-Townsend minima, pronounced intermediate-coupling resonances, and Landau-level resonances for skyrmions with larger winding numbers. These features strongly influence the topological and spin Hall conductivities, which depend sensitively on the incident electron energy. Our work provides important insights into the Hall transport in collective chiral spin textures such as the skyrmion crystal.

### [60] [Electric-field effects on defect migration energetics in GaN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01160)
*Farshid Reza,Hamdy Arkoub,Alexander S. Hauck,Adri C. T. van Duin,Miaomiao Jin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解GaN在运行电场（operating electric fields）下的缺陷输运（defect transport）行为，对于评估高功率和辐射环境中器件的可靠性至关重要。

Method: 基于包含结构、热力学和缺陷特性的密度泛函理论（DFT）训练集，开发了适用于GaN的ReaxFF反应力场（ReaxFF reactive force field）。

Result: 该力场计算的晶格参数、内聚能、缺陷形成能及迁移能等性质与先前的第一性原理和实验结果高度一致。外加电场可显著调控迁移势垒，且变化依赖于缺陷类型和电场取向。电场并非简单地线性偏置缺陷运动，而是通过电荷-晶格耦合（charge-lattice coupling）各向异性地改变迁移势垒，产生非线性输运行为。

Conclusion: 电场可通过诱导部分电荷重分布和局域晶格畸变，复杂地改变缺陷迁移的势垒分布，为理解GaN在高场条件下的缺陷输运提供了新见解。

Abstract: A predictive understanding of defect transport in GaN under operating electric fields is critical for assessing device reliability in high-power and radiation environments. In this work, a ReaxFF reactive force field for GaN is developed using a density-functional-theory training set that includes structural, thermodynamic, and defect properties. The force field yields various properties such as lattice parameters, cohesive energies, and defect formation and migration energies in close agreement with prior first-principles and experimental results. Under externally applied electric fields, we find that migration barriers can be strongly modulated, with changes that depend on defect type and field orientation. Notably, the electric fields do not simply linearly bias defect motion in GaN, but can anisotropically modify migration barriers through charge-lattice coupling, leading to nonlinear transport behavior. The response arises from field-induced partial charge redistribution and local lattice distortion. These results demonstrate that electric fields can complexly modify the defect migration landscape, providing new insight into defect transport in GaN under high-field conditions.

### [61] [Observation of Flat Bands in Type-II Weyl Semimetal TaRhTe$_{4}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01186)
*Harry Rankin,Tyler J. Slade,Benjamin Schrunk,Yevhen Kushnirenko,Andrew Eaton,K. U. R. R. S. Rathnayaka,Maxwell Doyle,Lin-Lin Wang,Paul C. Canfield,Adam Kaminski*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究报告在非中心对称的范德华II型外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal）TaRhTe₄中发现了化学势附近的平带（flat bands），这一发现未经密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）预测，为研究非平庸拓扑与平带共存提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平带长期以来仅理论预言，近期虽在魔角扭曲双层石墨烯、笼目（kagome）晶格等体系中实现，但唯有扭曲层状材料能调控平带至电子化学势附近以影响输运和热力学性质。本文旨在探索非磁性块体体系中是否存在化学势附近的平带。

Method: 采用角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）对非中心对称范德华II型外尔半金属TaRhTe₄进行实验测量。

Conclusion: TaRhTe₄提供了一个非平庸拓扑与费米能级附近平带共存的平台，扩展了平带物理的研究体系，尤其在非磁性块体外尔半金属中。

Abstract: Flat bands have been theoretically predicted for decades but have only recently been realized in quantum materials such as magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene, kagome and Lieb lattices, and rare-earth metal compounds. To date, only twisted layered materials have enabled tuning of flat-band energies near the electronic chemical potential, thereby influencing transport and thermodynamic properties. Here, we report the presence of flat bands near the chemical potential in bulk TaRhTe$_{4}$, a noncentrosymmetric van-der Waals type-II Weyl semimetal. Flat bands are rarely observed in Weyl semimetals, particularly in nonmagnetic bulk systems, and the observed flat bands were not predicted by density functional theory calculations. TaRhTe$_{4}$ therefore provides a platform in which nontrivial topology coexists with flat bands near the Fermi level, as evidenced by our angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy measurements.

### [62] [Synchronization and Swarming of Two-Mode Stochastic Oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00179)
*Szabolcs Vitus,Ferenc Járai-Szabó*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过一个同时具有空间移动性和内部双模随机振荡状态的智能体模型，研究了空间构型与内部状态之间的双向反馈如何驱动复杂集体动力学，发现了七种形态构型并揭示了离散的、量子化的拓扑吸引子，推导了标志自发手征对称性破缺的宏观标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同步（synchronization）与集群（swarming）是自组织（self-organization）的标志性表现，但现有研究较少同时考虑个体的空间移动性与内部随机振荡状态之间的耦合。本文旨在建立一种双向反馈机制，探索空间构型与内部状态跃迁共演化所形成的集体动力学。

Method: 构建了一种新颖的基于智能体（agent-based model）的模型，每个智能体既具有空间移动性，又具有内部的双模随机振荡状态。引入局部、依赖于距离的耦合，连接智能体的空间构型与其内部状态跃迁，形成双向反馈回路。通过大规模数值模拟，对旋转能（rotational energy）和径向弥散（radial dispersion）进行定量分析。

Result: 识别出七种不同的形态构型，从静止的Filled-disk状态到高度无序的Intense-motion状态。系统组织成离散的、量子化的拓扑吸引子（quantized topological attractors）。推导出宏观标度律Ω∝r^{-1/2}，证明旋转态并非刚体旋转，而是由自发手征对称性破缺（spontaneous chiral symmetry breaking）驱动的复合差分涡旋结构（composite differential vortex structures）。

Conclusion: 这些稳定的、量子化的动力学状态是受双向空间-相位反馈（bidirectional spatial-phase feedback）支配的系统的基本特征，为设计自主、去中心化的机器人集群（robotic swarms）提供了稳健的理论框架。

Abstract: Synchronization and swarming are canonical manifestations of self-organization, observable across scales from cellular processes to animal flocks. This study investigates the collective dynamics of a novel agent-based model where individuals exhibit both spatial mobility and internal, two-mode stochastic oscillatory states. By introducing a local, distance-dependent coupling between the agents' spatial configuration and their internal state transitions, we establish a mutual feedback loop that drives complex pattern formation. Through large-scale numerical simulations, we identify seven distinct morphological configurations, ranging from stationary \textit{Filled-disk} states to highly disordered \textit{Intense-motion} regimes. By performing a rigorous quantitative analysis of the rotational energy and radial dispersion, we transcend simple morphological classification and demonstrate that the system organizes into discrete, quantized topological attractors. We derive a macroscopic scaling law, $Ω\propto r^{-1/2}$, which proves that the emerging rotating states are not rigid-body rotations, but rather composite differential vortex structures characterized by spontaneous chiral symmetry breaking. Our results suggest that these stable, quantized dynamical states are fundamental features of systems governed by bidirectional spatial-phase feedback, offering a robust framework for designing autonomous, decentralized robotic swarms.

### [63] [On the Application of Poincare-Steklov Operators to the Problem of Resonant Scattering in a Cylinder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00656)

Method: 将问题转化为内边界值问题，利用庞加莱-斯捷克洛夫算子（Poincare-Steklov operator）定义边界条件，并通过分析相应的谱问题来研究共振散射频率。

Result: 在两根势垒间区域发生足够任意的形变时，波导中散射的共振特性成立；共振散射频率由谱问题的特征值（eigenvalue）给出。

Conclusion: 共振散射在波导结构形变下具有鲁棒性，谱方法可有效确定共振频率。

Abstract: The resonant nature of scattering in a waveguide with two barriers is proven in the case of a sufficiently arbitrary deformation of the region between the barriers. The problem is considered as an interior boundary value problem with boundary conditions defined by a Poincare-Steklov operator. A spectral problem is considered whose eigenvalue determines the resonant scattering frequency.

Conclusion: 同号涡旋系统的长时间平均涡旋密度具有径向对称性，该结论对于N=3得到严格证明，对于更多涡旋的情形则提出了合理的理论动机。

Abstract: We consider the vortex model on the plane, focusing on the case of vortices with the same sign and, for simplicity, assuming all vortices possess equal circulation.   We conjecture that, for a.e. initial data, the time average of the empirical density is radial.
  We prove the result for N=3 vortices by exploiting the integrability of the system.
  For N > 3 vortices we motivate the conjecture by transforming the problem into the independence of ergodic stroboscopic averages from initial data along a single trajectory, when using a suitable rotation angle as the independent variable instead of the time variable.

### [65] [On the spherical symmetry and finite-range assumptions of the interaction potential in the low energy study of dilute Bose gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00859)
*Lukas Reichmann,Arnaud Triay*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文考虑三维环面上处于格罗斯-皮塔耶夫斯基（Gross–Pitaevskii）区域中的玻色气体，论证如何去除相互作用势的径向性和紧支撑假设，从而推广玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose–Einstein condensation）的证明以及激发谱（excitation spectrum）收敛到博戈留波夫（Bogoliubov）预测的结果，并概述了文献[50]的证明思路。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在三维环面（three-dimensional torus）上的格罗斯-皮塔耶夫斯基区域中分析玻色气体，通过去除对相互作用势的径向性和紧支撑假设来推广已有证明，并概述文献[50]的证明框架。

Result: 成功移除了相互作用势的径向性和紧支撑假设，使玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚及激发谱收敛到博戈留波夫预测的结果在更一般的势函数下成立。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了玻色气体在格罗斯-皮塔耶夫斯基区域中相关理论结果的适用范围，表明凝聚和激发谱的博戈留波夫描述对更一般的相互作用势仍然有效。

Abstract: We consider a Bose gas on the three-dimensional torus in the Gross--Pitaevskii regime and explain how to remove the assumptions of radiality and compact support on the interaction potential in the proof of Bose--Einstein condensation and convergence of the excitation spectrum to Bogoliubov's prediction. In particular, we sketch the proof of [50].

</details>


### [66] [Scattering, Trapping and Cloaking-Type Effects of Plane Waves by Point Scatterers in Strain Gradient Elasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01070)
*E. Alevras,Th. Zisis,P. A. Gourgiotis*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了嵌入无限大应变梯度弹性介质中刚性点约束簇对时谐P波和SV波的平面应变散射问题，推导了封闭形式的动态格林张量（dynamic Green's tensor），并通过频率域方法识别共振放大与波俘获（wave trapping）现象，揭示了微观惯性长度与应变梯度长度之比对散射响应的主导作用，以及在反常色散与正常色散区间下截然不同的共振与屏蔽行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微结构固体中局域约束引起的波散射受材料长度尺度、色散与几何构型的强烈耦合影响。现有经典弹性动力学框架无法处理点约束的直接引入，亟需一种能容纳应变梯度效应并实现多散射（multiple-scattering）建模的理论方法。

Method: 基于应变梯度弹性理论（strain gradient elasticity），推导了平面应变问题的封闭形式动态格林张量；利用该张量在源点有界的特性，通过基本解叠加直接引入刚性点约束，将多散射问题约化为关于销钉反力振幅的有限维代数方程组；采用频率域分析方法，利用格林矩阵行列式局部极小值识别候选共振频率，并通过高阶曲率判据区分俘获主导共振与非局域散射响应。

Result: 响应主要由微观惯性长度与应变梯度能量长度之比决定。在反常色散（anomalous dispersion）区间，尖锐共振产生强位移局域化，包括密集圆形阵列中的周界局域俘获模式（perimeter-localized trapping modes）；在正常色散（normal dispersion）区间，共振被强烈衰减，销钉表现为弱散射体，产生近乎无扰动的隐身型响应（cloaking-type response）。泊松比、入射角及复合销钉构型的影响也被系统考察。

Conclusion: 通过调节内在材料长度与几何布局，可在微结构弹性介质中实现可调控的散射、俘获与波屏蔽机制，为应变梯度框架下的弹性波操控提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Wave scattering by localized constraints in microstructured solids is strongly influenced by the interplay of material length scales, dispersion and geometry. This work investigates plane-strain scattering of time-harmonic P and SV waves by clusters of rigid point constraints embedded in an infinite strain gradient elastic medium. A closed-form dynamic Green's tensor is derived for the plane-strain problem. Unlike the classical elastodynamic Green's tensor, the strain gradient Green's tensor remains bounded at the source, enabling point constraints to be introduced directly through superposition of fundamental solutions. The multiple-scattering problem is reduced to a finite-dimensional algebraic system for the pin reaction amplitudes. A frequency-domain procedure is developed to identify resonance-like amplification and trapping. Candidate resonant frequencies are associated with local minima of the Green matrix determinant, while higher-order curvature criteria distinguish trapping-dominated resonances from non-localized scattering responses. The results show that the response is governed primarily by the ratio of the microinertial and energetic strain gradient lengths. In the anomalous dispersion regime, sharp resonances produce strong displacement localization, including perimeter-localized trapping modes in dense circular arrays. In the normal dispersion regime, these resonances are strongly attenuated and the pins behave as weak scatterers, producing a cloaking-type response in which the incident field is only weakly perturbed. The influence of Poisson's ratio, incidence angle and compound pin configurations is also examined, demonstrating how intrinsic material lengths and geometric arrangement can be used to tune scattering, trapping and wave-screening mechanisms in microstructured elastic media.

</details>


### [67] [A scheme for topological phases of the Weyl $C^*$-algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01183)
*Giuseppe De Nittis,Santiago G. Rendel*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有拓扑相分类主要依赖K-理论（K-theory）等代数工具，论文旨在从纯态空间（pure state space）的拓扑视角出发，建立一种更本质的分类框架。

Method: 基于模型C*-代数（model $C^*$-algebra）的纯态空间拓扑，引入分类方案；将拓扑相描述为某些态纤维丛（fiber bundles of states）截面的同伦类（homotopy classes）。

Result: 将该分类程序应用于晶格平移不变的Weyl C*-代数（Weyl $C^*$-algebra）的态，恢复了A型和AI型拓扑绝缘体（topological insulators）有能隙谱投影子（gapped spectral projectors）的K-理论分类。

Conclusion: 该工作本质上推广了拓扑绝缘体中基于K-理论的分类概念，提供了从纯态空间拓扑出发的统一分类视角。

Abstract: In this work, we introduce a classification scheme for topological phases of matter based on the topology of the space of pure states of a model $C^*$-algebra. Under it, topological phases are described by homotopy classes of sections of certain fiber bundles of (pure) states. Applying this classification procedure on states of the Weyl $C^*$-algebra that are invariant under translations by a lattice, we recover the $K$-theoretic classification of gapped spectral projectors for topological insulators of types A and AI, thus essentially generalizing this notion.

### [68] [Demographic senescence as multi-level selection in miniature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00262)
*Ananda Shikhara Bhat,Hanna Kokko*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 本文证明，生物衰老（senescence）所产生的紧急死亡率模式可被理解为多层选择（multi-level selection）的产物。通过构建两层莫兰过程（two-level Moran type process）并利用其缩放极限（scaling limits），研究展示了描述群体结构中多层选择的数学框架同样能刻画衰老生物体内的损伤积累模式及由此产生的死亡率曲线。文章通过类比搭便车者与受损子系统的动态过程，论证了衰老模式与世代内多层选择过程在形式上是等价的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多层选择与衰老（senescence）两个领域初看缺乏共同点，本文旨在揭示二者之间的深层数学联系，证明衰老产生的紧急死亡率模式可以通过多层选择框架来理解。

Method: 研究构建了一个两层莫兰过程（two-level Moran type process），并通过其缩放极限（scaling limits）进行分析，将多层选择框架与衰老过程中的损伤积累和死亡率曲线在数学上统一起来。

Result: 研究发现，衰老生物体中的紧急衰老模式与世代内（within-generation）多层选择过程产生的模式在形式上是等价的：生物体内子系统扮演粒子（particles）的角色，生物体扮演集体（collectives）的角色，选择性消失（selective disappearance）扮演群体选择（group selection）的角色。

Conclusion: 复杂整合生物体中的衰老模式可被理解为多层选择过程的产物，其中损伤积累与搭便车者扩散的动力学在数学上具有同构性。

Abstract: Multi-level selection and senescence do not at first sight have much in common. Here, we demonstrate that the emergent mortality patterns generated by demographic senescence can be understood as the product of multi-level selection. We formulate a two-level Moran type process and use its scaling limits to illustrate that a simple mathematical framework that models multi-level selection in group-structured populations also models damage accumulation patterns and resultant mortality curves in ageing organisms. To verbally make the connection, observe that defectors spread within a group consisting of cooperators and defectors; when groups compete against each other, defector-rich groups suffer, and between-group selection causes such groups to be systematically under-represented. Exactly analogously, senescing individuals accumulate damage to physiological sub-systems, and `damage begets damage'; individuals who are more damaged are more likely to die, hence damage-rich individuals are systematically under-represented in later age classes. Thus, emergent senescence patterns in complex, integrated organisms are formally equivalent to the patterns generated by a within-generation multi-level selection process in which intra-organismal sub-systems play the role of particles, organisms play the role of collectives, and selective disappearance plays the role of group selection.

</details>

### [69] [Weak and dissipative solutions for the Hasegawa-Mima equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01119)
*Michele Gorini*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对Hasegawa-Mima方程的“类欧拉”速度形式，借鉴Lions关于欧拉方程的经典方法，证明了在二维环面或有界光滑区域上，对任意L²无散初值均存在耗散解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hasegawa-Mima方程是描述等离子体漂移波湍流（drift wave turbulence）的核心模型，但其在“类欧拉”速度形式下的弱解存在性问题尚未得到严格处理，尤其缺乏对任意L²初值耗散解存在性的证明。

Method: 将Hasegawa-Mima方程改写为类似于欧拉方程（Euler equations）的“类欧拉”速度形式，并借鉴Lions关于欧拉方程处理耗散解（dissipative solutions）的框架，通过适当的函数空间设定和弱解定义进行理论证明。

Result: 证明了在二维环面（𝕋²）或有界𝒞¹区域（D⊂ℝ²）上，对任意L²无散初值（divergence free initial condition）w∈L²(D)，Hasegawa-Mima方程的“类欧拉”速度形式均存在耗散解。

Conclusion: 该结果为Hasegawa-Mima方程在更宽泛的初值条件下提供了解的存在性保证，拓展了该方程弱解理论的基础，并为进一步研究湍流状态下的解行为提供了数学依据。

Abstract: We consider the Hasegawa-Mima equation in its ``Euler-like'' velocity form: \[\partial_t(u-Δ^{-1}u)+(u\cdot\nabla)u-u^\perp\log n_0=0,\] $n_0$ being the time-independent function appearing in the particle count $n=n_0e^{\frac{e\varphi}{T}}$, and $u$ being the drift velocity $\nabla^\perp\varphi=-\nabla\varphi\times\hat z$. Adapting the notion from Lions' book on the Euler equations, we prove the existence of dissipative solutions for this equation for any $L^2$ divergence free initial condition $w\in L^2(D)$, for $D=\mathbb T^2$ and $D\subset\mathbb R^2$ a bounded $\mathcal{C}^1$ domain.

</details>

### [70] [Dependence of charge separation efficiency on the exciton-charge transfer offset and Gaussian disorder in organic solar cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00699)
*Maik Schwuchow,Carsten Deibel,Angela Thränhardt*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过比较宏观两态速率模型与三维动力学蒙特卡洛（kMC）模拟，研究了低偏移有机太阳能电池中激子-CT态杂交、简并度比及高斯无序对电荷分离动力学的影响，发现无序在中小能量偏移下可显著提升效率，甚至在零或负偏移下通过有效驱动力实现电荷分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿有机太阳能电池（organic solar cells）日益依赖低能量偏移（low-offset）的半导体共混体系，挑战了传统上认为高效电荷分离需要大能量驱动力（energetic driving force）的观点。该体系中局域激子（local exciton, LE）与电荷转移态（charge-transfer state, CT）之间的能量偏移 $ΔE_{\mathrm{LE-CT}}$ 已接近热能，使得激子-CT杂交（exciton-CT hybridization）和激子能级的热再占据（thermal repopulation）成为影响器件性能的关键因素，亟需深入研究其微观机制。

Method: 本文直接比较了两种建模方法：一个宏观的两态速率模型（two-state rate model）与一个三维动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte-Carlo, kMC）模拟。通过这两种方法系统地对比了在不同 $ΔE_{\mathrm{LE-CT}}$ 范围以及有无高斯能量无序（Gaussian energetic disorder）条件下的电荷分离微观动力学。

Result: 在无无序条件下，解析速率模型在整个 $ΔE_{\mathrm{LE-CT}}$ 范围内均能准确复现kMC预测；宏观模型成功解释了内量子效率（internal quantum efficiency, IQE）曲线中源于能量偏移物理实现方式的水平偏移，且这些变化可完全由LE与CT态的简并度比（ratio of degeneracies）描述。引入高斯无序后，kMC模拟显示出依赖于 $ΔE_{\mathrm{LE-CT}}$ 的明确交叉行为：大偏移下无序主要起负面作用，而在中等和低偏移下无序能显著提升效率。载流子在无序展宽态密度（disorder-broadened density of states）中的热化（thermalization）创造了有效驱动力，使电荷分离在零或负偏移下仍能发生。

Conclusion: 宏观两态速率模型在忽略无序时能有效描述低偏移有机太阳能电池的电荷分离行为，而实际体系中高斯能量无序的存在能通过提供有效驱动力，在中小能量偏移条件下显著提升电荷分离效率，突破了传统大驱动力要求的理论限制。

Abstract: State-of-the-art organic solar cells increasingly rely on low-offset semiconductor blends, challenging the traditional requirement of a large energetic driving force for efficient charge separation. In these systems, the energetic offset $ΔE_{\mathrm{LE-CT}}$ between local exciton (LE) and charge-transfer (CT) states approaches the thermal energy, making exciton-CT hybridization and thermal repopulation of the exciton level critical to device performance. In this work, we directly compare a macroscopic two-state rate model with three-dimensional kinetic Monte-Carlo (kMC) simulations to investigate microscopic charge separation dynamics and the role of Gaussian energetic disorder. We demonstrate that in the absence of disorder, the analytical rate model accurately reproduces kMC predictions for the whole range of $ΔE_{\mathrm{LE-CT}}$. Specifically, the macroscopic model successfully explains horizontal shifts in the internal quantum efficiency curves that arise depending on how the energetic offset is physically realized in the constituent molecules. We show that these variations can be captured entirely through the ratio of degeneracies of the LE and CT states, respectively. Introducing Gaussian energetic disorder into the kMC simulation reveals a distinct crossover behavior depending on $ΔE_{\mathrm{LE-CT}}$. While disorder is mostly detrimental at large offsets, it can significantly boost efficiency at intermediate and low offsets. Thermalization of charge carriers within the disorder-broadened density of states creates an effective driving force allowing charge separation even at zero or negative energetic offsets.

</details>


### [71] [Non-self-averaging topological Anderson insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00892)
*Zheng-Wei Zuo,Jun-Chong Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文发现长程关联无序（long-range correlated disorder）能够诱导拓扑安德森绝缘体（topological Anderson insulator）进入一种非自平均（non-self-averaging）统计相。在该相中，李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）的相对方差在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下不为零，其分布偏离高斯分布（Gaussian distribution），导致中心极限定理（central limit theorem）失效，单个无序样本的拓扑性质偏离系综平均（ensemble average）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对无序拓扑量子相的研究主要集中于非关联或短程关联（short-range correlated）无序区域，这些拓扑安德森绝缘体通常是自平均（self-averaging）的。然而，长程关联无序对拓扑量子态的影响更为复杂，且由于缺乏可处理的解析方法，该领域受到的关注十分有限。

Method: 通过分析李雅普诺夫指数在热力学极限下的相对方差（relative variance）是否趋于零，判断系统是否具有自平均性；同时考察李雅普诺夫指数的分布是否呈高斯分布（Gaussian distribution），以判定系统的统计行为是否偏离中心极限定理（central limit theorem）。

Result: 长程关联无序可以诱导拓扑安德森态进入非自平均拓扑安德森绝缘体相。该相的特征表现为：李雅普诺夫指数的相对方差在热力学极限下保持非零有限值，且其分布呈现非高斯分布（non-Gaussian distribution）。

Conclusion: 非自平均拓扑安德森绝缘体揭示了关联无序（correlated disorder）与拓扑（topology）之间的相互作用，为理解复杂无序环境下的拓扑量子系统提供了新视角。

Abstract: Current research on the disordered topological quantum phases primarily focuses on the uncorrelated and short-range correlated disorder regime. These topological Anderson insulators are typically self-averaging. However, topological quantum systems with long-range correlated disorder have received limited attention due to the absence of tractable analytical methods. In fact, the long-range correlated disorder introduces more complex effects on topological quantum states. Here, we demonstrate that the long-range correlated disorder could induce anomalously statistical feature where the topological Anderson states become non-self-averaging, and the phase diagram is strongly dependent on individual disorder configurations. We term this statistical phase the non-self-averaging topological Anderson insulator. The non-self-averaging property is identified by the non-vanishing finite values of the relative variance of the Lyapunov exponent in the thermodynamic limit, alongside the non-Gaussian distributions of the Lyapunov exponent. Consequently, the topological properties of a single disordered sample deviate from the ensemble average, causing a breakdown of the central limit theorem. The non-self-averaging topological Anderson insulator provides insights into the interplay between correlated disorder and topology.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 综述了三种特定产生与衰变案例：(1) 重型标量粒子X共振产生后衰变为一个希格斯玻色子和一个更轻的标量粒子S；(2) 重型中性希格斯玻色子衰变为另一个中性希格斯玻色子和Z玻色子；(3) 重型带电希格斯玻色子产生后衰变为另一个中性希格斯玻色子和W玻色子。所回顾的搜寻基于LHC Run-2完整数据集及部分Run-3数据集。

Abstract: The search for new particles, conducted at the LHC by the ATLAS and CMS collaborations, covers several production and decay modes, leading to a large variety of final states that could be observed in both detectors. This review focuses on the production of new heavy scalars that have a Higgs boson in the final state. Three cases are covered: resonant production of a heavy scalar $X$ decaying into a Higgs boson and a lighter scalar $S$, heavy neutral Higgs boson decaying into another neutral Higgs boson and a $Z$ boson, and a heavy charged Higgs boson production with subsequent decay into another neutral Higgs boson and a $W$ boson. The reviewed searches are based on the complete LHC Run-2 dataset and partial Run-3 dataset.

### [73] [GPU-accelerated spectrum reweighting for new-physics searches in solar neutrino--electron scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00488)
*Guangbao Sun,Xuefeng Ding,Liang Sun,Xiang Zhou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于GPU加速的谱重加权框架，用于中微子-电子弹性散射实验中的新物理参数扫描。该框架通过避免为每个参数点重新生成探测器蒙特卡洛样本，将每个似然评估的耗时降低至毫秒级，在特定硬件上实现了相比单CPU线程58倍的加速比，使得在单台工作站上即可进行交互式参数扫描。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子-电子弹性散射的精密测量为检验弱相互作用和超越标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理提供了低能窗口，例如非标准相互作用（non-standard interactions, NSIs）和反常中微子磁矩（anomalous neutrino magnetic moment）均会修改微分散射截面。然而，当每个新物理参数点的反冲谱都需要通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo, MC）模拟来传播探测器响应时，似然检验的计算成本极其高昂，严重限制了参数扫描的效率。

Method: 提出了一种基于GPU加速的谱重加权（spectrum-reweighting）框架。该框架将箱到箱权重（bin-to-bin weights）应用于反冲谱（recoil-spectrum）层面，再与一个固定的二维响应模型（response model）折叠，该模型包含反冲能量与重建能量两个维度。探测器响应被保留在似然计算内部，而每个参数更新仅需对预计算的谱和响应核（response kernels）进行操作。实现采用NVIDIA Thrust的变换-归约原语（transformation–reduction primitives），并通过统一源码编译支持CUDA和OpenMP后端。

Result: 在基准测试中，单次似然评估在NVIDIA RTX 3080Ti上耗时约87毫秒，在NVIDIA A30X上耗时约52毫秒。A30X相较单CPU线程实现了58倍加速，相较满载64线程CPU实现了约2.5倍加速。主要加速来源于避免为每个参数点重新生成探测器MC样本，而非仅依赖GPU执行本身。

Conclusion: 该框架适用于中微子-电子散射分析中，新物理依赖可以通过重加权现有反冲谱来表征的场景，包括本文研究的味NSI和磁矩情况。消费级GPU的结果表明，在单台工作站上即可实现交互式参数扫描。

Abstract: Precision measurements of neutrino--electron elastic scattering provide low-energy tests of weak interactions and beyond-the-Standard-Model effects. Non-standard interactions (NSIs) and an anomalous neutrino magnetic moment modify the differential cross section through different kinematic terms, but both can alter the normalization and shape of the recoil-electron spectrum. Likelihood tests are computationally costly when each parameter point requires the recoil spectrum to be propagated through a detector response obtained from Monte Carlo (MC) simulation. We present a GPU-accelerated spectrum-reweighting framework that avoids regenerating detector MC samples for each new-physics parameter point. Bin-to-bin weights are applied at the recoil-spectrum level and folded with a fixed two-dimensional response model in recoil and reconstructed energy. This keeps the detector response inside the likelihood calculation while reducing each parameter update to operations on precomputed spectra and response kernels. The implementation uses NVIDIA Thrust transformation--reduction primitives and is compiled from a common source for CUDA and OpenMP back ends. In the benchmarks considered here, one likelihood evaluation takes ${\sim}87$ ms on an NVIDIA RTX 3080Ti and ${\sim}52$ ms on an NVIDIA A30X; the latter gives a $58\times$ speedup over a single CPU thread and ${\sim}2.5\times$ over a fully loaded 64-thread CPU. The consumer-GPU result demonstrates that interactive parameter scans are feasible on a single workstation. The main acceleration, however, comes from avoiding detector-MC regeneration at each parameter point rather than from GPU execution alone. The framework applies to neutrino--electron scattering analyses in which the new-physics dependence can be represented by reweighting an existing recoil spectrum, including flavor NSI and magnetic-moment cases studied here.

</details>


### [74] [Modeling Falling Backgrounds with Exponential Mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00884)
*Austin Townsend,Marc Osherson,Mike Hildreth,Stefano Castruccio*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出将有限指数混合模型（finite exponential mixture）作为一种灵活的半参数函数类，用于近似大型强子对撞机（LHC）新物理搜索中平滑下降的背景分布；基于极值理论（extreme value theory）的推导和两个数据集（n=28,619,185 和 n=5,036）的实证表明，该方法在大小数据集上性能与现有方法相当，且在模拟研究中偏差小、覆盖概率一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHC的新物理搜索常需在平滑下降的背景分布上寻找局部过量信号；现有的多项式等参数化背景模型在处理不断增长的数据集时需要大量针对特定分析（analysis-specific）的开发工作，因此亟需一种更加灵活且通用的背景建模方法。

Method: 基于极值理论（extreme value theory）的结论，提出有限指数混合（finite exponential mixture）作为半参数（semi-parametric）函数类来近似下降分布（falling distributions）；在两个公开数据集（n=28,619,185 和 n=5,036）上进行性能比较，并在模拟研究（n=5,036）中评估偏差和覆盖概率。

Result: 有限指数混合模型在大小两个数据集上的表现均与现有方法相当；在模拟研究中，该模型相对于真实统计不确定性（statistical uncertainty）表现出较小的偏差，并在主体区域（bulk）保持一致的标称覆盖概率（nominal coverage）。

Conclusion: 有限指数混合模型作为一种灵活的半参数背景建模方案，在LHC新物理搜索场景中具有可行性，能够在保持统计性能的同时减少针对特定分析的手动调参需求。

Abstract: Searches for new physics at the LHC often look for localized excesses on smoothly falling background distributions. Several classes of background models have been considered, including polynomials and other parametric families; however, these approaches can require extensive analysis-specific development as datasets grow. In this work, we motivate the finite exponential mixture as a flexible semi-parametric class of functions for approximating falling distributions, drawing on results from extreme value theory. Using two published datasets ($n=28,619,185$ and $n=5,036$), we show that the exponential mixture performance is comparable to existing methods for both small and large datasets. Finally, in simulation studies ($n = 5,036$), we find that the finite exponential mixture exhibits small bias relative to the true statistical uncertainty while maintaining consistent nominal coverage in the bulk.

</details>

### [75] [Putting Jet Substructure on Track(s)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00087)
*Kyle Lee,Ian Moult,Wouter J. Waalewijn*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用因子化定理（factorization theorems）和重整化群（renormalization group）技术，首次实现了大型强子对撞机（LHC）上基于径迹的喷注内部结构可观测量（jet substructure observables on tracks）的完整计算，将投影能量关联子（projected energy correlators）推进到四点、次领头共线对数（next-to-leading collinear logarithmic）精度，为实验与理论的高精度比较提供了系统可改进的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 喷注内部结构（jet substructure）是LHC分析策略的重要进展，但现有计算主要基于能量沉积，缺乏足够的角分辨率来测量日益精细的关联。利用径迹信息（tracking information）可以提供卓越的角分辨率，然而此前缺乏基于径迹的喷注内部结构观测量的完整理论计算。

Method: 基于因子化定理和重整化群技术，对投影能量关联子进行理论计算；具体计算了从两点到四点的投影能量关联子，并达到次领头共线对数精度。

Result: 首次完成了LHC上基于径迹的喷注内部结构观测量的完整计算，投影能量关联子达到当前喷注内部结构领域的最先进精度水平（state of the art），但扩展到了径迹情形。

Conclusion: 该工作显著推进了强子对撞机物理项目，使得实验测量与理论计算之间能够进行精确且系统可改进的比较，这得益于径迹测量提供的卓越角分辨率。

Abstract: One of the main advances in analysis strategies at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) has been the ability to study the detailed structure of energy flow within high transverse momentum jets, a field referred to as jet substructure. Jet substructure has provided new ways to search for new physics, measure Standard Model parameters, and study the dynamics of the strong nuclear force. To push to the next level of precision, and to make measurements of increasingly subtle correlations, requires exquisite angular resolution achieved through the use of tracking information. In this paper we leverage recent progress in our understanding of factorization theorems and renormalization group techniques to present the first complete calculations of jet substructure observables at the LHC on tracks. We compute projected energy correlators up to four points at next-to-leading collinear logarithmic accuracy, matching the state of the art for jet substructure observables, but extending to tracks. This marks a significant step in enhancing the collider physics program, enabling precise and systematically improvable comparisons between experimental measurements and theoretical calculations, made possible by the exceptional angular resolution of tracking.

### [76] [Classifying the hidden-charm pentaquarks via a flavor mixing scheme](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00411)
*Kan Chen,Bo Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于轻自由度味成分（flavor components of light degrees of freedom）对由基态单粲重子（single-charm baryons）与反D/D_s介子（$\bar{D}^{(*)}/\bar{D}_s^{(*)}$ mesons）构成的分子态进行分类的方案，并利用该框架统一解释了实验观测到的$P_c$和$P_{cs}$态，同时预言了单奇异和双奇异隐粲（hidden-charm）束缚态的存在及其质量谱。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 所有考虑的量子-介子系统按照其轻自由度的味成分进行分类。对于单奇异系统，吸引相互作用来源于$Σ_c^{(*)}\bar{D}_s^{(*)}$与$Ξ_c^{\prime(*)}\bar{D}^{(*)}$之间的道混合（channel mixing）；对于双奇异系统，吸引来源于$Ξ_c^{\prime(*)}\bar{D}_s^{(*)}$与$Ω_c^{(*)}\bar{D}^{(*)}$之间的道混合。利用从实验测得的$P_c$和$P_{cs}$态拟合出的参数，系统计算了这些束缚态的质量谱。

Result: 该分类方案能够一致地解释实验上观测到的$P_c$和$P_{cs}$态。基于该框架，还预言了单奇异和双奇异隐粲束缚态的存在，并给出了其质量谱的系统性预测结果。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于轻自由度味成分的分类框架为理解粲重子-介子分子态提供了统一视角，不仅能够解释现有实验数据，还能预测新的奇异隐粲束缚态，为未来实验搜索提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this work, we propose a scheme to classify the molecular states consisting of ground single-charm baryons ($Λ_c$, $Ξ_c$, $Σ_c^{(*)}$, $Ξ_c^{\prime(*)}$, $Ω_c^{(*)}$) and $\bar{D}^{(*)}/\bar{D}_s^{(*)}$ mesons. Within this framework, all considered baryon-meson systems are categorized according to the flavor components of their light degrees of freedom. We briefly illustrate how this classification scheme can consistently explain the experimentally observed $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$ states. This framework also predicts the existences of single-strange and double-strange hidden-charm bound states. The attractive interactions of these states arise from channel mixing between $Σ_c^{(*)}\bar{D}_s^{(*)}$ and $Ξ_c^{\prime(*)}\bar{D}^{(*)}$ for single-strange systems, and mixing between $Ξ_c^{\prime(*)}\bar{D}_s^{(*)}$ and $Ω_c^{(*)}\bar{D}^{(*)}$ for double-strange systems, respectively. Using parameters fitted from the measured $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$ states, we systematically present the predicted mass spectra for these single- and double-strange hidden-charm bound states.

### [77] [The Negative-$Σ\barΣ$ Angular-Parameter Puzzle in $J/ψ$ and $ψ(2S)$ Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00590)
*Chao-Qiang Geng,Xiang-Nan Jin,Chia-Wei Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 通过分析J/ψ和ψ(2S)衰变到重子八重态对的实验数据，发现Σ\barΣ通道的角分布参数为负（α_Σ^{J/ψ}<0），与其他通道形成对比。研究表明，SU(3)_F精确单态描述严重失败（χ²≈10⁴），而引入共同末态相互作用（final-state interaction）混合S波和D波振幅、并加入对称SU(3)_F破缺八重态的拟合则效果极佳（χ²=4.43），将负的Σ角参数归因于共同末态再散射对磁形状因子的压制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验测量发现J/ψ衰变到八重态重子对（octet baryon pairs）时，Σ\barΣ通道的角分布参数α_Σ^{J/ψ}为负，而其他J/ψ八重态通道以及对应的ψ(2S)通道的角参数均为正，这一反常现象（negative-Σ\barΣ puzzle）缺乏理论解释，亟需理解其物理根源。

Method: 首先检验SU(3)_F精确单态描述（SU(3)_F-exact singlet description）的适用性，进行χ²拟合；随后提出一个替代模型，允许共同的末态相互作用（common final-state interaction）混合S波和D波振幅（S- and D-wave amplitudes），并引入对称SU(3)_F破缺八重态（symmetric SU(3)_F-breaking octet）进行拟合对比。

Result: SU(3)_F精确单态描述的χ²拟合结果为χ²≈10⁴，失败明显；而包含共同末态相互作用和SU(3)_F破缺八重态的拟合给出χ²=4.43（标称自由度为2），强烈支持该破缺模式。负的Σ\barΣ角参数被追溯至共同末态再散射（common final-state rescattering）对磁形状因子（magnetic form factor）的压制。

Conclusion: 该负Σ角参数反常现象可通过SU(3)_F破缺和末态相互作用机制得到合理解释，而非单纯的SU(3)_F对称性描述所能涵盖。这一结论为理解重子对衰变中的角分布异常提供了关键的理论线索。

Abstract: Experimental measurements of $J/ψ$ and $ψ(2S)$ decays to octet baryon pairs reveal a negative-$Σ\barΣ$ puzzle in the angular distributions: $α_Σ^{J/ψ}<0$, whereas the other measured $J/ψ$ octet channels and the corresponding $ψ(2S)$ channels have positive angular parameters. We show that an $SU(3)_F$-exact singlet description fails decisively in a $χ^2$ fit, giving $χ^2\simeq10^4$. By contrast, a fit that allows a common final-state interaction to mix the ${\rm S}$- and ${\rm D}$-wave amplitudes, together with a symmetric $SU(3)_F$-breaking octet, gives $χ^2=4.43$ for two nominal degrees of freedom and strongly favors this breaking pattern. The negative $Σ\barΣ$ angular parameter is traced to the suppression of the magnetic form factor by the common final-state rescattering.

</details>
