### [81] [The left-cut for partial waves in terms of physical amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00136)
*Alexandre Salas-Bernárdez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对 2 → 2 散射过程，推导了左手割线（left-hand cut）上分波振幅（partial wave amplitude）的一种新表示，将其表达为右手割线（right-hand cut）虚部的积分，并显式提取了对数支割线（logarithmic branch cut）结构，为系统量化幺正化方法（如逆振幅法或 N/D 方法）中的左手割线不确定性提供了工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强子物理中，幺正化（unitarization）方法（如逆振幅法（Inverse Amplitude Method）或 N/D 方法）常用于处理散射振幅的低能行为，但左手割线（left-hand cut）的不确定性难以系统量化。本文旨在为此提供一个精确且显式的解析工具。

Method: 通过解析推导，将任意同位旋（isospin）和角动量（angular momentum）分波振幅的左手割线表达为右手割线（right-hand cut）虚部的积分形式。该表示显式提取了对数支割线（logarithmic branch cut）结构。

Result: 得到了一种新的、显式的左手割线表示，能够精确提取对数分支割线结构。该表示可用于系统量化逆振幅法或 N/D 方法等幺正化框架中的左手割线不确定性。

Conclusion: 该工作为散射振幅的左手割线不确定性提供了一种系统化的量化工具，有望改进幺正化方法的理论预测精度。

Abstract: We derive a novel representation of the partial wave amplitude over the left-hand cut for $2 \to 2$ scattering. We express the left-hand cut of arbitrary isospin and angular momentum partial waves as an integral of right-hand cut imaginary parts. This formulation provides an explicit, exact extraction of the logarithmic branch cut structures, offering a valuable tool to systematically quantify left-hand cut uncertainties in unitarization methods such as the Inverse Amplitude Method or $N/D$ approaches.

</details>


### [82] [Finite modular Coleman-Weinberg inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00528)
*Yoshihiko Abe,Komei Goto,Tetsutaro Higaki,Junichiro Kawamura,Tatsuo Kobayashi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于模形式耦合Coleman-Weinberg势的模块对称暴胀模型，其中模场的虚部作为暴胀子、实部作为重轴子，该模型能解释当前宇宙学观测，并讨论了再加热及轴子宇宙学后果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建一个基于模形式（modular forms）与Coleman-Weinberg势的模块对称（modular symmetric）暴胀模型，利用模场（modulus field）的虚部作为暴胀子（inflaton）、实部作为重轴子（heavy axion），以同时解释宇宙暴胀、再加热（reheating）及轴子宇宙学，并满足当前观测约束。

Method: 通过积分掉与模场通过模形式耦合的重矢量夸克（heavy vector-like quarks），生成Coleman-Weinberg势，从而构建模块对称暴胀模型。模场τ的虚部扮演暴胀子，实部被识别为重轴子。再加热通过模依赖的规范动能函数（modulus-dependent gauge kinetic functions）实现。

Result: 该模型成功解释了当前宇宙学观测。在可行参数区域内，再加热后轴子振荡主导宇宙能量密度，并在大爆炸核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis, BBN）之前衰变。轴子的量子涨落可达暴胀子量子涨落的约1%，由此引发的等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbations）可能在未来观测中被探测到。

Conclusion: 该模块对称暴胀模型不仅能与现有宇宙学观测自洽，而且轴子动力学及其产生的等曲率扰动为未来实验提供了可检验的预言。

Abstract: We propose a modular symmetric inflationary model based on a Coleman--Weinberg potential generated by integrating out heavy vector-like quarks that couple to the complex modulus field $τ$ through modular forms. In this framework, the imaginary part of modulus $τ$ plays the role of the inflaton, while the real part is identified with a heavy axion. We show that the model successfully explains the current cosmological observations. We further discuss reheating through modulus-dependent gauge kinetic functions and the cosmology of the axion. The axion oscillation dominates over the Universe after the reheating via inflaton decay, and then it decays before Big Bang Nucleosynthesis in the viable parameter region. The quantum fluctuation of the axion can be of order $\mathcal{O}(1)\% $ of that of the inflaton, which would induce isocurvature perturbations that may be detectable in future observations.

### [83] [70 years of Doubly-Logarithmic Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00771)
*B. I. Ermolaev*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文回顾了量子电动力学（QED）中双对数贡献（Double-Logarithmic, DL）的发现历史，介绍了双对数近似（Double-Logarithmic Approximation, DLA）计算框架的构建过程，并概述了DLA在QED、量子色动力学（QCD）及弱电相互作用（EW）理论中对形状因子、散射振幅和深度非弹性散射（DIS）结构函数等对象的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 梳理双对数近似（DLA）的历史发展脉络，并对DLA在多种高能物理过程中的广泛应用进行系统性概述。

Method: 采用历史回顾与文献综述的方法，追溯从Sudakov发现的DL贡献到Gorshkov等人构建DLA计算框架的演进过程。

Result: DLA已成为在QED、QCD和弱电相互作用理论框架下描述各类高能过程的基本方法之一。

Conclusion: DLA可广泛应用于形状因子（form factors）、散射振幅（scattering amplitudes）和深度非弹性散射（DIS）结构函数（structure functions）等对象。

Abstract: Existence of Double-Logarithmic (DL) contributions to scattering amplitudes in QED was discovered by V.V. Sudakov in 1956 and total summation of DL contributions to electron-photon scattering resulted in appearance of famous Sudakov exponentials. Then, thanks to contributions of V.G. Gorshkov, V.N. Gribov, G.V. Frolov and L.N. Lipatov, the pattern of calculations in Double- Logarithmic Approximation (DLA) was constructed. Since then, DLA has become one of basic ways of describing various high-energy processes in the framework of QED, QCD and theory of EW interactions. In the present paper, we remind the history of DLA and present a brief overview of application of DLA to various objects like form factors, scattering amplitudes, DIS structure functions.

### [84] [Gravitating Tubes Beyond World Line Paradigm In General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00036)
*Abhi Savaliya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文针对经典点粒子描述与广义相对论在应力-能量张量光滑性上的冲突（Geroch–Traschen障碍），提出以余维数为零的管状结构（codimension-zero tubes）作为引力物质的基本描述，证明了该模型具有光滑的集体应力-能量张量，在紫外极限下可恢复点粒子作用量，并在微扰稳定性分析中满足一致性约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典点粒子的应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）是分布性的（distributional），集中于一条一维世界线，这种高余维数（higher-codimension）源在爱因斯坦广义相对论中无法获得光滑时空解。Geroch与Traschen已证明该障碍对余维数≥2的源普遍成立。因此，需要一种新的、与广义相对论相容的物质描述方式。

Method: 论文提出余维数为零的管状结构（codimension-zero tubes）作为引力物质的基本描述。在辅助类时曲线（timelike curve）的管状邻域内构造类时管，其内部由类时余维数一超曲面（timelike codimension-one hypersurfaces）分层，超曲面的动力学由膜作用量（brane-like action）控制。

Result: 该模型的集体应力-能量张量是光滑的，区别于点粒子情形。在一大类张力（tension）与势（potential）分布下，管内强能量条件（strong energy condition）被破坏，但零能量条件（null energy condition）与弱能量条件（weak energy condition）仍然满足。在紫外极限（管半径趋于零）下，适当缩放拉格朗日密度后，管作用量退化为点粒子作用量加上一个正则的自力项，粒子的静质量（rest mass）成为有效量而非基本局域参数。场微扰分析显示，分层生成标量场是非动力学的、类似于cuscuton场（cuscuton-like）；叶面微小变形导出类时超曲面汇的Jacobi方程，进一步约束了允许的张力与势分布。

Conclusion: 引力管（gravitating tubes）提供了一种在几何与动力学上一致的物质描述，既尊重Geroch–Traschen障碍的存在，又解决了点粒子描述与广义相对论的不兼容问题。

Abstract: The simplest point-particle description of classical matter is incompatible with Einstein's General Relativity because the stress-energy tensor of a point particle is distributional and concentrated on a one-dimensional worldline. For such higher-codimension sources, smooth spacetime solutions generally do not exist. This obstruction was established by Geroch and Traschen for sources of codimension $\geq2$.
  Motivated by this result, this thesis proposes codimension-zero tubes as a fundamental description of gravitating matter. Timelike tubes are constructed within the tubular neighbourhood of an auxiliary timelike curve. The tube interior is foliated by timelike codimension-one hypersurfaces whose dynamics are governed by a brane-like action. The resulting collective stress-energy tensor is smooth, unlike that of a point particle. For a broad class of tension and potential profiles, the strong energy condition is violated inside the tube, while the null and weak energy conditions remain satisfied. In the ultraviolet limit, where the tube radius vanishes, an appropriate rescaling of the Lagrangian density reduces the tube action to the point-particle action together with a canonical self-force-like term. The particle's rest mass then emerges as an effective quantity rather than a fundamental localized parameter.
  Perturbative stability is analysed at two levels. Field perturbations yield an infinite squared sound speed, showing that the foliation-generating scalar is non-dynamical and cuscuton-like. Small deformations of the leaves lead to the Jacobi equation for timelike hypersurface congruences, further constraining admissible tension and potential profiles. These results establish gravitating tubes as a geometrically and dynamically consistent description of matter that respects the Geroch--Traschen obstruction.

</details>


### [85] [Acoustic Hawking radiation as a tunnelling effect in Michel accretion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00037)
*Nisha Jangid,Arnab K. Ray*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究稳态流体流入（Michel accretion）在声学黑洞（acoustic black hole）框架下的扰动及霍金效应（Hawking effect），发现欧拉扰动产生声学黑洞度量，向外传播的声波在声障（sonic barrier）处受阻但可隧穿，且霍金温度与霍金声子频率受时空几何增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索 Michel 吸积流入（Michel accretion inflow）在动力学系统鞍点处变为跨音速（transonic）时的声学黑洞性质，以及稳态流入对外部扰动的稳定性与声波传播行为。

Method: 对稳态流入施加欧拉动量型扰动（Eulerian perturbation），导出扰动传播的声学黑洞度量（metric of acoustic black hole），并分析高频行波（high-frequency travelling wave）的稳定性与声波隧穿行为。

Result: 欧拉扰动不会使稳态流入失稳；向外传播的声波被声障阻挡，但能以指数衰减幅度隧穿；霍金温度（Hawking temperature）与霍金声子频率（Hawking phonon frequency）受到时空几何（spacetime geometry）的增强。

Conclusion: Michel 吸积的稳态流入可作为声学黑洞模型，其声波隧穿与霍金辐射特性依赖于背景时空几何结构。

Abstract: Michel accretion becomes transonic at the saddle point of a dynamical system. An Eulerian perturbation on the steady inflow produces the metric of an acoustic black hole. As a high-frequency travelling wave the perturbation does not destabilize the steady inflow. Acoustic waves propagating outwards against the fluid inflow are blocked at the sonic barrier but can tunnel through it with an exponentially decaying amplitude. The Hawking temperature and the frequency of the Hawking phonons are enhanced by the spacetime geometry.

</details>


### [86] [Modified Cosmology from Mass-to-Horizon Relation: Background Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00133)
*Pranav Prasanthan,Hussain Gohar,Vincenzo Salzano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于质量-视界关系（mass-to-horizon relation）这一统一框架，研究了广义视界熵泛函（generalized horizon-entropy functionals）的宇宙学含义。通过Cai-Kim热力学第一定律推导出修正的弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equations），发现宇宙学可行性严格限制了与Bekenstein-Hawking面积律（area law）的偏差：可接受的场景局限于标准熵的邻域，显著偏差会破坏标准的辐射-物质-暗能量演化序列。所有可行模型在当前时期均预测与ΛCDM类似的宇宙学背景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探索质量-视界关系在宇宙学中的含义。这一关系为热力学自洽的广义视界熵泛函提供了统一框架，但对这些广义熵构造的宇宙学可行性缺乏系统的定量约束，因此需要严格检验其与观测宇宙学背景演化的一致性。

Method: 采用Cai-Kim表述的热力学第一定律（first law of thermodynamics），从质量-视界关系出发推导修正的弗里德曼方程，进而分析宇宙背景演化（background evolution）行为。通过考察熵泛函偏离Bekenstein-Hawking面积律的各种情形，定量评估其宇宙学可行性。

Result: 宇宙学可行性对广义熵的偏差施加了严格限制：可接受的场景仅局限于标准熵的狭窄邻域，更显著的偏差通常会破坏标准辐射-物质-暗能量（radiation-matter-dark-energy）演化序列。幂律纠缠修正（power-law entanglement corrections）可产生适度的早期暗能量（early-dark-energy）成分，但仅限于高度受限的参数空间；量子引力修正（quantum-gravity corrections）则因普朗克尺度（Planck scale）压制而观测上不可见。所有可行模型在当前时期预测ΛCDM类似的宇宙学背景。

Conclusion: 背景宇宙学（background cosmology）本身即可对此类热力学自洽的广义熵构造施加严格约束。可行的广义熵模型只能非常接近标准的Bekenstein-Hawking熵，否则会与标准的宇宙演化序列冲突，并且当前观测无法区分的预测与ΛCDM模型一致。

Abstract: We investigate the cosmological implications of the mass-to-horizon relation, which provides a unified framework for thermodynamically consistent generalized horizon-entropy functionals. Using the Cai-Kim formulation of the first law of thermodynamics, we derive the corresponding modified Friedmann equations and examine the resulting background evolution. We find that cosmological viability sharply restricts admissible deviations from the Bekenstein-Hawking area law: phenomenologically acceptable scenarios are confined to a narrow neighborhood of the standard entropy, while more pronounced deviations generically spoil the standard radiation-matter-dark-energy sequence. Power-law entanglement corrections can give rise to a moderate early-dark-energy component, but only within a tightly constrained region of parameter space, whereas quantum-gravity corrections are suppressed by the Planck scale and remain observationally irrelevant. Consequently, all viable models predict a $Λ$CDM-like cosmological background at the present epoch. These findings demonstrate that background cosmology alone imposes stringent constraints on thermodynamically consistent generalized entropy constructions of this class.

</details>


### [87] [Cosmology with a Non-minimally Coupled Dark Matter Fluid II. Cosmological Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00137)
*Samuele Silveravalle,Andrea Lapi,Francesco Benetti,Stefano Liberati*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了暗物质（dark matter）在流体层面与引力非最小耦合（non-minimally coupled to gravity）的宇宙学场景，分析了线性扰动（linear perturbations）的演化。研究发现：加速膨胀阶段产生的扰动呈现强蓝标量功率谱（strongly blue scalar power spectrum），与观测不符；而在反弹宇宙（bouncing universe）方案中，原初扰动可在收缩阶段产生近似标度不变（scale-invariant）的标量功率谱，且张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）符合当前约束，无需引入额外标量场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前期工作中，作者已证明暗物质与引力的非最小耦合（non-minimally coupled）可在流体层面驱动早期加速膨胀（accelerated expansion），从而解决视界问题（horizon problem）和平坦性问题（flatness problem），并在空间曲率（spatial curvature）存在时导致宇宙反弹（cosmological bounce）。本文进一步分析该框架下线性扰动的演化，以检验其能否产生与观测一致的原初扰动谱。

Method: 推导了标量、矢量和张量扰动的演化方程（equations governing scalar, vector and tensor perturbations），并在相关宇宙学阶段获得了解析解（analytic solutions）。

Result: 加速膨胀阶段产生的扰动产生强蓝标量功率谱（strongly blue scalar power spectrum），与观测不相容；而反弹宇宙方案中，原初扰动可在反弹前的收缩阶段（contracting phase）起源，产生近似标度不变（scale-invariant）的标量功率谱，同时张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）符合当前观测上限，且无需引入额外标量场。

Conclusion: 尽管当前分析基于简化的近似假设（simplifying approximations），有待后续改进，但这些结果表明非最小耦合暗物质（non-minimally coupled dark matter）可能为原初宇宙学扰动（primordial cosmological perturbations）的产生提供一种可行的替代机制。

Abstract: We extend our study of a cosmological scenario in which dark matter is non-minimally coupled to gravity at the fluid level. In previous work, we showed that this interaction can drive an early phase of accelerated expansion, addressing the horizon and flatness problems, and can also lead to a cosmological bounce in the presence of spatial curvature. Here we analyse the evolution of linear perturbations in this framework. We derive the equations governing scalar, vector and tensor perturbations, and obtain analytic solutions in the relevant cosmological regimes. We find that perturbations generated during the accelerated expansion phase produce a strongly blue scalar power spectrum and are therefore incompatible with observations. By contrast, in bouncing solutions primordial fluctuations can originate during the contracting phase before the bounce. In this case, the model yields an approximately scale-invariant scalar power spectrum while keeping the tensor-to-scalar ratio compatible with current bounds, without introducing additional scalar fields. Although our treatment relies on simplifying approximations that should be refined in future work, these results indicate that non-minimally coupled dark matter may provide a viable alternative mechanism for the generation of primordial cosmological perturbations.

</details>


### [88] [Cosmological implications of f(T, B) gravity: constraints from recent observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00169)
*Laxmipriya Pati,Santosh V. Lohakare,S. K. Maurya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在修正的挠率引力（modified teleparallel gravity）框架中引入边界项（boundary term）$B$，构建幂律模型 $f(T, B) = -T + α(-B)^β$，通过宇宙学观测数据（CC、Pantheon Plus、DESI BAO DR2）的马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）分析约束模型参数，验证其解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀和暗能量的能力。结果表明该模型在AIC准则下优于ΛCDM模型，并部分缓解了哈勃常数（$H_0$）张力，展现出动态幻象分割穿越（phantom-divide crossing）行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准ΛCDM模型在解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀和暗能量方面存在不足，尤其是哈勃常数（$H_0$）张力等问题。本文旨在通过考虑修正挠率引力（modified teleparallel gravity）中包含边界项（boundary term）的$f(T, B)$理论，提供一个超越ΛCDM的统一框架，以更好地拟合晚期宇宙观测数据。

Method: 采用幂律模型 $f(T, B) = -T + α(-B)^β$，其中$T$为挠率标量（torsion scalar），$B$为边界项（boundary term），该模型可在适当极限下还原为$f(T)$和$f(R)$引力。通过宇宙计时器（CC）、Pantheon Plus样本（PPS）和DESI重子声学振荡（BAO）第二版数据（DR2），结合马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法约束宇宙学参数和模型参数，并使用赤池信息准则（AIC）与ΛCDM模型进行对比。

Result: AIC分析表明，CC+PPS联合数据集强烈支持$f(T, B)$模型，其在晚期宇宙观测的拟合质量上优于ΛCDM。模型在一定程度上缓解了$H_0$张力，但需进一步分析以确认其统计显著性。背景宇宙学量显示该模型具有动态幻象分割穿越（phantom-divide crossing）特征，同时与晚期观测数据一致，给出了可行的膨胀历史和特征性暗能量演化。

Conclusion: $f(T, B)$幂律模型作为修正挠率引力框架中的一种统一描述，能够连接挠率与曲率基的引力理论，在拟合当前宇宙学数据方面表现出优于ΛCDM的潜力，并有望缓解哈勃常数张力，但其完整统计显著性仍需进一步专门分析。

Abstract: In this work, we examine the theoretical framework of modified teleparallel gravity with the inclusion of the boundary term in the action and investigate its cosmological implications by considering the power-law model $f(T, B) = -T + α(-B)^β$, with the aim of addressing the late-time accelerated expansion and the dark energy. In this context, $T$ denotes the torsion scalar and $B$ represents the boundary term, whose presence allows for departures from standard teleparallel dynamics and provides a unified description that connects torsion and curvature-based formulations, reproducing $f(T)$ and $f(R)$ gravity in appropriate limits. The viability of the model is assessed by confronting its theoretical predictions with observational data while constraining the cosmological and model parameters through a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) analysis using cosmic chronometers (CC), the Pantheon Plus sample (PPS), and the DESI baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) Data Release 2 (DR2) datasets, and comparing its performance with the standard $Λ$CDM model. The Akaike Information Criterion (AIC) analysis shows that the combined CC+PPS dataset strongly favors the $f(T, B)$ model, suggesting an improved phenomenological fit to late-time observations relative to $Λ$CDM. Our result further shows an alleviation of H0 tensions, although a dedicated analysis is required to establish its full statistical significance. Furthermore, the background cosmological quantities indicate that the model exhibits a dynamical phantom-divide crossing while remaining consistent with late-time observations and yielding a viable expansion history and characteristic dark energy evolution.

</details>


### [89] [Bondi Accretion onto a Damour-Solodukhin Wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00388)
*R. M. Yusupova,R. Kh. Karimov,A. Bhattacharya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究通过对比Damour-Solodukhin虫洞（DSWH）与Schwarzschild黑洞（SBH）的Bondi吸积轮廓，发现DSWH在参数λ远大于传统预期值（λ~1）时，仍能在视界附近有效模拟SBH的吸积特征，表明其作为黑洞模拟器的参数限制可能比原先认为的更为宽松。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Damour-Solodukhin虫洞（DSWH）已知能在某些性质上模拟Schwarzschild黑洞（SBH）的视界，但作为模拟器要求其参数λ极小（λ~0）。这一严格限制是否具有普遍性，特别是对于Bondi吸积这种重要的天体物理过程，尚待检验。

Method: 采用比较分析方法，系统对比DSWH与SBH两种天体在Bondi吸积（Bondi accretion）轮廓上的异同，考察DSWH参数λ在不同取值下的模拟表现。

Result: DSWH在λ~1的较高取值下，其部分吸积轮廓仍能在视界（horizon）附近成功模拟SBH的相应特征，表明传统上对λ必须极小的要求可能过于严格。

Conclusion: DSWH作为SBH模拟器的参数限制在Bondi吸积背景下可以显著放宽，这意味着DSWH在更宽泛的参数区间内仍可能充当有效的黑洞模拟器。

Abstract: The Damour-Solodukhin wormhole (hereinafter DSWH) is known to mimic Schwarzschild black hole (hereinafter SBH) horizon in some properties. To act as a mimicker, the DSWH parameter $λ$ by definition is required to be extremely tiny, i.e., $λ\sim 0$. Our comparative analyses show that such a requirement may be too restrictive at least as far as the Bondi accretion profiles of the two objects, the DSWH and SBH, are concerned. Intriguingly, it turns out that some profiles of DSWH mimic those for the SBH near the horizon even at values of $λ$ considerably higher, i.e., $λ\sim 1$.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现对于弦理论中的4维膜世界黑洞，无论静态还是旋转的潮汐荷电情形，Thorne环猜想在使用相同准局域质量时均统一成立。

Conclusion: 统一Thorne环猜想虽然在Kerr-Newman黑洞中不成立，但在弦理论4维膜世界黑洞中，针对潮汐荷电情形，该猜想可统一成立。

Abstract: In a recent article, Hod [1] has concluded the non-existence, heretofore unnoticed, of a unified Thorne's hoop conjecture that holds for the quasi-local mass, $\mathcal{M}(r\leq R_{+})$ for static Reissner-Nordstrőm black hole, but does not hold for the spinning electrically charged Kerr-Newman black holes, when the same quasi-local mass is used. While the conclusion is correct and important, we wish to point out a curious exception for which the conjecture holds in a unified way for both the static and spinning \textit{tidal} charged $4d$ braneworld black holes of string theory, when the mass in the conjecture is the same quasi-local mass.

### [91] [Probing the chaos bound via spinning particles in Kerr-Newman-AdS spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00432)
*Deyou Chen,Chuang Yang,Kangqiao Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋测试粒子探测 Kerr-Newman-AdS 时空中混沌界（chaos bound）违反的调控机制，发现粒子自旋、黑洞旋转与电荷以及宇宙常数（cosmological constant）之间存在复杂的竞争耦合关系，共同决定混沌界违反的条件与方向依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用自旋测试粒子（spinning test particles）作为探针，研究其在 Kerr-Newman-AdS 时空中的动力学行为，分析不同参数（如粒子自旋、黑洞旋转、电荷、宇宙常数）对混沌界违反的影响。

Result: 混沌界违反由时空几何、电磁力和粒子动力学共同调控；粒子自旋通过耦合轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）调节违反的方向依赖性与参数阈值；负宇宙常数（negative cosmological constant）充当势阱，其值越大混沌越强；黑洞顺行旋转（prograde rotation）可抑制甚至完全消除电荷驱动的违反，而电荷是违反的触发条件且受自旋调节；Kerr-AdS 极限下违反需黑洞反向旋转且旋转参数足够大、宇宙常数足够小；RN-AdS 极限下违反条件由电荷和宇宙常数联合决定，电磁排斥比电磁吸引更容易诱发违反。

Conclusion: Kerr-Newman-AdS 时空中的混沌界违反受粒子自旋、黑洞旋转与电荷、宇宙常数的多重竞争耦合调控，不同参数极限下违反条件呈现不同特征，为广义相对论与混沌系统的交叉研究提供了定量理解。

Abstract: In this paper, we employ spinning test particles as probes to investigate the regulatory effects of particle and black hole parameters on the violation of the chaos bound in Kerr-Newman-AdS spacetime. Our results demonstrate that the chaos bound violation is governed by the interplay of spacetime geometry, electromagnetic forces, and particle dynamics. The particle spin modulates the direction dependence and parameter thresholds of the violation through its coupling with the orbital angular momentum, which contributes to the total angular momentum. The negative cosmological constant acts as a potential well: a larger value enhances the chaotic behavior. A competitive coupling exists between the black hole rotation and charge -- its prograde rotation exerts a stabilizing effect that can suppress or even completely quench charge-driven violations, while the charge serves as a condition for triggering the violation, with its effect modulated by the spin stabilization. In the Kerr-AdS limit, the violation occurs only when the black hole rotates opposite to the $z$-axis with a sufficiently large rotation parameter and a sufficiently small cosmological constant. In the RN-AdS limit, the violation condition is jointly determined by the charge and the cosmological constant, with electromagnetic repulsion more readily inducing the violation than electromagnetic attraction.

Result: 发现了五自由度传播模式中纵向振幅（Al）与呼吸标量振幅（Ab）之间存在普适关系 Al/Ab = -2(1 - k²/ω²)。识别了一种新的矢量-张量极化转换机制：在优先参考系中，矢量模式会在运动探测器处不可避免地产生可观测的张量极化。优先参考系效应还会导致显著的引力波双折射。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种新的、与观测者无关的引力波极化分类方法，揭示了此前未曾注意的极化混合效应，并为检验洛伦兹破缺引力理论（Lorentz-violating gravity）提供了新途径。

Abstract: Gravitational wave (GW) polarizations are traditionally classified in a fixed frame ($E(2)$ classification), which does not account for how polarization patterns change under Lorentz boosts. In this work, we derive the explicit transformation laws for all six GW polarizations under longitudinal and transverse boosts. For gravity theories devoid of preferred frames, we propose a symmetry-based classification of the GW polarizations they admit. Among our key findings, we demonstrate that a propagating mode with five degrees of freedom strictly locks its longitudinal and breathing scalar amplitudes via the universal relation $A_l/A_b = -2(1-k^2/ω^2)$. For theories with a preferred frame, we analyze Bumblebee gravity and reveal that preferred-frame effects induce significant GW birefringence and observer-dependent polarization mixing. Crucially, we identify a novel vector-to-tensor polarization conversion mechanism, where vector modes in the preferred frame inevitably generate observable tensor polarizations for moving detectors, offering a new pathway to test Lorentz-violating gravity. Our framework provides a novel, observer-independent classification of GW polarizations and reveals previously unnoticed polarization mixing effects.

### [93] [Relaxation without ringdown for a compact object in modified gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00559)
*Gianmassimo Tasinato*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究一种具有黑洞外部几何但内部结构不同的致密天体，其奇宇称扰动表现为纯耗散弛豫极点而非振荡准正规模，这种奇特动力学响应源自隐藏的手征对称性，并在黑洞极限下弛豫时间发散、极点坍缩至零频。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验强引力区域的非广义相对论新物理（new strong-field physics beyond General Relativity），传统黑洞和致密天体的动力学响应通常表现为振荡模式，而该文旨在寻找一种具有全新动力学特征的可解析模型。

Method: 在矢量-张量理论（vector–tensor theory）中构造一个由矢量场支撑的正则致密解，外部匹配无表面层的史瓦西几何（Schwarzschild geometry）；通过被动边界条件精确控制奇宇称扰动，利用隐藏的手征对称性（hidden chiral symmetry）将扰动问题转化为单向输运而非波动传播，解析计算推迟格林函数和磁化率，并通过积分内部推导有效膜响应。

Result: 奇宇称扰动表现为纯耗散弛豫极点而非振荡准正规模；该致密天体因各向异性应力可超越Buchdahl极限并连续连接到黑洞紧凑度极限；外区没有常规的准正规模谱，而内区与匹配条件破缺对称性并量子化涨落谱；在黑洞极限下，弛豫时间发散、极点坍缩至零频，有限频外部扰动与内部解耦。

Conclusion: 黑洞行为不是通过振荡ringdown的出现，而是通过弛豫模式的消失来逼近，这为区分黑洞和新型致密天体提供了全新的动力学判据。

Abstract: Compact objects with black-hole-like exteriors may hide new strong-field physics in their interiors, making their dynamical response a sensitive probe of gravity beyond General Relativity. We present an analytically tractable, gravitationally bound compact object with a genuinely new dynamical signature: under a minimal passive boundary prescription, its exactly controlled odd-parity sector exhibits purely dissipative relaxation poles, rather than the oscillatory modes usually associated with black holes and exotic compact alternatives. The object we study is a regular, vector-supported compact solution of a vector--tensor theory, matched without any surface layer to an exterior Schwarzschild geometry. Owing to its anisotropic stress, it can violate the Buchdahl bound and be continuously connected to the black-hole compactness limit. Its unusual response follows from a hidden chiral symmetry, which turns the perturbation problem into one-way transport rather than ordinary wave propagation. The exterior region alone has no conventional quasinormal-mode spectrum; instead, the regular interior and the matching conditions break the symmetry and quantize the fluctuation spectrum. We analytically compute the retarded Green function and susceptibility, and derive an effective membrane response by integrating out the object's interior. In the black-hole limit, the relaxation times diverge, the poles collapse toward zero frequency, and finite-frequency exterior perturbations decouple from the interior. Black-hole behaviour is therefore approached through the disappearance of relaxation modes, not through the emergence of ringdown.

Method: 要求统计流形上曲率（curvature）和挠率（torsion）全局为零，将信息空间的全部性质编码进非度量张量（non-metricity tensor）。利用这一框架区分一般ξ参数化空间与θ（或η）参数化空间，其对应关系类似于广义相对论（general relativity）与对称远程引力（symmetric teleparallel gravity）之间的关系。

Conclusion: 对称远程引力（symmetric teleparallel gravity）的几何框架为信息几何（information geometry）提供了一种新的理论基础，有望统一并简化传统黎曼几何与对偶仿射联络的表述方式。

Abstract: Information geometry has traditionally been formulated within the framework of Riemannian geometry and dual affine connections. In this work, we reframe this foundational structure by introducing the geometric machinery of symmetric teleparallel gravity. By requiring both curvature and torsion to vanish globally on the statistical manifold, we demonstrate that the fundamental properties of the information space can be entirely encoded into the non-metricity tensor.
  This approach allows us to distinguish the general $ξ$-parameterized space from the $θ$- (or $η$-) parameterized space, mirroring the relationship between conventional general relativity and symmetric teleparallel gravity. Specifically, the $θ$- or $η$-coordinates emerge as the special coordinates in the coincident gauge, where the connection coefficients vanish.

### [95] [Spin-torsion interaction and geodesic bending](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00667)
*Sagar Kumar Maity,Amitabha Lahiri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究费米子内禀自旋（intrinsic spin）在时空中诱发挠率（torsion）的效应，进而产生有效四费米子相互作用（four-fermion interaction）。该效应影响恒星内部零测地线（null geodesic）和类时测地线（timelike geodesic）的偏折，并在常规曲率诱导效应之外引入额外的挠率贡献。分析表明，挠率对零测地线偏折的修正对于低质量和高质量白矮星（white dwarf）均非常微小，但在中子星（neutron star）等更致密的天体中有可能显著增大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索费米子自旋与时空挠率之间的耦合如何修改广义相对论中的测地线方程，特别是密度恒定的球对称费米子物质分布下恒星内部测地线偏折行为的变化。

Method: 采用自旋诱导挠率的框架，引入有效四费米子相互作用，并在球对称、恒定密度的简并费米子物质背景下分析零测地线和类时测地线的偏折。

Result: 发现测地线偏折中除了传统的曲率贡献外，还存在一个额外的挠率修正项，其大小取决于费米子数密度、不同手性（chirality）费米子种类的耦合常数以及物质分布的温度。对于白矮星，该修正非常微小；对于中子星等更致密天体，效应可能显著增大。

Conclusion: 挠率对测地线偏折的修正虽在常规致密星（如白矮星）中可忽略，但在极端致密天体（如中子星）中不可忽视，可能成为检验自旋-时空相互作用的重要观测窗口。

Abstract: The intrinsic spin of fermions induces torsion in spacetime, leading to an effective four-fermion interaction. This affects the bending of null and timelike geodesics inside a star with a spherically symmetric distribution of gravitationally dense fermionic matter of constant density. Our analysis shows an additional torsional contribution to the geodesic deflection, alongside the conventional curvature-induced effect. This change depends on the fermion number density, coupling constants of the different species of fermions with different chiralities, and the temperature of the matter distribution. We have shown that the torsion-induced corrections to null geodesic bending remains very small for both low- and high-mass white dwarfs, whereas significantly larger effects may arise in more compact astrophysical objects such as neutron stars.

### [96] [Thermodynamic-Geometric Phase Transition and Gravitational-Wave Quasinormal Modes of Schwarzschild Black Holes in $f(Q)$ Gravity: An RVB-Residue Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00670)
*Wen-Xiang Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个基于留数（residue）的框架，将 $f(Q)$ 引力中史瓦西型黑洞的热力学几何（thermodynamic geometry）与其引力波准正态模（quasinormal-mode）谱联系起来。研究表明，逆黑化函数的单极点留数同时控制霍金温度与 tortoise 坐标的对数单值性（logarithmic monodromy），从而进入内行准正态模边界条件。在扩展的 $f(Q)$ 态空间中，热力学 Hessian 的退化条件与热力学曲率的奇异性一致，并体现在准正态模谱的频移、Lyapunov 指数、阻尼时间和近视界单值性变化中，从而精确阐述了热力学-几何相结构与引力波 ringdown 之间的内在关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在从解析结构层面揭示 $f(Q)$ 引力中黑洞的热力学几何（thermodynamic geometry）与引力波准正态模（quasinormal-mode）谱之间的内在联系，从而为理解黑洞热力学相变与引力波 ringdown 信号之间的对应关系提供一个严格的框架。

Method: 基于对称遥平行引力（symmetric teleparallel gravity）的 $f(Q)$ 理论框架，采用 Robson-Villari-Biancalana (RVB) 方法提取逆黑化函数的单极点留数（simple-pole residue），分析其对霍金温度、tortoise 坐标对数单值性以及准正态模内行边界条件的控制作用。通过热力学 Hessian 的退化条件与热力学曲率的奇异性对比，建立与准正态模谱中光子球频率、Lyapunov 指数、阻尼时间和近视界单值性变化的对应关系。

Result: 在广义相对论史瓦西极限下，热容为有限负值，一维 Ruppeiner 几何无内禀曲率奇异性，无热力学相变。在扩展 $f(Q)$ 态空间中，修正的视界函数与有效 Wald 熵产生非平凡热力学 Hessian；其退化条件与热力学曲率的奇异性吻合，并对应准正态模谱的频移、Lyapunov 指数、阻尼时间及近视界单值性变化。

Conclusion: 热力学-几何相结构与引力波 ringdown 是同一修正黑洞度量解析结构在不同投影下的表现，二者之间存在精确的内在关联。

Abstract: We construct a residue-based framework connecting the thermodynamic geometry of a Schwarzschild-type black hole in $f(Q)$ gravity with its gravitational-wave quasinormal-mode spectrum. The analysis is based on the symmetric teleparallel formulation of gravity, in which the gravitational field is encoded by the nonmetricity scalar $Q$ rather than by curvature or torsion. For the Schwarzschild branch, the Robson--Villari--Biancalana (RVB) method gives the Hawking temperature through the simple-pole residue of the inverse blackening function. We show explicitly that the same residue also controls the logarithmic monodromy of the tortoise coordinate near the event horizon, and therefore enters the ingoing quasinormal-mode boundary condition. In the strict general-relativistic Schwarzschild limit the heat capacity is negative and finite, the one-dimensional Ruppeiner geometry contains no intrinsic curvature singularity, and no genuine thermodynamic phase transition occurs. In the extended $f(Q)$ state space, however, the modified horizon function and the effective Wald entropy generate a non-trivial thermodynamic Hessian. Its degeneracy condition coincides with singular behavior of the thermodynamic curvature and is reflected in the quasinormal-mode spectrum through shifts of the photon-sphere frequency, Lyapunov exponent, damping time, and near-horizon monodromy. This gives a precise statement of the internal relation between thermodynamic-geometric phase structure and gravitational-wave ringdown: both are different projections of the same analytic structure of the corrected black-hole metric.

### [97] [Closed Timelike Curves from a Vacuum Traveling Wave](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00788)

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个精确的真空时空解，该时空从满足弱、主、强能量条件的正则渐近平直初始数据出发，演化出闭合类时曲线（closed timelike curves），并研究了其编年视界（chronology horizon）在退化极限下的几何性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在广义相对论框架下，从物理上合理的初始条件（满足各类能量条件）是否能够自发产生闭合类时曲线，从而对时间机器（time machine）的可行性进行严格的经典引力分析。

Method: 利用爱因斯坦场方程确定时空几何，通过两个函数——谐和横向轮廓（harmonic transverse profile）和行波模（traveling-wave mode）——来描述演化；编年视界的退化极限由生成它的闭合类光测地线（closed null geodesic）的零自旋系数（boost）和光学标量（optical scalars）消失来刻画，该条件对应于Killing旋量（Killing spinor）的存在。

Result: 得到了一个真空精确解，其中闭合类时曲线在时间机器核心（time-machine core）中由类空变为类时；编年视界存在一个退化极限，在该极限下其生成闭合类光测地线的自旋系数和光学标量均趋于零。

Conclusion: 该构造表明，在满足标准能量条件的正则初始数据下，理论上可以演化出包含闭合类时曲线的时空，且编年视界的退化极限与Killing旋量条件相关联，这对理解因果性破坏的边界性质具有重要意义。

Abstract: We construct an exact vacuum spacetime that develops closed timelike curves from regular, asymptotically flat initial data respecting the weak, dominant, and strong energy conditions. Einstein's equations fix the geometry through two functions, a harmonic transverse profile and a traveling-wave mode, whose evolution drives the closed curves of the time-machine core from spacelike to timelike. The chronology horizon admits a degenerate limit in which its generating closed null geodesic has vanishing boost and optical scalars, the conditions for a Killing spinor.

</details>


### [98] [Gravitational Wave Signatures of Schwarzschild Black Hole in a Generalized Dehnen-Type $(1,4,γ)$ Dark Matter Halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00812)
*Bahromjon Shokirov,Arabboy Mirzakulov,Tursunali Xamidov,Sanjar Shaymatov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了广义Dehnen型暗物质（DM）晕中的类史瓦西黑洞周围的时间型测地线运动、周期轨道及其引力波信号，发现暗物质晕参数增大会导致MBO和ISCO半径及角动量增大、ISCO能量升高，并使周期轨道变大、轨道周期变长、波形振幅降低；产生的毫赫兹频段引力波信号可能被LISA、Taiji、天琴等未来空间探测器观测到，表明暗物质晕会在极端质量比旋进（EMRI）引力波信号中留下可观测印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究暗物质（dark matter, DM）分布如何影响黑洞（black hole, BH）周围测试粒子的轨道动力学以及极端质量比旋进（extreme mass-ratio inspiral, EMRI）系统产生的引力波（gravitational-wave）信号。

Method: 采用Dehnen型（1,4,γ）暗物质晕修正的类史瓦西（Schwarzschild-like）黑洞度规；对周期轨道及其引力波极化（gravitational-wave polarization）的计算采用数值拼凑法（numerical kludge approach）。

Result: 密度分布参数γ增大导致边际束缚轨道（marginally bound orbit, MBO）和内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）的半径与角动量增大，ISCO能量升高；暗物质晕参数γ、ρ_s和r_s增大使周期轨道尺寸增大、轨道周期变长、波形振幅降低；引力波谱主要集中在毫赫兹频段，部分特征应变（characteristic-strain）峰值高于LISA、Taiji和天琴（TianQin）等未来空间引力波探测器的灵敏度曲线。

Conclusion: 暗物质晕的分布会在EMRI引力波信号中留下可观测的印记，有望被下一代空间引力波探测器探测到。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate timelike geodesic motion, periodic orbits, and the associated gravitational-wave signals around a Schwarzschild-like black hole (BH) embedded in a generalized Dehnen-type dark matter (DM) halo. We show that the Dehnen-type $(1,4,γ)$ DM halo profile modifies test-particle dynamics, with increasing the parameter of density profile, $γ$, leading to larger marginally bound orbit (MBO) and innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) radii and angular momenta, together with a higher ISCO energy. These findings provide further insight into the role of the DM distribution in modifying the orbital dynamics, energy, and angular momentum of timelike test particles near the BH. Furthermore, we investigate the gravitational-wave signals produced by a stellar-mass compact object moving along periodic orbits around a supermassive BH embedded in a generalized Dehnen-type DM halo. Using the numerical kludge approach, we calculate the orbital trajectories and the corresponding gravitational-wave polarizations. We find that increasing the halo parameters $γ$, $ρ_s$, and $r_s$ produces larger periodic orbits, longer orbital periods, and lower waveform amplitudes. The resulting spectra lie mainly in the millihertz frequency range, while several characteristic-strain peaks lie above the sensitivity curves of future space-based gravitational-wave detectors such as LISA, Taiji, and TianQin. These results suggest that the surrounding DM halo may leave observable imprints on extreme mass-ratio inspiral (EMRI) gravitational-wave signals.

</details>


### [99] [Environmental effects vs. modified gravity in the LISA massive black hole binary population](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00845)
*Lorenzo Copparoni,Enrico Barausse*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过Fisher矩阵预报与层次嵌套抽样分析，发现LISA探测到的质量双黑洞引力波信号中，环境效应（吸积与粘性迁移）与修正引力效应（变牛顿常数Ṫ）在单事件层面不可区分，但在种群层面，即使极端天体物理假设下，环境效应也不会显著偏离真空预言，不会对LISA的广义相对论检验造成偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究LISA观测到的质量双黑洞（massive black hole binaries）引力波信号中，环境效应（吸积与盘内粘性迁移）能否留下可探测的印记，以及这些效应是否会与修正引力效应（如变牛顿常数Ṫ）产生混淆，从而影响LISA对广义相对论（general relativity）的检验。

Method: 选取吸积与盘内粘性迁移作为环境效应的代表通道，变牛顿常数Ṫ作为修正引力效应代表；将Fisher矩阵预报（Fisher-matrix forecasts）与基于天体物理种群模型的合成星表的层次嵌套抽样分析（hierarchical nested-sampling analysis）相结合。

Result: 即使在天体物理极端假设下（活跃比例50%、超爱丁顿吸积尾端），种群层面的后验分布仍与真空情况完全一致；但层次种群分析可能对活跃比例给出非平凡上限，并对爱丁顿比（Eddington-ratio）分布的斜率给出温和下界。

Conclusion: 在天体物理现实场景中，环境效应不太可能对LISA利用质量双黑洞进行的广义相对论检验产生偏差。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave signals from massive black hole binaries observed by LISA can carry imprints of both the astrophysical environment of the source and possible deviations from general relativity. We investigate whether environmental effects leave a detectable imprint on the LISA binary population, and whether they can mimic modified-gravity effects with the same frequency dependence. As representative channels we adopt accretion and viscous migration in a circumbinary disk for the environmental sector, and a time-varying Newton constant $\dot G$ for the modified-gravity sector. All three effects enter the waveform at the same negative post-Newtonian order and are described, at leading order, by a common phase-deformation parameter, which makes them formally degenerate at the single-event level. Combining Fisher-matrix forecasts with a hierarchical nested-sampling analysis of synthetic catalogs from astrophysically motivated population models, we find that, even under extreme astrophysical assumptions -- an active fraction of $50\%$, together with a super-Eddington accretion tail -- the population-level posteriors remain fully compatible with vacuum. However, a hierarchical population-wide analysis may yield a non-trivial upper limit on the active fraction and a mild lower bound on the slope of the Eddington-ratio distribution. Environmental effects are therefore unlikely to bias LISA's tests of general relativity with massive black hole binaries in astrophysically realistic scenarios.

### [100] [Horizon-scale intensity and polarization images of rotating Konoplya-Zhidenko black holes with thick accretion flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01017)
*Bing-Bing Chen,Chen-Yu Yang,Guo-Ping Li,Xin-Yun Hu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由几何厚光学薄吸积流包围的Konoplya-Zhidenko旋转非克尔黑洞的阴影和偏振图像。数值结果显示，阴影图像由外部亮环（高阶像）和内部暗区（事件视界）构成；变形参数增大高阶像尺寸但不改变整体形状，自旋参数和观测倾角增强高阶像的不对称性，并导致左侧强度远大于右侧。偏振图像中，高阶像区域的线偏振度显著小于其他区域。厚盘模型在强度和偏振图像上均产生与薄盘模型显著不同的特征，这些观测特征可作为探测时空几何和近吸积动力学的有效探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的黑洞阴影和偏振图像研究多基于薄盘吸积模型，而实际天体物理中厚吸积流更为常见。本文旨在探讨厚吸积流模型下Konoplya-Zhidenko旋转非克尔黑洞的阴影和偏振特征，并评估这些特征作为探测时空几何与吸积动力学探针的潜力。

Method: 采用解析弹道近似吸积流模型（analytical ballistic approximation accretion flow model）描述几何厚、光学薄的吸积流，并数值求解黑洞阴影和偏振图像。通过调节变形参数（deformation parameter）、自旋参数（spin parameter）和观测者倾角（observer inclination angle）等关键参数，分析图像特征的演变规律。

Result: 阴影图像包含外亮环（高阶像）和内暗区（事件视界）；变形参数增大会扩大高阶像尺寸但不改变其整体形状；自旋参数和观测倾角增大时，高阶像不对称性增强，左侧强度显著大于右侧；偏振图像中高阶像区域线偏振度远小于其他区域，偏振向量布满整个像平面。

Conclusion: 厚盘模型产生的强度和偏振图像特征与薄盘模型存在显著差异；在本文框架下，观测到的强度和偏振信号可作为探测黑洞时空几何和近事件视界吸积动力学的有效探针。

Abstract: We investigate the shadow and polarization images of a Konoplya-Zhidenko rotating non-Kerr black hole surrounded by a geometrically thick and optically thin accretion flow. The accretion flow is described by an analytical ballistic approximation accretion flow model. The numerical results show that the shadow image exhibits two main features, an outer bright ring and an inner dark region. The former corresponds to higher order images, while the latter is produced by the black hole event horizon. Increasing the deformation parameter $η$ does not significantly change the overall shape of the higher order images, but it enlarges their size. Increasing the spin parameter $a$ and the observer inclination angle $θ_o$ enhances the asymmetry of the higher order images and makes the intensity on the left side much larger than that on the right side. This behavior is associated with frame dragging and the relativistic Doppler effect. In the polarization images, the degree of linear polarization is much smaller in the higher-order image region than in other regions, and the polarization vectors extend over the whole image plane. These results indicate that the thick disk model produces features in both intensity and polarization images that differ markedly from those in thin disk models. Within the framework used in this work, the observed intensity and polarization signatures can serve as effective probes of the underlying spacetime geometry and near horizon accretion dynamics.

### [101] [Backreaction of stimulated Hawking radiation in an optical analogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01118)
*Lorenzo M. Procopio,Raul Aguero-Santacruz,David Bermudez,Ulf Leonhardt*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过光纤光学事件视界（event horizon）类比实验，发现霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）的产生机制并非复杂的级联过程，而是存在一个简单直接的过程，并测量了该过程对场的反作用（backreaction），为理解引力系统中黑洞如何辐射提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 霍金辐射将引力、量子力学与热力学联系起来，但一直未在天文观测中被直接证实；此外，场量子如何产生霍金量子的具体机制此前尚不清楚。

Method: 本文在光纤光学事件视界（fibre-optical analogue of the event horizon）类比系统中进行了实验与理论分析，以研究霍金辐射的产生过程。

Result: 实验发现了一个简单、直接的霍金辐射产生过程，而非此前认为的复杂级联过程，并成功测量了该过程对场的反作用（backreaction）。

Conclusion: 该发现暗示其他实验室类比系统乃至引力场中的黑洞辐射也可能存在类似的直接过程，为理解黑洞如何辐射提供了新的洞见。

Abstract: Hawking radiation - the emission of quantum particles at the event horizon of a black hole - connects gravity with quantum mechanics and thermodynamics; the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy has been the benchmark for potential quantum theories of gravity. But Hawking radiation has never been observed in astronomy, only in laboratory analogues and the chances of ever observing it in space are astronomically small. The energy of Hawking radiation must come from the gravitational field around the black hole, but how field quanta generate Hawking quanta has been unknown. Here we report on experimental and theoretical evidence for the process that generates Hawking radiation in a fibre-optical analogue of the event horizon. There, as in gravity, it has been believed that Hawking radiation comes from a complicated, cascaded process; here we have found a simple, direct process and measured its backreaction on the field. Our findings suggest an equally direct process for other laboratory analogues and perhaps also for gravitational fields, shedding light on how black holes might radiate.

</details>


### [102] [Preheating and oscillon formation in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01177)
*Areef Waeming,Josu C. Aurrekoetxea,Katy Clough,Pau Figueras,Áron D. Kovács*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究早期宇宙中非线性过程形成的标量场孤子结构（振荡子，oscillons）在标量-张量理论高阶导数修正下的行为，发现尽管振荡子性质变化不大且通常不形成黑洞，但在大耦合条件下，形成阶段的有效场论（EFT）描述会失效，此时需要引入下一阶修正项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究标量-张量理论中领先阶高阶导数贡献（leading order higher derivative contributions）是否会改变早期宇宙中振荡子（oscillons）的形成与增长，并确定有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）描述在哪些极限下会失效。

Method: 基于标量-张量理论，引入领先阶高阶导数修正项，分析非微扰过程形成的振荡子的性质及其演化；通过考察度规曲率项的大小来判断EFT有效性的边界。

Result: 振荡子的性质未发生显著改变，且通常不会形成黑洞；但在大耦合条件下，形成阶段可能使系统演化离开EFT的有效范围，导致可预测性丧失；若振荡子成功形成，则它们倾向于稳定，且EFT修正保持有界。

Conclusion: EFT的失效由振荡子最稠密区域的度规大曲率项触发，因此忽略局部反作用（local backreaction）和非线性场动力学的近似方法可能遗漏重要效应。

Abstract: Non-perturbative processes in the early universe may create overdense structures in scalar fields like the inflaton, called oscillons. In this work, we explore whether the leading order higher derivative contributions to the scalar-tensor theory change the formation and growth of these structures, and investigate the limits in which the effective field theory (EFT) description breaks down. We find that whilst the properties of the oscillons are not significantly modified, and black holes do not generically form, for large couplings the period of formation can result in the evolution leaving the regime of validity of the EFT, at which point predictivity is lost and the next order terms in the EFT should become relevant. If the oscillons survive their formation, they tend to be stable and the EFT corrections remain bounded. The EFT breakdown is triggered by large curvature terms in the metric in the densest regions of the oscillon, meaning that approximations of such modified theories that neglect the local backreaction and non-linear dynamics of the fields may miss important effects.

</details>

### [103] [The Role of Compressibility in Modified Quasi-Linear Viscoelasticity: A Comparison of Simple Shear and Torsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00813)
*Valentina Balbi,Griffen Small*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了可压缩性（compressibility）在有限应变下软固体修正准线性粘弹性（MQLV）本构框架中的作用，发现仅在体积变化发生时可压缩性才影响响应，剪切应力对可压缩性不敏感，而法向应力表现出显著敏感性，并与Poynting效应存在耦合作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有修正准线性粘弹性（MQLV）框架通常假设材料不可压缩或弱可压缩，但可压缩性对软固体在有限应变下力学响应的影响尚不明确，尤其在不同变形模式下的角色有待澄清。

Method: 在不可压缩和弱可压缩假设下，针对简单剪切（simple shear）和扭转（torsion）两种变形模式，推导了解析与半解析结果。

Result: 可压缩性仅在有体积变化时影响响应；等容变形下体积贡献为零。剪切应力与扭矩对可压缩性不敏感，而法向应力与轴向力因剪切与体积弛豫的耦合表现出显著敏感性。体积效应与Poynting效应在简单剪切中相互抵消、减弱弛豫，在扭转中相互增强、促进弛豫。上述趋势与脑组织实验吻合，但弱可压缩模型对高可压缩材料（如琼脂糖凝胶）存在局限。

Conclusion: 研究强调了在建模法向应力响应时考虑可压缩性的重要性，并推动发展完全可压缩的本构公式及其数值实现。

Abstract: We investigate the role of compressibility in the modified quasi-linear viscoelastic (MQLV) constitutive framework for soft solids at finite strain, where shear and bulk responses are governed by distinct relaxation functions. Analytical and semi-analytical results are derived for simple shear and torsion, under incompressible and slightly compressible assumptions. We show that compressibility affects the response only when volume changes occur: under isochoric deformations, the bulk contribution vanishes, while even small deviations from isochoricity significantly alter the normal response. Shear stress and torque are largely insensitive to compressibility, whereas normal stress and axial force exhibit pronounced sensitivity due to the coupling between shear and bulk relaxation. We further demonstrate that volumetric effects interact with the Poynting effect: in simple shear they oppose each other, reducing relaxation, while in torsion they reinforce each other, enhancing it. These trends agree with brain tissue experiments but reveal limitations of the slightly compressible model for highly compressible materials, such as agarose gels. Overall, the results emphasise the importance of accounting for compressibility in modelling normal stress responses and motivate the development of fully compressible formulations and numerical implementations.

</details>


### [104] [Pattern formation in nonlinear dynamics of nematic liquid crystals above the flexoelectric instability threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00723)
*E. S. Pikina,E. I. Kats,A. R. Muratov,V. V. Lebedev*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟和现象学理论，研究向列相液晶中挠性电不稳定性的非线性阶段，发现了一维静态斑图与动态行波/驻波斑图，并基于类金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg-Landau）唯象学对结果进行了阐释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管液晶中电流体动力学（electro-hydrodynamic）不稳定性的实验数据已大量积累，但理论解释长期局限于线性分析（linear analysis）。为突破这一局限，本文研究向列相液晶中挠性电不稳定性（flexoelectric instability）的非线性阶段。

Method: 基于一套完整的非线性电流体动力学方程组，对受外加交变电场（alternating electric field）影响的、具有负介电各向异性（negative anisotropy in dielectric permittivity）和负电导各向异性（negative anisotropy in electrical conductivity）的向列相液晶进行分析；采用此前工作中提出的模型[1,2]进行非线性动力学数值模拟，并在不稳定性阈值附近引入类金兹堡-朗道唯象学（Ginzburg-Landau-like phenomenology）。

Result: 识别出两类斑图（pattern）：一维静态结构（static patterns）和动态结构（dynamic patterns，包括驻波与行波）。动态斑图的形成时间尺度远大于外加电场周期。驻波（standing waves）对小尺度横向扰动（transverse perturbations）稳定，而传播波（propagating waves）不稳定。

Conclusion: 挠性电效应驱动的非线性不稳定性可产生一维静态与动态斑图，斑图类型取决于材料和实验控制参数；类Ginzburg-Landau唯象学可用少数参数合理描述数值结果。

Abstract: For many decades, researchers have been studying various types of electro-hydrodynamic instabilities in liquid crystals. A significant amount of experimental data has been collected, however, the theoretical interpretations of the results typically rely on linear analysis. In response to this limitation, we investigate the nonlinear stage of the flexoelectric instability in nematics, focusing on liquid crystals with a negative anisotropy in their dielectric permittivity and electrical conductivity. We base our analysis on a comprehensive set of nonlinear electro-hydrodynamic equations for these nematics influenced by an external alternating electric field. The equations predict an instability that is driven by the flexoelectric effect. In order to examine the peculiarities of this phenomenon, we use a model that was proposed in our previous publications, Refs. [1,2], which allows us to perform numerical simulation of nonlinear dynamics. We examine patterns that are formed above the instability threshold. Through numerical simulations, we have identified static and dynamic patterns that occur over a timescale that is much longer than the period of the external electric field. The static patterns are one-dimensional structures and dynamic patterns are standing or traveling one-dimensional waves. The type of the realized pattern depends on the material and experimentally controlled parameters. We found that the standing waves are stable with respect to small transverse perturbations, whereas the propagating waves are unstable. We present a Ginzburg-Landau-like phenomenology that applies near the instability threshold. This approach allows us to rationalize our numerical findings with a few parameters.

</details>


### [105] [Single Chain Expulsion from Diblock Copolymer Micelles with Dense Corona](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00992)
*Shuang Yuan,Jiajia Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory）和二维自由能面（2D free energy surface）分析，研究了嵌段共聚物胶束中单链排出的自由能景观，发现排出势垒与疏水嵌段长度和溶剂选择性呈线性关系，并识别出一个近简并的反应通道，为理解胶束链交换中的超伸展机制（hyperstretching mechanism）和过渡态系综（transition state ensemble）提供了连续介质理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解嵌段共聚物胶束中单链排出（single-chain expulsion）的自由能景观，揭示链交换过程的微观机制，并解释近期实验中观察到的排出势垒（expulsion free energy barrier）与嵌段长度及溶剂选择性之间的线性标度关系。

Method: 采用自洽场理论（self-consistent field theory）构建自由能景观，以链的亲水-疏水连接点（junction）到胶体质心的距离作为第一反应坐标；引入连接点与疏水嵌段自由端之间的距离作为第二反应坐标，构建二维自由能面（two-dimensional free energy surface），并利用弦方法（string method）识别最小能量路径（minimum energy path）。

Result: 排出自由能势垒与疏水嵌段长度及溶剂选择性呈线性关系，与近期实验结果一致；所有最小能量路径汇聚至一个近简并的反应通道，在该通道内疏水嵌段的端到端距离呈现宽分布，但对应的排出势垒几乎无法区分。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一个连续介质层次的理论基础，用于理解胶束链交换中的超伸展机制（hyperstretching mechanism）和过渡态系综（transition state ensemble）。

Abstract: We use self-consistent field theory to investigate the free energy landscape for single-chain expulsion from a diblock copolymer micelle with a dense corona. Using the distance from the micelle center-of-mass to the hydrophilic-hydrophobic junction of the chain as the reaction coordinate, we compute the free energy landscape for chain exchange. Our results show that the expulsion free energy barrier scales linearly with both the hydrophobic block length and the solvent selectivity, consistent with recent experiments. To accurately resolve chain conformation, we introduce a second reaction coordinate: the distance between the junction and the free end of the hydrophobic block, and construct a two-dimensional free energy surface. Using the string method to identify the minimum energy path, we find that all pathways converge to a nearly degenerate reaction channel, irrespective of the initial path. Within this channel, the end-to-end distance of the hydrophobic block exhibits a broad distribution, yet the corresponding expulsion barriers remain nearly indistinguishable. Together, these findings establish a continuum-level theoretical foundation for understanding the hyperstretching mechanism and the transition state ensemble in micellar chain exchange.

</details>


### [106] [Diffusiophoretic transport of colloids and emulsions in complex environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01031)
*Amir A. Pahlavan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文综述了多孔介质中化学梯度驱动扩散泳（diffusiophoresis）与扩散渗流（diffusioosmosis）的输运机制，将其纳入经典胶体输运框架，并重点讨论了溶质锋面对死孔脱除增强和横向迁移对宏观突破曲线的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多孔介质中普遍存在化学梯度，经典胶体输运模型（colloid transport models）未充分考虑扩散泳（diffusiophoresis）的作用，亟需将其整合到现有输运框架中以解释和预测复杂环境中的胶体行为。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，首先梳理化学梯度的来源及扩散（spreading）与混合（mixing）的区别；接着总结经典胶体输运理论、扩散泳与扩散渗流的最小物理化学模型（minimal physicochemical model），以及相关的实验平台。

Result: 近期结果表明：扩散性溶质锋面（diffuse solute fronts）可通过延长驱动力持续时间增强死端孔隙（dead-end pores）内的泳动去除；流道内的横流线迁移（cross-streamline migration）可使宏观突破曲线（breakthrough）和弥散（dispersion）变化数个数量级。

Conclusion: 文章最后讨论了乳液液滴、多相流、受限介质及活体介质等开放问题，特别指出从二维微模型的代数混合（algebraic mixing）到三维多孔介质混沌混合（chaotic mixing）的转变是未来重要课题。

Abstract: Chemical gradients are ubiquitous in porous and crowded environments, including soils, filters, fabrics, tissues, hydrogels, biofilms and living cells. They arise from displacement fronts, dissolution and precipitation, ion exchange, metabolism, root exudation, evaporation, gas dissolution, freeze--thaw cycles and externally imposed chemical treatments. These gradients can drive colloids, macromolecules and emulsion droplets by diffusiophoresis, while simultaneously driving diffusioosmotic flows along confining surfaces. Classical models of colloid transport in porous media emphasize hydrodynamic dispersion, surface interactions, straining, deposition, detachment and filtration. This chapter places diffusiophoresis within that broader transport framework and reviews how porous media generate, stretch, disperse and sustain the solute gradients that drive phoretic motion. We first discuss sources of chemical gradients and the distinction between spreading and mixing, then summarize classical colloid transport, the minimal physicochemical model for diffusiophoresis and diffusioosmosis, and the experimental platforms used to study these effects. Particular emphasis is placed on recent results showing that diffuse solute fronts can enhance phoretic removal from dead-end pores by prolonging the duration of forcing, and that cross-streamline migration within flowing pathways can change macroscopic breakthrough and dispersion by orders of magnitude. We close by discussing emulsion droplets, multiphase flows, confined and living media, and open problems, including the transition from algebraic mixing in two-dimensional micromodels to chaotic mixing in three-dimensional porous media.

</details>

### [107] [An analog ac voltage amplifier based on a single straintronic magnetic tunnel junction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00104)
*Cael Johnson,Rahnuma Rahman,Supriyo Bandyopadhyay*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文探讨了应变磁性隧道结（straintronic magnetic tunnel junction, s-MTJ）在模拟电压放大中的应用。通过将栅极电压固定在线性区中点并叠加小交流信号，可实现无失真电压放大；与晶体管放大器不同，其放大倍数可通过外部电源电压调节。文章基于磁化动力学建模，分析了无失真放大下输入信号的最大允许幅度和频率，并推导了放大倍数的表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统磁性隧道结（MTJ）主要用于数字存储与逻辑应用；而新近提出的应变磁性隧道结（s-MTJ）因其电导可通过栅压产生的机械应变连续调节，展现出模拟应用的潜力。本文旨在探索s-MTJ在模拟电压放大中的可行性，并分析其相较于晶体管放大器的独特优势。

Method: 通过将s-MTJ的栅极电压固定于电导-栅压转移特性曲线线性区的中点，并叠加小幅交流电压，实现无失真放大。采用磁化动力学（magnetization dynamics）建模，分析输入信号的幅度与频率约束，并推导放大倍数的解析表达式。

Result: 研究发现，s-MTJ可实现无失真的交流电压放大，其放大倍数不再仅依赖器件内部参数（如跨导和厄利电阻），而是可通过外部电源电压进行调节。基于磁化动力学模型，获得了输入信号最大允许幅度与频率的约束条件，并给出了放大倍数的表达式。

Conclusion: s-MTJ作为一种新型模拟放大器件，在电压放大应用中具有独特的可调放大倍数优势，适用于多种模拟电路场景。其线性区工作特性与外部电压调控能力为模拟信号处理提供了新的器件选项。

Abstract: Magnetic tunnel junctions (MTJs) are known for their digital applications (memory and logic). A special class of them called "straintronic" magnetic tunnel junctions (s-MTJ) has lately emerged as a potential platform for analog applications because their conductance can be varied continuously with mechanical strain generated with a gate voltage. The conductance versus gate voltage (transfer) characteristic always has a linear region and that can be leveraged for a variety of analog applications. Here, we discuss one such application, namely analog voltage amplification. If the s-MTJ's gate voltage is fixed around the midpoint of the linear region and a small ac voltage is superimposed on it, then the ac voltage can be amplified without distortion as long as its amplitude is small enough to avoid gate voltage excursion beyond the linear region. Unlike a transistor-based voltage amplifier whose amplification is determined solely by the transistor's internal parameters - namely the transconductance and Early resistance - here the amplification can be varied by an external power supply voltage. We examine the maximum allowed amplitude and frequency of input signal for distortion-free amplification by modeling the magnetization dynamics and derive an expression for the amplification.

</details>


### [108] [Universal Scaling of the Spin Hall Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00343)
*Atsuo Shitade,Naoto Nagaosa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋和磁矩累积系数研究狄拉克电子的自旋霍尔效应，在自洽T-矩阵近似下考虑短程非磁性杂质，发现了三种不同的标度区域，包括一个指数为0.6的新标度关系，从而构建了无歧义的自旋霍尔效应统一理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）的理论描述中，自旋流的定义长期存在歧义。本文旨在通过自旋与磁矩累积系数（spin and magnetic-moment accumulation coefficients）来研究狄拉克电子的自旋霍尔效应，从而构建一个无歧义的自旋霍尔效应统一理论。

Method: 采用自洽T-矩阵近似（self-consistent T-matrix approximation）处理短程非磁性杂质（short-range nonmagnetic impurities），通过改变电导率（electric conductivity）σ^{yy}来研究自旋和磁矩累积系数的标度行为。

Result: 发现三种不同的标度区域：超清洁区（superclean regime）中系数正比于σ^{yy}，源于斜散射（skew scattering）；中等无序区（moderately dirty regime）中系数近似常数；脏区（dirty regime）中呈现新的标度关系，系数正比于(σ^{yy})^{0.6}，其指数与反常霍尔电导率（anomalous Hall conductivity）的标度指数不同。

Conclusion: 研究结果构建了自旋霍尔效应的统一理论，消除了自旋流定义上的歧义，揭示了自旋霍尔效应与反常霍尔效应在标度行为上的异同。

Abstract: We study the spin Hall (SH) effect for the Dirac electrons in terms of the spin and magnetic-moment accumulation coefficients $-Γ^{00} g_{s(m)z}^{\phantom{s(m)z} xy}$. We take short-range nonmagnetic impurities into account within the self-consistent $T$-matrix approximation. Similarly to the universal scaling for the anomalous Hall (AH) effect, we find three disctinct regimes by changing the electric conductivity $σ^{yy}$; the superclean regime with $-Γ^{00} g_{s(m)z}^{\phantom{s(m)z} xy} \propto σ^{yy}$ owing to the skew scattering, moderately dirty regime with almost constant $-Γ^{00} g_{s(m)z}^{\phantom{s(m)z} xy}$, and dirty regime with a new scaling relation $-Γ^{00} g_{s(m)z}^{\phantom{s(m)z} xy} \propto (σ^{yy})^{0.6}$ whose exponent differs from that of the AH conductivity. Our results construct a unified theory of the SH effect without any ambiguity of spin current.

### [109] [Modulation of anomalous Hall angle in a magnetic topological semimetal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00396)
*Jinying Yang,Yanxing Shang,Xingchen Liu,Yibo Wang,Xuebin Dong,Qingqi Zeng,Meng Lv,Shen Zhang,Yang Liu,Binbin Wang,Hongxiang Wei,Yizheng Wu,Stuart Parkin,Gangqin Liu,Claudia Felser,Enke Liu,Baogen Shen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反常霍尔角（anomalous Hall angle, θA）是衡量纵向驱动电流转换为横向自旋极化霍尔电流效率的关键参数，对于反常霍尔传感应用中的磁场检测灵敏度至关重要。然而，该角度难以调控，且磁性材料的典型值通常仅为0.1°至3°。

Method: 提出将tanθA表示为电阻率（electrical resistivity）与反常霍尔电导率（anomalous Hall conductivity）乘积的函数；利用磁性Weyl半金属（magnetic Weyl semimetal）Co₃Sn₂S₂及其Fe掺杂的单晶纳米片（nanoflakes）进行微加工制备反常霍尔器件。

Result: 成功将tanθA调控至0.46，对应约25°的反常霍尔角。基于Fe掺杂Co₃Sn₂S₂单晶纳米片的微加工器件在1 Hz下实现了7028 μΩucm/T的高霍尔灵敏度（Hall sensitivity）和23.5 nT/Hz⁰·⁵的磁场可探测度（magnetic field detectability）。

Conclusion: 通过材料选择和参数化公式实现了反常霍尔角的大幅调控，为开发高性能反常霍尔磁场传感器提供了新途径。

Abstract: The anomalous Hall angle (θA) is a measure of the efficiency of converting a longitudinal driving current to a transverse spin-polarized Hall current. For anomalous Hall sensing, a large anomalous Hall angle can improve the sensitivity of magnetic field detection. However, modulation of this angle is challenging and magnetic materials typically have low angles of 0.1 to 3°. Here, we report modulation of the anomalous Hall angle in the magnetic Weyl semimetal Co3Sn2S2. We propose that the angle parameter tanθA can be formulated as a function of the product of electrical resistivity and anomalous Hall conductivity. Our scheme was utilized to demonstrate the modulation of tanθA up to a magnitude of 0.46, corresponding to an angle of around 25°. Microfabricated anomalous Hall devices using Fe-doped Co3Sn2S2 single-crystalline nanoflakes exhibit a high Hall sensitivity of 7028 μΩucm/T and a magnetic field detectability of 23.5 nT/Hz0.5 at 1 Hz.

### [110] [Real-time dynamics of triplet-resonant tunneling driven by nonequilibrium phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00520)

Method: 采用实时电荷传感（time-resolved charge sensing）技术，在声子辐照下对双量子点（double quantum dot）的激发态进行直接测量，观测电荷和自旋动力学。

Conclusion: 实验结果揭示了声子驱动下双量子点激发态中电荷与自旋动力学的实时行为，表明非平衡声子环境能够诱导定向输运，为开发超出平衡态限制的新型功能器件提供了实验基础。

Abstract: Driven nonequilibrium systems can host emergent functionalities beyond equilibrium, but real-time access to excited-state dynamics remains limited. Here we report real-time measurements of phonon-driven charge and spin dynamics in excited states of a double quantum dot. Under phonon irradiation, resonant inter-dot tunneling emerges at triplet resonance. Time-resolved charge sensing reveals that the resonant inter-dot tunneling is strongly modified by spin blockade. For weaker inter-dot coupling, the nonequilibrium phonon environment generates a unidirectional transport cycle along the phonon density gradient.

### [111] [Robustness of Quantum Discord in Nonequilibrium Electronic Transport through Tunnel-Coupled Quantum Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00602)
*Thingujam Yaiphalemba Meitei,Saikumar Krithivasan,Md. Manirul Ali,Arijit Sen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究双量子点（double quantum dot, DQD）系统与费米子库（fermionic reservoirs）耦合下的非平衡动力学，发现量子失协（quantum discord）在非平衡稳态下保持有限，且比经典关联更具鲁棒性，表明可通过非平衡电子输运调控介观系统中的非经典关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子关联（quantum correlations）是量子信息处理的核心资源，而已有的纠缠（entanglement）度量无法捕获全部量子关联。量子失协（quantum discord）能揭示超出纠缠的量子关联，但其在开放费米子量子器件中的非平衡行为尚待系统研究。

Method: 采用量子朗之万方程（quantum Langevin equation）形式，得到双量子点系统与费米子库耦合下的精确约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrix），从而在非平衡条件下系统分析量子失协和经典关联（classical correlations）的瞬态动力学与稳态行为。

Result: 量子失协在非平衡稳态下于广泛参数范围内保持有限。热梯度（thermal gradients）降低了关联的整体幅度，但量子失协仍然存在且表现出更强的鲁棒性（greater resilience）。

Conclusion: 非平衡电子输运（nonequilibrium electronic transport）结合环境谱特性（spectral properties）和库不对称性（reservoir asymmetry），提供了调控介观系统中非经典关联的有效手段；量子失协可作为开放费米子量子器件（open fermionic quantum devices）的稳健特征。

Abstract: Quantum discord captures quantum correlations beyond entanglement and can remain finite even when the entanglement vanishes. We investigate the transient nonequilibrium dynamics and steady-state behavior of quantum discord and classical correlations in a double quantum dot (DQD) system coupled to fermionic reservoirs. By employing a quantum Langevin equation formalism, we obtain the exact reduced density matrix of the system, enabling a comprehensive analysis of its quantum and classical correlations under nonequilibrium conditions. The influence of system-reservoir coupling strength, spectral bandwidth, thermal bias, and varying initial state on both the transient dynamics and steady-state correlations is systematically analyzed. Quantum discord remains finite in the nonequilibrium steady state over a broad parameter range. Although thermal gradients reduce the overall magnitude of correlations, quantum discord persists and exhibits greater resilience. These results demonstrate that nonequilibrium electronic transport, together with the environmental spectral properties and reservoir asymmetry, provides an effective means of controlling nonclassical correlations in mesoscopic systems and establishes quantum discord as a robust hallmark of open fermionic quantum devices.

</details>


### [112] [Spinterface-like mechanism of the chirality-induced spin selectivity in donor chiral-bridge acceptor complexes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00668)
*Subhajit Sarkar,Oliver L. A. Monti,Yonatan Dubi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种分子内自旋界面（intramolecular spinterface）机制，通过施主-手性桥-受主（D--χB--A）复合物中的双电子Lindblad模型，定量解释了手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）效应在时间分辨EPR实验中观测到的自旋极化现象，而无需引入本征自旋轨道耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验发现手性与非手性分子在时间分辨EPR信号上存在差异，这被归因于手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）效应，但其微观起源及与CISS的关联仍存在争议，尤其是在缺乏金属界面的体系中。

Method: 建立了一个双电子Lindblad模型，其中光激发的电荷转移电子穿过手性桥，与残留的施主电子发生交换作用，该施主电子充当局域磁矩（localized magnetic moment），类似于电极表面的感生磁矩。通过桥的电荷电流在施主-桥界面产生有效螺线管场（solenoidal field），打破自旋简并和方向对称性，从而实现自旋选择性输运。

Result: 模型在真实实验条件和电荷转移时间尺度下产生了数十百分比的自旋极化，与三聚体（triads）和DNA发夹结构（DNA hairpins）中报告的CISS特征定量吻合。模型明确展示了自旋极化对螺线管耦合强度、温度和自旋混合率的依赖关系，识别了能够产生稳健CISS-like自旋过滤的内部自旋界面（internal spinterface）参数区间。

Conclusion: 孤立D--χB--A复合物中的CISS-like信号完全可由自旋界面机制解释，这为理解基于器件和分子内部的CISS平台提供了一个统一的概念框架。

Abstract: The chirality-induced spin selectivity (CISS) effect has been invoked to explain recent reports of differences in the time-resolved EPR signals between chiral and achiral molecules. However, the microscopic origin of these differences and their connection to CISS remains contested, particularly since these systems lack a metal interface. Here we introduce an intramolecular spinterface-like mechanism that naturally arises within donor-chiral bridge-acceptor (D--$χ$B--A) complexes and quantitatively reproduces experimentally reported observed spin polarization in time-resolved EPR studies. In our two-electron Lindblad model, the photoexcited charge-transfer electron traversing the chiral bridge exchanges with the residual donor electron, which acts as a localized magnetic moment analogous to an induced magnetic moment on an electrode surface. The resulting through-bridge charge current produces an effective solenoidal field at the donor--bridge interface, breaking spin degeneracy and directional symmetry, thus enabling spin-selective transport without invoking intrinsic spin-orbit coupling on the bridge. We show that the interplay between this current-induced field, donor thermalization (which breaks time-reversal symmetry), and bridge spin mixing yields tens-of-percent polarization over realistic experimental conditions and charge-transfer time scales, matching reported CISS signatures in triads and DNA hairpins. By explicitly resolving the dependence on solenoidal coupling strength, temperature, and spin-mixing rates, the model identifies the regime in which internal spinterfaces can generate robust CISS-like spin filtering. These findings demonstrate that CISS-like signals in isolated D--$χ$B--A complexes are fully compatible with a spinterface mechanism, providing a unified conceptual framework for interpreting both device-based and molecule-internal CISS platforms.

</details>


### [113] [Facet-selective ballistic supercurrent in a weak topological insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00683)
*Prasanna Rout,Ankit Khola,Lalit Pandey,Paolo Sessi,Xiaochun Huang,Ivo Cools,S. Galeski,Matthias Bode,Johan Åkerman,Floriana Lombardi,Thilo Bauch,Saroj P. Dash*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该实验在弱拓扑绝缘体（weak topological insulator）ZrTe₅中实现了沿特定晶面的弹道超电流（ballistic supercurrent），通过约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）和超导量子干涉（superconducting quantum interferometry）证实了超电流集中在具有无隙拓扑表面态的晶面上，确立了弱拓扑绝缘体作为面分辨超导器件平台的地位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在三维晶体中，将超导关联（superconducting correlations）诱导至拓扑保护的表面态以实现空间分离且局限于特定表面的超电流尚未实现。本文旨在利用弱拓扑绝缘体ZrTe₅，探索能否实现选择性晶面（facet-selective）的弹道超电流。

Method: 研究基于弱拓扑绝缘体ZrTe₅构建约瑟夫森结，通过超导量子干涉测量观察临界电流（critical current）的振荡行为，并旋转磁场以分析干涉图案随磁场方向的变化。同时测量临界电流的温度依赖性和干涉瓣形状以判断输运机制。

Result: 超导量子干涉显示类似SQUID的临界电流振荡，周期为磁通量子（flux quantum），表明超电流集中于特定晶面上的无隙拓扑表面态。旋转磁场产生显著不同的干涉图案，超电流分布与体拓扑（bulk topology）关联。临界电流呈指数温度依赖，干涉瓣为三角形，提示高透射拓扑通道引起的弹道输运（ballistic transport）。

Conclusion: 弱拓扑绝缘体被确立为一种可实现面分辨超导器件（facet-resolved superconducting devices）和高阶拓扑超导（higher-order topological superconductivity）的平台。

Abstract: Topological superconductivity is widely pursued by inducing superconducting correlations in topologically protected boundary states. In two dimensions, this strategy has been realized using one-dimensional topological edge modes, but in three-dimensional crystals, spatially separated surface supercurrents confined to selected facets have not yet been achieved. Here we demonstrate facet-selective ballistic supercurrent in Josephson junctions based on the weak topological insulator ZrTe<sub>5</sub>. Superconducting quantum interferometry reveals SQUID-like critical current oscillations with flux-quantum periodicity, establishing that the supercurrent is spatially concentrated on specific crystallographic facets that host gapless topological surface states. Rotating the magnetic field yields markedly distinct interference patterns, linking the supercurrent distribution to the underlying bulk topology. The exponential temperature dependence of the critical current and triangular interference lobes provide signatures of ballistic transport due to high-transmission topological channels. These results establish weak topological insulators as a platform for facet-resolved superconducting devices and higher-order topological superconductivity.

Method: 通过至多三根纳米线，每根纳米线配置两个侧栅电极（side-gate electrodes），构建通用逻辑电路，实现完备的逻辑门集合。

Result: 成功实现了AND、OR、NOT、COPY四种功能完备的逻辑门，以及半加器（half-adder）组合逻辑电路；器件具有通用布局和可扩展性，结合快速开关与小电压信号等已有实验进展，具备实际应用潜力。

Abstract: The observation of the gate-controlled supercurrent (GCS) effect in superconducting nanostructures initiated major research efforts toward the realisation of superconducting-based computing architectures. Here we introduce a universal logic circuit that can be a promising superconducting building block of classical hybrid supercomputers. We demonstrate a functionally complete set of logic gates by realising the AND, OR, NOT and COPY gates. The general layout and scalability of our device, combined with recent experiments demonstrating fast switching and small voltage signals, make it a functional candidate in superconducting electronics. Our device enables the realization of all classical logic gates and the half-adder combinational logic circuit using at most three nanowires, each uniquely configured with two side-gate electrodes.

### [115] [Electrical control of spin photocurrent in a magnetoelectric oxide Cr$_2$O$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00807)
*Zhuo-Cheng Gu,Hiroaki Ishizuka*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过非线性响应理论，以 Cr₂O₃ 为例，论证了在磁电材料（magnetoelectrics）中可利用电场调控磁振子自旋光电流（magnon spin photocurrent），揭示了场致 Dzyaloshinsky–Moriya 相互作用对自旋电流电导率的关键调制作用及其各向异性，并证明了电场对共振频率与峰强的可控性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自旋电子学（spintronics）中，利用电场或电流控制磁性是一个核心课题。本文旨在探索是否能够通过电场在磁电材料中调控磁振子自旋光电流，以拓展电控磁性的手段。

Method: 采用非线性响应理论（nonlinear response theory），以 Cr₂O₃ 为模型体系，分析电场对自旋电流的调制机制，并计算自旋电流电导率随电场和光偏振的变化。

Result: 电场诱导的 Dzyaloshinsky–Moriya 相互作用（Dzyaloshinsky–Moriya interaction）是改变自旋电流电导率的关键因素，且该电导率对光偏振表现出显著的各向异性（anisotropy）。共振频率（resonance frequency）和峰强（peak intensity）均对外电场 E 呈现不同的依赖性；此外，双磁振子过程（two-magnon processes）导致连续谱（continuum spectrum）的出现，源于场诱导的自旋倾斜（spin canting）。

Conclusion: Cr₂O₃ 是实现电可调自旋光伏效应（electrically tunable spin photovoltaic effect）的理想平台，电场可以有效控制自旋光电流，为自旋电子学器件的电控方案提供了新途径。

Abstract: Controlling magnetism by electric field or current is a central topic in spintronics. In this work, we argue that the magnon spin photocurrent can also be controlled by the electric field in magnetoelectrics. Taking Cr$_2$O$_3$ as an example, we demonstrate how the spin current is modified by the electric field, using nonlinear response theory. We find that the Dzyaloshinsky--Moriya interaction induced by the applied field plays a key role in modifying spin-current conductivity, which exhibits pronounced anisotropy with respect to the light polarization. In particular, both the resonance frequency and the peak intensity show distinct dependences on the external electric field $E$, demonstrating electrical control of the spin photocurrent. In addition, we show that the two-magnon processes give rise to a continuum spectrum, a consequence of the field-induced spin canting. These results show that Cr$_2$O$_3$ is a promising platform for realizing electrically tunable spin photovoltaic effect.

### [116] [Symmetry Classification of Non-Reciprocal Responses in Multiterminal Ring Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00919)
*Chen-How Huang,Tero T. Heikkilä*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于对称性的框架，用于分类多端环状量子器件中的非互易响应（non-reciprocal response）。通过将器件建模为$n$顶点环，并引入每条键（bond）上的二元方向变量，将全部$2^n$种电流构型按拓扑绕数（topological winding number）$W$划分为对称性轨道（orbit）。以最小非平凡情形$n=3$证明了两个与微观细节无关的结论：轨道内简并的解除需要同时破缺时间反演（time-reversal, $T$）和空间反演（spatial inversion, $I$）；破缺后的残余几何对称性决定了哪些响应可观测。通过三个量子点（quantum dot）耦合超导库（superconducting bath）的玩具模型验证了理论预测，实现了反应性量子循环器（reactive quantum circulator）响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多端环状量子器件中的非互易响应缺乏系统性的对称性分类框架，现有研究多依赖于具体微观模型。本文旨在发展一种不依赖微观细节的普适对称性理论，以解释和预测此类器件中的非互易输运行为。

Method: 将器件抽象为$n$顶点环，每条键上定义二元变量$e_k\in\{+1,-1\}$编码信号流向偏好，对称群将所有$2^n$种构型划分为由拓扑绕数$W$标记的等价类（轨道）。以$n=3$为最小非平凡情形，分析时间反演$T$与空间反演$I$对称性破缺的条件，以及残余几何对称性对可观测响应的约束。采用三量子点耦合超导库的玩具模型进行数值验证。

Result: 对于$n=3$情形，轨道内简并的解除（即产生非互易响应）必须同时破缺$T$和$I$中的两者，单独破缺任一对称性均不足。当$T$和$I$均破缺后，器件剩余几何对称性决定可观测响应类型：等腰三角形几何仅允许两种响应——均匀循环（uniform circulation，所有键电流同向）和基边反向半循环（semi-circulation），而腰边反向半循环被对称性禁止。玩具模型验证了预测，实现了反应性量子循环器响应。

Conclusion: 本文建立的对称性框架为多端环状量子器件中的非互易响应提供了普适分类方法，揭示了拓扑绕数与对称性破缺之间的深层联系，并为设计特定功能的非互易量子器件（如量子循环器）提供了指导原则。

Abstract: We present a symmetry-based framework to classify the non-reciprocal responses of multiterminal ring quantum devices. The device is modeled as a ring of $n$ vertices, where a binary variable $e_k\in\{+1,-1\}$ on each bond encodes the preferred direction of signal flow between terminals. Non-reciprocity corresponds to a preferred current configuration on the ring, and the symmetry group of the device partitions all $2^n$ configurations into equivalence classes(orbits) characterized by a topological winding number $W$. Using the minimal non-trivial case $n=3$, we establish two results independent of microscopic details. First, lifting the degeneracy within an orbit generates non-reciprocal responses. For $n=3$ this requires simultaneous breaking of both time-reversal $T$ and spatial inversion $I$. Breaking either alone is insufficient. Second, the residual geometry symmetry after $T$ and $I$ are broken determines which responses are observable. For an isosceles triangular geometry, only two types of response are allowed: uniform circulation (all bonds carrying current in the same direction) and semi-circulation with the reversed bond on the geometrically distinct base. Semi-circulation with the reversed bond on either equal leg is symmetry-forbidden. Both predictions are validated using a minimal toy model of three quantum dots coupled to superconducting baths, which demonstrates a reactive quantum circulator response.

</details>


### [117] [Modification of Damon-Eshbach magnetostatic mode spectra in ferromagnet/paramagnet bilayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00964)
*M. A. Kuznetsov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在静磁近似（magnetostatic approximation）下，计算了面内磁化铁磁/顺磁双层膜中体与表面自旋波的频谱，发现当系统温度接近顺磁层的居里温度（Curie temperature）时，表面自旋波可变为单向传输模式，且该模式可通过外磁场或温度进行开关调控，为可调谐磁子逻辑器件提供了理论平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索铁磁/顺磁双层结构中偶极耦合（dipolar coupling）对磁静模（magnetostatic modes）频谱的影响，特别是寻求实现可调控单向表面自旋波（unidirectional surface spin waves）的条件，以服务于可调谐磁子逻辑器件（tunable magnonic logic devices）的设计需求。

Method: 采用静磁近似计算面内磁化铁磁/顺磁双层膜中体自旋波与表面自旋波的频谱；将顺磁层磁化率建模为 $χ\propto 1/(T-T_C)$，以描述其随温度接近居里温度（Curie temperature）而增大的行为；通过分析Damon-Eshbach模的修正，推导表面自旋波单向传输的条件与频率非互易性（frequency nonreciprocity）的幅度。

Result: 确定了表面自旋波成为单向传输模式（即仅能沿单一方向传递能量）的条件；给出了其频率非互易性的大小；论证了通过改变外磁场或温度可以实现单向波模式的开关切换。

Conclusion: 铁磁/顺磁双层体系能够实现可调控的单向表面自旋波传输，具有构建可调谐磁子逻辑器件的潜力。

Abstract: Using the magnetostatic approximation, we calculate the spectra of bulk and surface spin waves in an in-plane magnetized ferromagnet/paramagnet bilayer. Due to the dipolar coupling between the layers, the paramagnet becomes polarized, which in turn modifies the spectrum of the Damon-Eshbach magnetostatic modes. We assume that the paramagnet is characterized by a magnetic susceptibility, $χ\propto 1/(T-T_C)$, which reaches large values when the system temperature $T$ is close to the Curie temperature $T_C$. We find the conditions under which surface spin waves become unidirectional, i.e., capable of carrying energy in only one direction, and determine the magnitude of their frequency nonreciprocity. We demonstrate the possibility of switching the unidirectional wave regime on and off by varying the external magnetic field or temperature, making the ferromagnet/paramagnet system an attractive platform for tunable magnonic logic devices.

### [118] [Magnon-polaron mediated spin Seebeck effect in altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00993)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该研究从理论层面分析了在外加磁场（external magnetic field）作用下交变磁体的自旋塞贝克效应（spin Seebeck effect），研究其沿面内不同方向的自旋塞贝克系数差异，并结合磁弹性相互作用（magnetoelastic interactions）分析共振峰的响应行为。

Result: 交变磁体在外加磁场下的自旋塞贝克系数沿面内方向表现出显著各向异性（directional anisotropy），且该各向异性随磁场增强而增大；磁弹性相互作用产生的共振峰相对于外加磁场的位置反映了内在的磁振子能带各向异性（magnon band anisotropy），提供了局部化特征以增强交变磁响应的可区分性。

Conclusion: 自旋塞贝克效应的方向各向异性与磁弹性共振峰可作为交变磁有序（altermagnetic order）的可靠实验特征，同时为交变磁体在自旋电子学（spintronic）器件中的应用奠定理论基础。

Abstract: Altermagnets, distinguished by compensated antiparallel spins yet nondegenerate magnon spectra, bridge the gap between ferromagnets and antiferromagnets. Although several probes such as anisotropic transport and spectroscopic measurements have been proposed to identify altermagnetic order, experimentally accessible transport signatures remain highly desirable. Here, we show that in altermagnets subject to an external magnetic field, the spin Seebeck effect exhibits pronounced directional anisotropy. Specifically, the spin Seebeck coefficient differs significantly along in-plane directions, and this anisotropy increases with field strength. Magnetoelastic interactions further produce resonant peaks whose positions with respect to an applied magnetic field reflect the intrinsic magnon band anisotropy, and provide localized features that enhance the distinguishability of the altermagnetic response. The peaks provide a robust experimental signature of altermagnetic order. Our findings serve as signatures of altermagnetic order while laying the groundwork for their application in spintronic devices.

### [119] [Exceptional points in dissipative coupling polaron-polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00994)
*A. J. Vega-Carmona,D. A. Mendoza,A. Camacho-Guardian,M. A. Bastarrachea-Magnani*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了耗散性光-物质耦合（dissipative light-matter coupling）如何与强关联效应结合，在双激子共振（biexciton resonance）存在的情况下塑造极化子-极化激元（polaron-polariton）的集体量子激发，发现其能产生反常色散关系与奇异点（exceptional points），且奇异点的位置与共存性受耗散耦合和组分衰减率调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强关联（strong correlations）与耗散（dissipation）如何共同塑造集体量子激发（collective quantum excitations）是多体物理学（many-body physics）的核心挑战，现有研究对二者在激子-极化激元（exciton-polariton）体系中的协同效应认识不足。

Method: 在双激子共振存在的情况下，研究强相互作用的激子-极化激元体系，引入耗散性光-物质耦合，分析由此形成的极化子-极化激元准粒子（quasiparticles）的能谱特性。

Result: 多体关联（many-body correlations）与非厄米耦合（non-Hermitian coupling）的相互作用导致了极化子-极化激元能谱中的反常色散关系（anomalous dispersion relations）和奇异点；奇异点的位置与共存性由耗散耦合以及激子组分与光子组分的相对衰减率（relative decay rates）共同控制，使得奇异点能够出现在不同的极化子-极化激元分支上。

Conclusion: 耗散性极化子-极化激元被识别为一个多功能平台（versatile platform），可用于探索以可调光-物质准粒子为特征的非厄米多体物理学（non-Hermitian many-body physics）。

Abstract: Understanding how strong correlations and dissipation combine to shape collective quantum excitations is a central challenge in many-body physics. We investigate the effect of dissipative light-matter coupling on strongly interacting exciton-polaritons in the presence of a biexciton resonance, which gives rise to polaron-polariton quasiparticles. We show that the interplay between many-body correlations and non-Hermitian coupling generates anomalous dispersion relations and exceptional points in the polaron-polariton spectrum. The location and coexistence of exceptional points are controlled by the dissipative coupling and the relative decay rates of the excitonic and photonic constituents, allowing them to emerge across different polaron-polariton branches. These results identify dissipative polaron-polaritons as a versatile platform for exploring non-Hermitian many-body physics with tunable light-matter quasiparticles.
