### [120] [Bandwidth-Limited Critical Currents in Electrically Tunable Moiré Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01056)
*Riccardo Bertini,Xueqiao Wang,Sergey Slizovskiy,Zhiren Zheng,Julien Barrier,Chiara Pizzo,Robin Smeyers,Krystian Nowakowski,Hitesh Agarwal,Alvaro Moreno,Bert Jorissen,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Milorad V. Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明在莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）中，微带（miniband）带宽决定了非平衡态输运（out-of-equilibrium transport）的临界电流（critical current）。通过实验、理论模型和跨平台比较，揭示了临界电流随带宽变窄而显著降低的规律，并建立了该关系作为石墨烯超晶格中的普适特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔超晶格中的窄微带带宽已知与关联相和拓扑相密切相关，但带宽对高电流输运（high-current transport）行为的影响尚不明确。本文旨在探索带宽在非平衡态输运中的角色，并建立其与临界电流之间的直接联系。

Method: 实验上，将双层石墨烯与六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride, hBN）对齐，利用面外位移场（out-of-plane displacement field）连续展平价带微带，测量高电流输运区间的临界电流变化。理论上，构建了最小解析模型（minimal analytical model）来拟合临界电流的降低行为，并通过与不同莫尔平台（moiré platform）的比较验证标度关系的普适性。

Result: 实验观察到临界电流随微带带宽变窄而显著下降，该行为被最小解析模型所捕捉。跨平台比较表明，临界电流与带宽之间的标度关系（scaling）是石墨烯超晶格的普适特征（universal feature）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了微带色散（miniband dispersion）与高电流输运之间的直接联系，并将高电流输运机制确立为一种快速、可访问的电学探针（electrical probe），用于探测带宽的演化。

Abstract: Moiré superlattices host narrow minibands whose bandwidth governs correlated and topological phases. Here, we demonstrate that the bandwidth also sets the critical current for the onset of out-of-equilibrium transport. In bilayer graphene aligned to hexagonal boron nitride, we explore the high-current transport regime as we continuously flatten the valence miniband using an out-of-plane displacement field. We observe a significant reduction in the critical current, which is captured by a minimal analytical model and corresponds to the calculated narrowing of the miniband. Moreover, by comparing distinct moiré platforms, we show that the scaling between critical current and bandwidth is a universal feature of graphene superlattices. Our results reveal a direct link between miniband dispersion and high-current transport, and establish this regime as a fast and accessible electrical probe of bandwidth evolution.

</details>


### [121] [Confinement in a magnetically induced WSe$_2$ quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01192)
*Rachid El Aitouni,Mohammed El Azar,Clarence Cortes,David Laroze,Ahmed Jellal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用有效狄拉克哈密顿量（effective Dirac Hamiltonian）和Kummer合流超几何函数（Kummer's confluent hypergeometric function）等数学工具，理论研究了单层二硒化钨（WSe₂）量子点中局域磁场对大质量狄拉克费米子（massive Dirac fermion）的约束效应。结果表明，局域磁场能有效抑制克莱因隧穿（Klein tunneling），促进稳定准束缚态（quasibound state）的形成，并产生可调谐的共振峰，为过渡金属硫族化合物（transition metal dichalcogenide, TMD）纳米结构中的自旋-谷输运控制提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于存在磁通量（magnetic flux）的有效狄拉克哈密顿量，通过使用Kummer合流超几何函数、贝塞尔函数（Bessel function）和汉克尔函数（Hankel function）精确推导波函数和散射系数，系统分析了散射效率（scattering efficiency）和载流子密度分布（carrier density distribution）随入射能量、磁场强度和量子点半径的变化规律。

Result: 局域磁场能够有效抑制克莱因隧穿，促进稳定准束缚态的形成。低能载流子被磁势垒强烈约束，磁局域化（magnetic localization）与几何约束（geometric confinement）的相互作用产生了尖锐且可调谐的共振峰（resonance peak）。

Conclusion: 该研究为在过渡金属硫族化合物纳米结构中控制自旋-谷输运（spin-valley transport）提供了重要见解，并为量子约束器件和量子信息技术的发展奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Monolayer tungsten diselenide (WSe$_2$) has become a suitable platform for quantum transport and spintronics and valleytronics applications because it possesses an intrinsic band gap and strong spin-orbit coupling and spin-valley coupling features. The electrostatic confinement of Dirac fermions proves challenging in graphene because of Klein tunneling, yet WSe$_2$ provides an environment that supports both carrier localization and the development of confined quantum states. In this work, we theoretically investigate the confinement of massive Dirac fermions in a WSe$_2$ quantum dot generated by a localized magnetic field. Using the effective Dirac Hamiltonian in the presence of a magnetic flux, we derive the exact wave functions and scattering coefficients by employing Kummer's confluent hypergeometric functions together with Bessel and Hankel functions. Our results show that the localized magnetic field provides an efficient mechanism to suppress Klein tunneling and promote the formation of stable quasibound states. We systematically examine the scattering efficiency and carrier density distributions as functions of the incident energy, magnetic field strength, and quantum dot radius. We find that low-energy carriers are strongly confined by the magnetic barrier, while the interplay between magnetic localization and geometric confinement gives rise to sharp and tunable resonance peaks. These results provide valuable insight into the control of spin-valley transport in transition metal dichalcogenide nanostructures and establish a theoretical basis for the development of quantum confinement devices and quantum information technologies.

### [122] [Graph-Native Reinforcement Learning Enables Traceable Scientific Hypothesis Generation through Conceptual Recombination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00924)

TL;DR: 本文提出 Graph-PRefLexOR，一种图原生的推理模型家族，通过分组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行微调，将推理组织为显式阶段（机制探索、图构建、模式提取和假设综合），在材料科学开放式问题中相较基线模型提升 40-65% 的推理可追溯性，并展现出更大的语义多样性。

Method: 开发 Graph-PRefLexOR 模型家族，采用分组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行微调，将推理组织为四个显式阶段：机制探索（mechanism exploration）、图构建（graph construction）、模式提取（pattern extraction）和假设综合（hypothesis synthesis）。该设计将神经语言生成与符号关系结构（symbolic relational structure）相结合，使因果连接可被构建、检查和复用。

Conclusion: 图原生强化学习（graph-native reinforcement learning）可作为通往可解释 AI 系统（interpretable AI systems）的路径，用于材料设计及其他科学领域中的科学假设生成。

Abstract: Accelerating materials discovery requires AI systems that can generate scientifically valid hypotheses through multi-step, domain-grounded reasoning. Standard large language models often produce fluent but weakly traceable responses to open-ended materials design problems, making it difficult to determine whether final answers are supported by coherent intermediate reasoning. We develop Graph-PRefLexOR, a family of graph-native reasoning models fine-tuned with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to organize reasoning into explicit phases for mechanism exploration, graph construction, pattern extraction, and hypothesis synthesis. This design links neural language generation with symbolic relational structure, enabling causal connections to be constructed, inspected, and reused. On 100 open-ended questions from materials science and mechanics literature, Graph-PRefLexOR achieves 40-65% improvements over corresponding base models, with the largest gains in reasoning traceability. Embedding analyses show broader semantic exploration and approximately 2-3 times greater semantic diversity than baselines. Semantic backtracking and layer-wise hidden-state analyses further show stronger alignment between structured reasoning and final answers. Finally, test-time graph expansion reveals that additional compute primarily increases long-range conceptual recombination within a bounded semantic space, rather than simply expanding semantic coverage. These results establish graph-native reinforcement learning as a pathway toward interpretable AI systems for scientific hypothesis generation in materials design and other scientific applications.

### [123] [Optimal Resource Utilization for Autonomous Laboratory Orchestrators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01188)
*Austin McDannald,Julia Tisaranni,Howie Joress*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种两步法，用于解决自主实验室平台中多仪器硬件约束下的资源调度与执行问题：第一步利用约束编程（constraint programming）寻找最小化总时间的最优调度方案；第二步通过任务状态依赖系统（status dependencies）确保该调度方案的稳健执行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自主实验室（autonomous laboratories）中，AI代理（AI agents）可以建议下一批实验，但如何充分利用可用资源来规划和执行这些任务是一个完全不同的问题，尤其当面临多仪器（multiple instruments）具有不同容量和吞吐量（throughputs）的实际硬件约束时，这一问题更具挑战性。

Method: 该方法包含两步：首先，采用约束编程（constraint programming）在满足硬件限制与容量的前提下，找到使总时间最小化的最优调度方案；其次，为每个任务引入状态依赖系统（system of status dependencies），以实现对最优调度方案的稳健执行（robust execution）。

Result: 约束编程能够找到满足硬件限制与容量的最优调度，最小化总时间；状态依赖系统使得该最优调度能够在实际执行中保持稳健。

Conclusion: 该方法有效解决了自主金属-有机框架（metal-organic framework, MOF）合成平台在真实硬件约束下的资源利用问题，实现了从调度优化到稳健执行的完整流程。

Abstract: In autonomous laboratories, AI agents suggest the next batch of experiments to do. However, planning and executing those tasks taking full advantage of the available resources is a completely different question. This can be challenging when dealing with real-world hardware constraints, especially so when there are multiple instruments with different capacities and throughputs. Here we demonstrate a 2-step method to address resource utilization for our autonomous platform for metal-organic framework synthesis. First, we use constraint programming to find optimal schedules. This finds schedules that minimizes the total time while still satisfying the limitations and capacities of the hardware. Secondly, we use a system of status dependencies for each task, which allows for the robust execution of the optimal schedules.

### [124] [On a new class of high-corank Kac-Moody algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00792)
*Simon Beaudoin,Quentin Bonnefoy,Alessio Marrani,Michel Rausch de Traubenberg,Victor Saulquin*

Main category: math.RA

TL;DR: 本文提出了几族与Kac-Moody代数（Kac-Moody algebras）相关的广义Cartan矩阵（generalized Cartan matrices）的递归构造方法，其矩阵规模和余秩（corank）均呈指数增长。构造由连通多重图（connected multigraphs）及其对称广义Cartan矩阵上的块倍增（block-doubling）操作编码，并将余秩问题转化为谱图论（spectral graph theory）问题。论文给出了两个显式递归族，计算了它们的谱和余秩，并强调了绝对指数增长与相对渐近密度的区别。所得代数通常是不定的（indefinite）且余秩大于一，因此根格（root lattice）中包含多个独立中心方向和多个各向同性根方向。文中还讨论了替代构造及其在引力、超引力、弦/M-理论及相关广义对称性问题中的可能应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 系统构造具有大余秩（corank）的广义Cartan矩阵（generalized Cartan matrices），将余秩问题转化为谱图论（spectral graph theory）问题，从而揭示Kac-Moody代数（Kac-Moody algebras）中指数增长的结构复杂性，并为高余秩不定代数（indefinite algebras）的代数结构提供构造框架。

Method: 通过连通多重图（connected multigraphs）及其对称广义Cartan矩阵上的块倍增（block-doubling）操作递归构造广义Cartan矩阵族。将余秩问题等价转化为谱图论问题，即矩阵$2\mathrm{Id}-\operatorname{Adj}(G)$的余秩等于邻接矩阵特征值$2$的重数。给出了两个显式递归族并计算其谱和余秩。

Result: 构造的广义Cartan矩阵族的规模和余秩均呈指数增长。所得Kac-Moody代数通常是不定的（indefinite）且余秩大于一，根格（root lattice）中包含多个独立中心方向和多个各向同性根方向。明确了绝对指数增长与相对渐近密度之间的差异。

Conclusion: 总结了替代构造方法，并指出了这些高余秩不定Kac-Moody代数在引力（gravity）、超引力（supergravity）、弦/M-理论（string/M-theory）及相关广义对称性问题中的潜在应用。

Abstract: We present recursive constructions of several families of generalized Cartan matrices associated with Kac-Moody algebras, whose sizes and coranks grow exponentially. The constructions are encoded by connected multigraphs and by block-doubling operations on their associated symmetric generalized Cartan matrices. Equivalently, the corank problem is translated into a spectral graph-theoretic problem: the corank of $2\mathrm{Id}-\operatorname{Adj}(G)$ is the multiplicity of the adjacency eigenvalue $2$. We give two explicit recursive families, compute their spectra and coranks, and emphasize the difference between absolute exponential growth and relative asymptotic density. The resulting algebras are typically indefinite and singular of corank larger than one, and therefore contain several independent central directions and several isotropic radical directions in the root lattice. We also discuss alternative constructions and possible applications to the algebraic structures appearing in gravity, supergravity, string/M-theory and related generalized symmetry problems.

### [125] [A universal time-of-arrival signature of Bose--Einstein condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00184)
*Mathieu Beau,Timothey Szczepanski*

TL;DR: 本文证明玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚会在谐波囚禁气体自由下落的时间到达（TOA）统计中产生一个尖点；在准经典长飞行时间（time-of-flight）极限下，该尖点的单侧斜率之比是普适的，等于理想气体热容之比，且仅被弱相互作用轻微扰动，因此可作为凝聚的时间域可测量特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation）在动力学观测中是否留下可区分的特征信号，特别是在时间到达（time-of-arrival, TOA）统计中是否存在可测量的奇异性（singularity）。

Method: 基于准经典长飞行时间极限（semiclassical long time-of-flight regime）分析，引入小参数 ε=σ_V/√(2gH)≪1，并考虑理想气体远场极限（ideal-gas far-field limit）下的统计行为，同时纳入有限原子数与弱相互作用效应进行扰动分析。

Result: 到达时间分布的均值与标准差（均受纵向速度方差控制）在凝聚转变处保持连续，但出现一个尖点（cusp）。该尖点的单侧斜率之比是普适常数 R_∞=2.5556…，等于阱内气体在临界温度以下与以上的热容之比 C(T_c⁻)/C(T_c⁺)。有限原子数会圆化该尖点，弱相互作用仅造成轻微扰动。

Conclusion: 时间到达统计中的尖点结构提供了一个可测量的时间域凝聚信号，且该信号对有限尺寸效应和弱相互作用具有鲁棒性（robust），表明其可用于实验探测玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚的转变。

Abstract: We show that Bose--Einstein condensation produces a cusp in the time-of-arrival (TOA) statistics of a harmonically trapped gas released into free fall. In the semiclassical long time-of-flight regime, with $ε=σ_V/\sqrt{2gH}\ll1$, both the mean and standard deviation of the arrival time distribution, which are governed by the longitudinal velocity variance, remain continuous, but acquire a cusp whose one-sided slope ratio is universal within the ideal-gas far-field limit, $\mathcal{R}_\infty=2.5556\ldots$, and equals the trapped-gas specific-heat ratio $C(Tc^-)/C(Tc^+)$. Finite atom number rounds the cusp and weak interactions perturb it only weakly, leaving a measurable time-domain signature of condensation.

### [126] [Scattering, bound states, and resonances in the one-dimensional Dirac equation via supersymmetric quantum mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00306)
*Camila C. Soares,Luis B. Castro,Antonio S. de Castro*

TL;DR: 本文针对一维狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）在标量和矢量相互作用下的散射与离散谱问题，通过自旋对称性（spin-symmetry）条件将其约化为等效的Sturm--Liouville问题，并利用超对称量子力学（supersymmetric quantum mechanics）与形状不变性（shape invariance），以双曲Pöschl--Teller势为例给出了透射概率的闭式表达式；通过解析延拓（analytic continuation）统一描述了散射态与束缚态，并讨论了复动量平面上的极点模式与共振/准正则模（quasi-normal-mode）行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一维狄拉克方程的散射与束缚态问题通常需要分别处理，缺乏统一的解析框架；本文旨在建立一种基于自旋对称性的映射方法，将耦合的一阶狄拉克系统转化为一个等效的Sturm--Liouville（类薛定谔）问题，从而统一描述透射、反射与解析延拓行为。

Method: 在自旋对称性条件下，将一阶狄拉克方程组精确映射为单个自旋分量的Sturm--Liouville问题；针对双曲Pöschl--Teller型有效相互作用，利用超对称量子力学与形状不变性导出透射概率的闭式解；通过解析延拓从透射振幅的极点恢复束缚态谱；利用手征变换（chiral transformation）关联自旋对称性与赝自旋对称性（pseudospin-symmetry）扇区。

Result: 获得了双曲Pöschl--Teller势下透射概率的闭式表达式；通过解析延拓后的透射振幅极点重现了已知的束缚态谱；在势垒构型下给出了复动量平面上的极点模式及其与共振和准正则模行为的关联。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个统一处理一维狄拉克方程散射与束缚态的解析框架，建立了散射振幅与束缚态极点之间的直接联系；手征变换进一步允许结果在自旋与赝自旋对称性扇区间自由转换，避免了重复推导。

Abstract: We develop a unified treatment of scattering and discrete spectra for the one-dimensional Dirac equation with scalar and vector interactions. Under the spin-symmetry condition, the coupled first-order Dirac system maps exactly onto an effective Sturm--Liouville (Schrö\-din\-ger-like) problem for a single spinor component. This mapping provides a convenient framework for analyzing transmission, reflection, and analytic continuation. As an explicit application, we consider effective interactions of hyperbolic Pöschl--Teller type and exploit supersymmetric quantum mechanics and shape invariance to obtain a closed-form expression for the transmission probability. The bound-state spectrum is then recovered from the poles of the analytically continued transmission amplitude, reproducing known results and offering a unified description of scattering and bound states. For the barrier configuration, we briefly comment on the resulting pole pattern in the complex momentum plane and its connection with resonance and quasi-normal-mode behavior. Moreover, we use the chiral transformation to relate the spin- and pseudospin-symmetry sectors and translate results between them without repeating the full derivation.

</details>


### [127] [Wallis Products from the Four-Dimensional Singular Harmonic Oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00340)
*Bin Ye,Ruitao Chen,Lei Yin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从四维奇异谐振子（four-dimensional singular harmonic oscillator）出发，通过变分推导（variational derivation）得到了 Wallis 乘积（Wallis product）及其倒数形式，展示了这类无穷乘积源于径向变分动力学中共有的 Gamma 函数结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从量子力学系统的变分处理中自然导出 Wallis 乘积及其倒数，揭示该经典无穷乘积与奇异谐振子、Gamma 函数结构以及 Coulomb 对偶（Coulomb-dual）描述之间的深层数学物理联系。

Method: 作者在四维奇异谐振子中引入有效角参数 ν 吸收逆平方相互作用（inverse-square interaction），采用四次方试探波函数族（quartic trial family）$R_a(ρ)=Nρ^νe^{-aρ^4}$ 进行变分极小化，并利用径向 Kustaanheimo–Stiefel 关系 $r=ρ^2$ 连接四维谐振子与三维 Coulomb 问题。

Result: 变分极小化得到由相邻 Gamma 函数决定的准确度比值（accuracy ratio），在大 ν 半经典极限下该比值趋近于 1。限制 ν 为奇序列 $ν=2n-1$ 时得到标准 Wallis 乘积，偶序列 $ν=2n$ 时则得到其倒数形式。

Conclusion: Wallis 型无穷乘积在谐振子的逆平方形变（inverse-square deformation）下仍然存在，并源于径向变分动力学中统一的 Gamma 函数结构；Coulomb 对偶解释进一步将两支乘积分别关联到对偶 Coulomb/MICZ 描述中的整数与半整数有效角动量扇区（angular sector）。

Abstract: We present a variational derivation of the Wallis product and its reciprocal from the four-dimensional singular harmonic oscillator. The inverse-square interaction is absorbed into an effective angular parameter $ν$, so that the lowest exact energy in a fixed sector is $E_{4d,\mathrm{exact}}=\hbarω(ν+2)$. Motivated by the radial Kustaanheimo--Stiefel relation $r=ρ^2$ between the four-dimensional oscillator and the three-dimensional Coulomb problem, we use the quartic trial family $R_a(ρ)=Nρ^νe^{-aρ^4}$. The minimized variational energy yields an accuracy ratio governed by adjacent Gamma functions. In the large-$ν$ semiclassical limit, this ratio approaches unity. Restricting $ν$ to the odd sequence $ν=2n-1$ gives the standard Wallis product, whereas the even sequence $ν=2n$ gives its reciprocal form. The Coulomb-dual interpretation further relates the two branches to integer and half-integer effective angular sectors in the dual Coulomb/MICZ description. The result shows that Wallis-type infinite products persist under an inverse-square deformation of the oscillator and arise from a common Gamma-function structure in radial variational dynamics.

</details>


### [128] [Three-qubit nonlocality paradoxes: beyond GHZ](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00795)
*Nadish de Silva,Santanil Jana,Ming Yin*

Main category: quant-ph

Conclusion: 本文成功完成了对所有基于双条件奇偶性证明的三量子比特非局域性悖论的完全分类，揭示了该领域中此前未被认识到的丰富结构和复杂性。

Abstract: Quantum nonlocality paradoxes, such as that of GHZ, provide maximally sharp logical obstructions to classical probabilistic models of quantum correlations. They are key resources in a broad variety of information-theoretic tasks that exhibit unconditional quantum advantage. For example, in nonlocal games, which are communication tasks that serve as core technical tools in recent landmark results in quantum computational complexity theory.

  In this work, we completely classify all three-qubit nonlocality paradoxes established via a biconditional parity proof; this is a very large class of paradoxes that encompasses all earlier-known examples. We do this by introducing a suite of new structural and combinatorial techniques. ### [129] [Analytical connection between exact and approximate solutions of the periodically-driven two-level system starting from the Heun equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01030)
*Pietro Follia,Bassano Vacchini*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了描述线性驱动和旋转波近似（圆形驱动）下二能级系统动力学的严格解之间的解析联系。通过将薛定谔方程映射为Heun方程，并利用超几何函数、Floquet解和连分式展开，发展了一套微扰方法，不仅恢复了旋转波近似，还正确得到了Stark位移、Bloch-Siegert位移以及高频近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性驱动和旋转波近似（rotating-wave approximation）是周期性外场驱动二能级系统（two-level system）的两类重要情形，其严格解均可通过Heun方程获得，但两者之间的联系尚不明确。本文旨在建立这两类严格解之间的解析联系，从而统一理解不同驱动模式下的动力学行为。

Method: 将薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）映射为Heun方程：线性驱动对应汇合型Heun方程（confluent Heun equation），旋转波情形对应Heun方程（Heun equation）。通过分析以超几何函数（hypergeometric functions）表示的局部解，引入路径乘法性Floquet解（path-multiplicative Floquet solutions）和双边级数（bilateral series），导出两个连分式展开（continued-fraction expansions），并施加一致性条件进行微扰求解。

Result: 建立了线性驱动严格解与旋转波情形严格解之间的直接解析联系。该微扰程序不仅恢复了旋转波近似本身，还正确给出了Stark位移（Stark shift）、Bloch-Siegert位移（Bloch-Siegert shift）以及高频近似（high-frequency approximation）。

Conclusion: 周期性驱动二能级系统的线性驱动与旋转波近似两类严格解可以通过统一的解析框架相联系，该框架为理解不同驱动机制下的量子动力学提供了桥梁，并为更高阶修正的系统计算开辟了途径。

Abstract: We investigate and establish an analytic connection between the exact solutions describing the dynamics of a two-level system driven by periodic external fields, focusing on the cases of linear driving and the so-called rotating-wave approximation, or circular driving. In both cases, the exact solutions can be obtained by mapping the Schrodinger equation onto Heun equations: the confluent Heun equation for linear driving and the Heun equation for the rotating-wave case. In particular, we demonstrate a direct analytic connection between the exact solutions for linear driving and those for the rotating-wave case. This result is obtained by analyzing local solutions expressed in terms of hypergeometric functions, which, in the case of the confluent Heun equation, can be derived by considering path-multiplicative Floquet solutions involving a bilateral series. This series leads to two continued-fraction expansions that can be perturbatively solved by imposing a suitable consistency condition. The connection between the linear-driving and rotating-wave solutions is established through a perturbative procedure that allows us to recover not only the rotating-wave approximation itself, but also the correct Stark and Bloch-Siegert shifts, as well as the so-called high-frequency approximation.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两点能量测量方案（two-point energy measurement scheme）推导轨迹分辨的功统计生成函数；利用费米子高斯态形式论进行具体计算。

Result: 随机跳跃动力学下，功分布随着探测事件增加从梳状结构（comb-like structure）过渡到亚高斯尾部（sub-Gaussian tails）收缩的近高斯形式；受控跳跃中，因果非连接时每次跳跃贡献恒定能量，因果连接时平均功先下降后饱和呈亚线性增长；连续观测淬火（monitored quenches）会消除孤立淬火分布的精细结构，使统计趋近高斯分布。

Conclusion: 监测协议（measurement protocols）能显著改变功统计的分布形态，从离散梳状到连续高斯，调控非平衡功涨落的特征尺度与增长规律。

Abstract: We investigate work statistics in monitored transverse-field Ising chains subject to both a quantum quench of the transverse field and either stochastic quantum jumps or controlled measurement sequences. For generalized measurements, we derive a trajectory-resolved generating function for work statistics in the two-point energy measurement scheme. Evaluating it using a fermionic Gaussian-state formalism, we show that, under stochastic jump dynamics, the work distribution crosses over from a comb-like structure to an essentially Gaussian form with shrinking sub-Gaussian tails, as the number of detection events grows. For controlled jump protocols, the energy added by each jump is constant when successive jumps are causally disconnected but decreases and then saturates when they lie within each other's light cone, yielding linear and sublinear growth of the average work, respectively. For monitored quenches, continuous observation washes out the fine structure of the isolated-quench distribution and again drives the statistics toward Gaussian behavior.

### [134] [Coupling effect of nearest-neighbor interacting qubit chains to a single qubit system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00307)
*Manuel Allan L. Orongan,Lemuel John F. Sese,Rayda P. Gammag*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个定理，为任意与时间无关的哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）中不影响局部动力学、局部可观测量或任何局部现象的项提供充分判据，无需近似。通过在三个自旋链系统（含Ising相互作用、Dzyalonshinskii-Moriya相互作用及横向磁场）中验证，定理正确预测了约化动力学（reduced dynamics）行为，并阐明了不可交换性导致“涌现耦合（emergent coupling）”的物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子多体系统中，哈密顿量通常包含大量相互作用项，但部分项可能对局部物理现象无贡献。如何在不做近似的前提下，系统性地识别此类“惰性”项，是理解复杂量子系统局部行为的关键问题。

Method: 首先从数学上证明一个定理，为任意与时间无关的哈密顿量中不影响局部动力学、局部可观测量或任何局部现象的项给出充分判据，无需任何近似。随后通过三个量子比特链（qubit chain）系统进行解析验证：系统一为多链Ising相互作用；系统二将最后一个Ising相互作用替换为Dzyalonshinskii-Moriya（DM）相互作用；系统三在中间环境量子比特上施加横向磁场，使定理所需的交换关系不再成立。三个系统的约化动力学均通过解析推导获得。

Result: 定理正确预测了前两个系统的约化动力学行为。第三系统显示所有哈密顿量成分均贡献于约化动力学，验证了定理不适用时的情况。进一步分析第三系统非直接相互作用量子比特间的纠缠动力学，发现纠缠源于中间相互作用的非交换性（non-commutativity）产生的“涌现耦合”。

Conclusion: 该定理提供了一种无需近似即可识别哈密顿量中对局部现象无贡献项的有效判据。在研究涌现耦合时，该定理可用于排除那些不会产生涌现耦合的中间相互作用项，从而简化对非直接相互作用子系统间纠缠来源的分析。

Abstract: This study establishes a theorem that provides sufficient criteria for identifying terms in any time-independent Hamiltonian that have no influence on local dynamics, local observables, or any local phenomena, without any approximation. The usefulness of this theorem is demonstrated by predicting the behavior of three systems. The first system consists of multiple qubit chains with Ising interactions. The second system is formed by a single qubit chain, differentiated by the substitution of Dzyalonshinskii-Moriya (DM) interaction for the last Ising interaction. The predictions were verified by analytically deriving the reduced dynamics of both systems. A third system was also considered, namely, a short qubit chain with a transverse magnetic field on the intermediary environment qubit. This transverse magnetic field signals that the commutation relation required by our theorem no longer holds. The third system's local dynamics were also derived analytically, demonstrating that all Hamiltonian constituents contributed to the reduced dynamics. The physical consequences of our theorem's inapplicability were also explored using this third system by analyzing the entanglement dynamics between the qubits that do not directly interact. The results showed that the entanglement is caused by an \textit{emergent coupling} between the two non-directly interacting subsystems. This \textit{emergent coupling} arises from the non-commutativity of the intermediate interactions connecting the two subsystems. When searching for these \textit{emergent couplings}, our theorem can eliminate intermediate interactions that will not produce them.

*Feng-Li Lin,Ching-Yu Huang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过子系统热化（subsystem thermalization）与功统计（work statistics）两种操作诊断，研究周期驱动（Floquet）量子非可积Ising链的热化行为。结果显示两种诊断捕捉到相同的动力学交叉（dynamical crossover），从而建立了统一且实验可行的Floquet热化分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 同时采用子系统热化与功统计两种操作诊断：通过小子系统约化密度矩阵（reduced density matrix）精确测量局域平衡（local equilibration）并分辨预热化平台；利用功的特征函数（characteristic function）——包括含和不含两点测量（two-point measurements）的方案——以及相关涨落定理（fluctuation theorem）来捕捉相干贡献与热平衡偏差。

Conclusion: 子系统热化与功统计两种诊断在Floquet系统中揭示相同的热化交叉，这一统一框架可用于实验上表征相互作用量子系统中的Floquet热化、预热化区（prethermal regime）及相干能量吸收（coherent energy absorption）。

Abstract: We study Floquet thermalization in a periodically driven quantum non-integrable Ising chain by combining two operational diagnostics: subsystem thermalization and work statistics. For generic interacting Floquet systems, stroboscopic dynamics lead to heating toward an infinite-temperature state at low driving frequencies, to a prethermal state during the crossover regime, and then to a finite-temperature state at high driving frequencies. We show that reduced density matrices of small subsystems provide a precise measure of local equilibration and clearly resolve prethermal plateaus. In parallel, we analyze the statistics of work performed over a Floquet cycle using both the characteristic function of work with and without the two-point measurements, and the related fluctuation theorem, which captures coherent contributions and deviations from thermal equilibrium. By comparing these two diagnostics within the same Floquet setting, we demonstrate that work statistics encode the same dynamical crossover that governs subsystem thermalization. Our results establish a unified and experimentally accessible framework for characterizing Floquet thermalization, prethermal regimes, and coherent energy absorption in interacting quantum systems.

### [136] [Susceptibility-kinetic uncertainty relations for quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01035)
*Didrik Palmqvist,Ludovico Tesser,Janine Splettstoesser*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入部分动力学活性（partial dynamical activity）概念，并借助与系统-储库耦合重标度相关的量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information），建立了适用于任意开放量子系统的普适磁化率-动力学不确定性关系（susceptibility-kinetic uncertainty relation），从而将传统动力学不确定性关系（kinetic uncertainty relation）从经典随机过程拓展到量子体系，并证明该关系在弱耦合马尔可夫极限下能够还原已有定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过引入部分动力学活性，利用与系统-储库耦合重标度相关的量子Fisher信息，构建了一个磁化率项（susceptibility term）来保证对任意开放量子系统的普适有效性，该磁化率项可通过调节系统-储库耦合强度在实验上测量。

Result: 证明了所建立的磁化率-动力学不确定性关系在弱耦合马尔可夫极限下可以涵盖已有的动力学活性定义，并为基于关联函数的活性给出了信息几何（information-geometric interpretation）解释。通过对双量子点（double quantum dot）稳态输运的数值验证，展示了该关系在量子效应使传统动力学不确定性关系失效时仍能提供严格的精度约束。

Conclusion: 该磁化率-动力学不确定性关系为任意量子系统的精度优化提供了一种普适且强大的理论工具。

Abstract: Kinetic uncertainty relations bound current precision of stochastic processes by dynamical activity. The extension of these bounds to quantum systems has been impeded by coherence, strong system-reservoir coupling, and the subtlety of defining dynamical activity in the quantum regime. Here, we introduce a partial dynamical activity through the quantum Fisher information associated with the rescaling of the system-reservoir coupling and show that it bounds current precision via a universal susceptibility-kinetic uncertainty relation. The general validity of this relation for any open quantum system is guaranteed by the natural contribution of a susceptibility term, which is experimentally accessible by tuning the system-reservoir coupling strength. We show how the partial dynamical activity encompasses previous definitions of activity in the weak-coupling Markovian limit and that it provides an information-geometric interpretation of correlator-based activities. We illustrate the tight constraint on precision that our bound provides with the example of steady-state transport through a double quantum dot, where quantum effects invalidate previously developed kinetic uncertainty relations. We expect our bound to provide a powerful tool for optimizing precision in arbitrary quantum systems.

</details>


### [137] [Quantum-Informed Portfolio Selection: An End-to-End Pipeline Validated on Trapped-Ion Hardware with Real Market Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01037)
*Romina Yalovetzky,Martin J. A. Schuetz,Zichang He,Jiayu Shen,Yue Sun,Rudy Raymond,Shauna Sahay,Kishore Perla,Ruben S. Andrist,Grant Salton,Helmut G. Katzgraber,Roger Bongiovanni,Niraj Kumar,Rob Otter*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出 qReduMIS，一种递归混合量子-经典算法，将投资组合多样化问题建模为资产相关图上的最大独立集问题，利用量子近似优化算法（QAOA）识别冻结节点以引导经典约简，在 Quantinuum 98 量子比特离子阱系统上对多达 225 只资产的真实金融数据进行测试，在最大指标上成功概率达 0.95，平均近似比不低于 0.96，且时间求解标度指数比独立 QAOA 低 3.2 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 投资组合多样化是现代投资管理的基石，可形式化为资产相关图上的最大独立集问题，但在大规模场景下求解计算困难，亟需探索量子算法用于实际金融优化。

Method: 提出端到端 pipeline——qReduMIS，一种递归混合量子-经典算法。该方法并非直接用量子优化生成最终解，而是利用量子近似优化算法（Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm, QAOA）的最大独立集测量结果，识别可能属于最优解的冻结节点，从而引导并解锁后续（可证明最优的）经典约简步骤。

Result: 在四个主要市场指数（最多 225 只资产）的真实数据上，使用 Quantinuum 98 量子比特的 Helios 离子阱系统执行实验，QAOA 电路核最多 78 量子比特、1016 个双量子比特门。独立 QAOA 在 S&P 100 和 Nikkei 225 两个最大指数上无法找到最优解，而 qReduMIS 成功概率分别达到 0.40 和 0.95；所有四个指数的平均近似比不低于 0.96。在 H2-1 噪声模拟器上的系统基准测试显示，对于 p=2 层 QAOA，qReduMIS 的最优时间求解标度指数比独立 QAOA 小 3.2 倍。

Conclusion: qReduMIS 通过混合量子-经典递归策略显著提升了 QAOA 在投资组合多样化问题上的求解能力，在规模较大时仍能保持高成功概率和近似比，且标度性能优于独立 QAOA，展示了混合方法在金融优化中的实用潜力。

Abstract: Portfolio diversification - a cornerstone of modern investment management - can be formulated as a Maximum Independent Set (MIS) problem on asset correlation graphs. Solving this problem at scale is computationally challenging, motivating the exploration of quantum algorithms for practical financial optimization. We propose an end-to-end pipeline leveraging qReduMIS, a recursive hybrid quantum-classical algorithm. Rather than using quantum optimization to directly produce a final solution, qReduMIS leverages independent set measurements from the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA) to identify frozen nodes - vertices likely to belong to optimal solutions - thereby guiding and unblocking subsequent (provably optimal) classical reductions on the remaining graph. We benchmark qReduMIS on real financial data from four major market indices with up to 225 assets, executing experiments on Quantinuum's 98-qubit trapped-ion Helios system, with QAOA circuits acting on kernels of up to 78 qubits and 1016 two-qubit gates. While standalone QAOA fails to find the optimal solution for two of the largest indices (S&P 100 and Nikkei 225), qReduMIS achieves success probabilities of $0.40$ and $0.95$, respectively, with average approximation ratios $\geq 0.96$ across all four indices. We perform a systematic benchmark on the Quantinuum H2-1 noisy emulator over 73 asset correlation graphs of varying size showing that, for $p=2$ QAOA layers, the optimal time-to-solution scaling exponent of qReduMIS is $3.2$ times smaller than that of standalone QAOA.

### [138] [Polynomial equivalence of the global transverse-field Ising model and the gate model of quantum computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01227)
*Matthias Werner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在非单调时变全局横向场条件下，横向场伊辛模型（transverse-field Ising model）等价于门模型量子计算（gate model of quantum computation），可在多项式开销内模拟任意量子电路；该结果同时也意味着，若量子计算严格强于经典计算，则此类伊辛模型无法被高效经典模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 横向场伊辛模型在量子模拟与量子计算领域受到广泛关注，尤其是作为量子退火（quantum annealing）等模拟量子计算的物理平台。然而，该模型是否等价于门模型量子计算一直是一个悬而未决的问题，本文旨在回答这一核心问题。

Method: 基于Cesa和Pichler关于里德伯原子（Rydberg atoms）全局控制的最新结果，作者构建了一种利用具有全局横向场的伊辛模型来模拟任意量子电路的构造方法，并在时间、量子比特数和能量标度上证明了多项式开销。

Result: 对于非单调时变全局横向场的情形，该伊辛模型确实等价于门模型量子计算；所建立的多项式开销虽在现有量子硬件上过大，但为更优模拟方法的开发提供了动机。此外，若量子计算严格强于经典计算，则该模型无法被高效经典模拟，构成一条不可行定理（no-go theorem）。

Conclusion: 该结果连接了模拟量子模拟、量子优化、复杂性理论（complexity theory）与控制理论等多个领域，既为全局横向场伊辛模型的量子计算能力提供了肯定性证明，也排除了其高效经典模拟的可能性（在量子优势假设下）。

Abstract: The transverse-field Ising model has attracted a lot of attention in recent years, especially in the quantum simulation and quantum computation literature. This interest is driven by many platforms for analog quantum computation, which implement the transverse-field Ising model for solving optimization problems, such as quantum annealing. However, it has remained an open question whether the Ising model with a global transverse field is equivalent to the gate model of quantum computation. Here we answer this question affirmatively for the case of a non-monotonic time-dependent transverse field. Building on a recent result by Cesa and Pichler on global control of Rydberg atoms, we provide a construction that allows simulating arbitrary quantum circuits using the Ising model with global transverse field with polynomial overhead in time, qubit number, and energy scale. Although the polynomial overheads we establish here are large relative to what is feasible on real-world quantum hardware, our result motivates the development of more sophisticated methods for simulating quantum circuits using the Ising model with a global transverse field. Additionally, under the assumption that quantum computing is strictly more powerful than classical computing, our result serves as a no-go theorem for efficient classical simulation of the transverse-field Ising model with a time-dependent global transverse field. Therefore, our finding is relevant for multiple communities, from analog quantum simulation and quantum optimization on various platforms to complexity and control theory.

</details>

### [139] [Slow heat-driven flow in a gas of hard disks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00449)
*Amit Kumar,Abhishek Dhar,Baruch Meerson*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过理论推导与事件驱动分子动力学模拟，研究了受限通道中弹性碰撞硬磁盘气体的缓慢热驱动流动，验证了有限密度下等压气体动力学（isobaric gas dynamics）的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有等压流体动力学理论主要基于理想气体假设，缺乏对有限密度效应（finite-density effects）的探讨以及直接的粒子级模拟验证。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 首先在稀薄极限下将等压流体动力学理论简化为理想气体描述，然后引入硬磁盘流体的非理想状态方程（non-ideal equation of state），将其推广至有限密度情形，并数值求解一维方程。最后，采用事件驱动分子动力学模拟（event-driven molecular dynamics simulations）对理论进行直接检验。

Result: 有限密度效应会导致与理想气体预测的显著偏差。在稀薄和有限密度两种条件下，理论预测与分子动力学模拟结果均吻合良好。

Conclusion: 本文提供了首个针对强非均匀冷却流（strongly inhomogeneous cooling flow）中等压气体动力学的粒子级测试验证，确认了理论在有限密度范围内的有效性。

Abstract: We study a slow heat-driven flow in a gas of elastically colliding hard disks confined to a long channel. The initial state consists of two regions with large temperature and density contrasts but nearly equal pressures, leading to a low-Mach-number, nearly isobaric evolution. In the dilute limit, the corresponding isobaric hydrodynamic theory reduces to a previously known ideal-gas description. We extend this theory to finite densities by incorporating a non-ideal equation of state of a hard-disk fluid, and solve the resulting one-dimensional equations numerically. Finite-density effects produce appreciable deviations from the ideal-gas prediction. We then test the theory directly against event-driven molecular dynamics simulations of hard disks and find very good agreement in both the dilute and finite-density regimes. The results provide, to our knowledge, the first particle-level test of isobaric gas dynamics of a strongly inhomogeneous cooling flow.

*Vikas,Rahul Marathe,Anjan Roy*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文证明，除已知的生理量相关性外，单个细胞生长（stochastic single-cell growth）与随机不对称分裂（stochastic asymmetric partitioning）条件下的概率分布及其统计关系，同样可以区分不同的细胞分裂模型（Timer、Sizer、Adder）以及单细胞生长范式（线性与指数生长），并且这些结论在细胞生长速率与上一代相关时依然成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微生物细胞生长与分裂的调控机制复杂，现有研究主要通过出生尺寸、分裂尺寸等生理量的相关性来区分分裂模型（Timer、Sizer、Adder）。但单一的相关性分析可能不足以全面刻画不同模型的差异，需要探索更丰富的统计特征（如概率分布）来提升模型区分度。

Method: 论文首先将生理量之间的相关性分析推广至随机单细胞生长与随机不对称分裂的情形；随后引入这些量的概率分布以及它们之间的统计关系作为新的区分依据；最后将解析结果与已发表的实验数据进行比较，并检验当细胞生长速率与上一代细胞相关时结论的稳健性。

Result: 研究表明，生理量的概率分布及其统计关系不仅能区分Timer、Sizer、Adder三种分裂模型，还能进一步区分线性生长（linear growth）与指数生长（exponential growth）两种单细胞生长模式。将解析结果与实验数据对比后，验证了这种区分能力。此外，即使细胞生长速率与上一代存在相关性，上述结论仍然有效。

Conclusion: 概率分布和统计关系为区分细胞分裂模型与生长范式提供了比单纯相关性分析更强有力的工具，且该方法对代际生长速率相关性具有鲁棒性（robustness）。

Abstract: Complex interactions among regulatory molecules determine the rules underlying cell growth and division in microbial cells. While the governing molecular network may not always be obvious, it is well known that correlations among certain physiological quantities measured in experiments, such as birth-size, division-size, division-time, and division-added-size, can differentiate among various cell-division models, such as Timer, Sizer, and Adder. Here we show that, apart from these correlations, which we extend for the case of stochastic single-cell growth and stochastic asymmetric partitioning, probability distributions of these quantities and statistical relationships between them can also be used to differentiate between these division models. Interestingly, we show that these quantities can not only differentiate the division models, but also distinguish among the single-cell growth paradigms, such as linear and exponential growth. We then demonstrate this differentiability among various division and growth models by comparing our analytical results with published experimental data. We further show that these results remain valid even when the growth rate of a cell is correlated with the growth rate of cells from previous generations in the lineage.

### [141] [Power-Law Relaxation of Non-Gaussian Parameter and Self-Dynamic Structure Factor in Multidimensional Rugged Energy Landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00767)
*Bimman Bagchi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对多维粗糙能量景观中标记粒子的扩散，发展了一个基于关联淬火高斯随机场（correlated quenched Gaussian random fields）的理论框架，通过粗粒化迁移率场和迁移率-记忆近似，揭示了非高斯参数（non-Gaussian parameter）在不同维度下的长时间弛豫行为（$t^{-1/2}$ 在一维、$(\ln t)/t$ 在二维、$t^{-1}$ 在 $d>2$ 维度），并展示了粗糙能量景观在有效扩散系数、自动态结构因子和非高斯涨落弛豫中的独特特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粗糙能量景观（rugged energy landscape）会导致异质性迁移率（heterogeneous mobility）和非高斯扩散（non-Gaussian diffusion），但现有理论对有限时间扩散行为以及非高斯性弛豫的维度依赖机制尚缺乏系统描述。

Method: 将多维粗糙能量景观建模为关联淬火高斯随机场（correlated quenched Gaussian random fields），利用自传播子（self-propagator）和自动态结构因子（self-dynamic structure factor）表征有限时间扩散；引入粗粒化迁移率场（coarse-grained mobility field）和迁移率-记忆近似（mobility-memory approximation），将非高斯参数与粒子采样迁移率的时间关联建立联系。

Result: 在均匀化扩散区（homogenized diffusive regime），迁移率关联呈代数衰减，导致非高斯参数弛豫时间行为为：一维 $t^{-1/2}$、二维 $(\ln t)/t$、$d>2$ 时 $t^{-1}$，其幅度取决于维度和初始系综（initial ensemble）。

Conclusion: 粗糙能量景观在有效扩散系数（effective diffusion coefficient）、自动态结构因子和非高斯涨落弛豫中留下独特特征，理论框架统一描述了维度、空间关联和初始制备对非高斯扩散行为的影响。

Abstract: Ruggedness of the underlying energy landscape gives rise to heterogeneous mobility and non-Gaussian diffusion. We develop a theoretical framework for tagged-particle diffusion in multidimensional rugged energy landscapes modeled as correlated quenched Gaussian random fields. Using the self-propagator and self-dynamic structure factor, we characterize finite-time diffusion beyond the effective diffusion coefficient. We determine the effects of dimensionality, spatial correlations, and initial preparation. By introducing a coarse-grained mobility field and a mobility-memory approximation, we relate the non-Gaussian parameter to the time correlation of the mobility sampled by the particle. In the homogenized diffusive regime, the mobility correlation decays algebraically, leading to long-time relaxation of the non-Gaussian parameter as $t^{-1/2}$ in one dimension, $(\ln t)/t$ in two dimensions, and $t^{-1}$ for $d>2$, with amplitudes that depend on dimensionality and the initial ensemble. Our results show that rugged energy landscapes leave distinct signatures in the effective diffusion coefficient, self-dynamic structure factor, and relaxation of non-Gaussian fluctuations.

### [142] [Phase diagram of a double-occupancy cell model of a fluid with Curie-Weiss interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01009)
*R. V. Romanik,O. A. Dobush,M. P. Kozlovskii,I. V. Pylyuk,M. A. Shpot*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种具有居里-外斯（Curie-Weiss）相互作用的双占据元胞流体模型，发现其与完全图上的Blume-Capel模型同构；通过局域排斥与全局吸引相互作用的竞争，该简单模型展现出包括双临界点、三临界行为和三相共存在内的丰富热力学相行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索局域排斥与长程吸引竞争如何在最小多占据格气（multiple-occupancy lattice-gas）模型中产生复杂相行为，揭示其热力学机制。

Method: 通过从自旋变量到占据变量的简单变换，证明该模型与完全图上的Blume-Capel模型同构（isomorphic）；随后在巨正则系综（grand-canonical ensemble）中结合解析与数值方法研究其相行为。

Result: 该模型展现出单一临界点、两个不同临界点、三临界行为（tricritical behavior）以及三相点（triple-point）形成等多种热力学行为；当排斥足够强时，系统存在三种不同密度的流体相，导致气-液和液-液共存；确定了临界点、三临界点和三相点的位置并构建了相应相图。

Conclusion: 研究表明，双占据排斥与长程吸引之间的竞争足以在最小多占据格气模型中产生复杂的相行为，为理解类似系统提供了简化理论框架。

Abstract: A double-occupancy cell model of a fluid with Curie-Weiss interaction is studied. First, we show that the model is isomorphic to the Blume-Capel model on a complete graph through a simple transformation from spin to occupancy variables. We then investigate its phase behavior within the grand-canonical ensemble using a combination of analytical and numerical methods. Despite its simplicity, the model exhibits a remarkably rich thermodynamic behavior depending on the ratio between the local repulsive and global attractive interactions. We identify regimes characterized by a single critical point, two distinct critical points, tricritical behavior, and triple-point formation. For sufficiently strong repulsion, the system possesses three fluid phases of different densities, leading to both gas-liquid and liquid-liquid coexistence. The locations of the critical, tricritical, and triple points are determined, and the corresponding phase diagrams are constructed. These results demonstrate that the competition between double-occupancy repulsion and long-range attraction is sufficient to generate complex phase behavior in a minimal multiple-occupancy lattice-gas model.

### [143] [Universal Short-Imaginary-Time Quantum Critical Dynamics Near Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01076)
*Yu-Rong Shu,Yuan-Biao Li,Shuai Yin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子系统边界上的短虚时临界动力学，发展了普适标度理论并在二维量子伊辛模型中验证，发现了边界普适类所控制的丰富动力学临界行为，并揭示了边界初始滑移指数在量子-经典映射中的非常规表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虚时演化（imaginary-time evolution）长期以来被用作基态制备的标准范式，但其内在动力学性质在很大程度上被忽视了。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统研究量子系统边界上的短虚时临界动力学。

Method: 发展了描述边界短虚时临界动力学的普适标度理论（universal scaling theory），并在二维量子伊辛模型（quantum Ising model）中通过解析与数值手段进行了验证。

Result: 对于有序初始态，边界序参量（boundary order parameter）$M_s$随虚时$\tau$按$M_s \propto \tau^{-β_1/νz}$衰减；对于无序初始态，边界序参量的自关联由新临界指数$θ_1$控制。边界初始滑移指数（boundary initial-slip exponent）$θ_1'$在普通转变（ordinary transition）中为负，在特殊转变（special transition）中为正。此外，$θ_1$不遵循常规的量子-经典映射（quantum-classical mapping）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为边界临界动力学提供了新的物理见解，并为在量子多体系统中探测奇异的边界临界行为开辟了新途径。

Abstract: While imaginary-time evolution has long served as a standard paradigm for ground-state preparation in numerical simulations and quantum devices, its intrinsic dynamical properties has been largely overlooked. Here, we investigate the short-imaginary-time critical dynamics in quantum systems with boundaries. A universal scaling theory is developed and verified in the two-dimensional quantum Ising model, uncovering rich dynamic critical behaviors dictated by boundary universality classes. For ordered initial states, the boundary order parameter $M_s$ decays with imaginary time $τ$ as $M_s \propto τ^{-β_1/νz}$, where $β_1$ denotes the boundary order parameter exponent, and $ν$ and $z$ correspond to the correlation length exponent and the dynamic exponent, respectively. For disordered initial states, the autocorrelation of the boundary order parameter is governed by a novel critical exponent $θ_1$, which is closely related to the critical initial slip behavior of $M_s$ characterized by the corresponding exponent $θ_1'$. In contrast to its positive bulk counterpart, the boundary initial-slip exponent $θ_1'$ is negative for the ordinary transition while remaining positive for the special transition. Although the static universality classes of $d$-dimensional quantum phase transitions generally coincide with those of $(d+1)$-dimensional classical phase transitions, we show that $θ_1$ does not follow this conventional quantum-classical mapping. We further discuss the implications of our results for more exotic forms of boundary criticality. Our findings provide new physical insights into boundary critical dynamics and offer a novel route for probing exotic boundary critical behaviors in quantum many-body systems.

</details>


### [144] [Brownian ratchets and pumps universally simulate many-body active dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01231)
*Charles Stahl,Ethan Lake,Vedika Khemani*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明，两种简单的驱动机制——多体布朗泵（many-body Brownian pump）和多体布朗棘轮（many-body Brownian ratchet）——可以在任意弱噪声下普适地模拟自旋系统中的任何局域活性动力学（local active dynamics），并构建了一个双层伊辛棘轮模型，展示了利用稳态热流自主生成和稳定非平衡集体行为的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性系统（active systems）展现出大量平衡态下被禁止的现象，但其动力学通常由抽象的局域更新规则指定，物理上自然的驱动何时能产生相同行为尚不清楚。本文旨在建立简单物理驱动机制与抽象局域活性动力学之间的普适模拟关系。

Method: 以概率元胞自动机（probabilistic cellular automata）为显式模型，提出两种驱动机制：一是时间周期哈密顿量（time-periodic Hamiltonian）耦合冷浴的多体布朗泵；二是静态哈密顿量耦合热浴与冷浴的多体布朗棘轮，利用稳态热流驱动局域活性动力学。通过理论证明，任何连续时间或离散时间的局域活性动力学均可被这两种机制在任意弱噪声下近似模拟。

Result: 证明了对任意连续时间（或离散时间）局域活性动力学，总存在一个多体布朗棘轮（或泵）可在任意弱噪声下逼近该动力学。作为具体展示，构建了一个双层晶格上的简单铁磁伊辛棘轮（ferromagnetic Ising ratchet）：当两层分别耦合不同温度浴时，该模型即使在对称性破缺场下也能作为鲁棒的经典记忆，这在平衡态中是不可能的。

Conclusion: 棘轮机制可利用稳态热流自主生成并稳定新颖的集体行为，实现了非平衡多体动力学的一种新的静态设置。该工作为物理驱动的活性动力学提供了普适性理论框架。

Abstract: Active systems can exhibit a broad range of phenomena forbidden in equilibrium. Their dynamics are often specified by abstract local update rules, and it is generally unclear when the same behavior can arise from physically natural driving. Here we show that two simple driving mechanisms can universally simulate any local active dynamics in spin systems. The first is the familiar setting of a time-periodic Hamiltonian coupled to a cold bath, which we call a "many-body Brownian pump." As a second mechanism, we promote the Brownian ratchet, traditionally a mechanism for transport, to a "many-body Brownian ratchet": a static Hamiltonian coupled to a hot bath and a cold bath, where the resulting steady heat current can be harnessed not only to drive transport but also to generate local active dynamics. Using probabilistic cellular automata as an explicit model, we prove that for any continuous-time (or discrete-time) local active dynamics, there is always a many-body Brownian ratchet (or pump) that approximates the dynamics, up to noise that can be made arbitrarily weak by tuning energy scales and other parameters. As a concrete demonstration, we construct a simple ferromagnetic Ising ratchet on a bilayer lattice. When the two layers are coupled to baths at different temperatures, this model serves as a robust classical memory even under a symmetry-breaking field, something impossible in equilibrium. More broadly, our work shows that ratchets can use steady heat currents to autonomously generate and stabilize novel collective behavior, realizing a new static setting for nonequilibrium many-body dynamics.

</details>

### [145] [Constraining dark energy with complementary probes of large-scale structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31977)
*Neel Shah,Kazuya Koyama,Johannes Noller,Lanyang Yi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究利用有效场论框架（EFTofDE）结合多种大尺度结构探针（DESI DR1红移空间畸变、DES Y3 3×2点测量、ISW效应交叉关联）对暗能量扰动参数进行联合约束，相较于仅使用CMB+BAO+SNe数据，暗能量扰动参数{c_B, c_M}的优值（FoM）提升了2.69倍，映射到唯象函数{μ(z), Σ(z)}后FoM提升3.37倍，并发现w0wa参数与扰动参数之间存在显著互依性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为观测上确定暗能量（dark energy）的本质，需在背景膨胀之外一致地建模存在暗能量时的宇宙学扰动（cosmological perturbations），并通过多种互补探针对该联合理论空间进行约束。

Method: 在暗能量有效场论框架下约束模型，将膨胀历史探针与多种大尺度结构（large-scale structure）探针相结合，包括DESI DR1的红移空间畸变、DES Y3的3×2点测量、以及CMB温度各向异性与星系计数或CMB透镜化之间交叉关联所给出的积分萨克斯-沃尔夫效应。

Result: 最优数据集组合使暗能量扰动参数{c_B, c_M}的FoM提升2.69倍，映射到唯象函数{μ(z), Σ(z)}后FoM提升3.37倍；w0wa参数与扰动参数后验分布存在显著互依性，由梯度稳定性条件引入的理论先验导致；EFTofDE模型相较于ΛCDM的偏离显著性为2.9σ，与w0waCDM模型的3.1σ非常接近。

Conclusion: 不同大尺度结构探针之间具有互补性，可显著提升对暗能量扰动的约束能力；EFTofDE框架下参数间的理论先验（梯度稳定性条件）对后验分布有重要影响；当前数据对ΛCDM的偏离在EFTofDE和w0waCDM两种模型中表现出非平凡的相似性。

Abstract: To observationally pin down the nature of dark energy, it is essential to consistently model cosmological perturbations in the presence of dark energy alongside the background expansion and constrain this joint theory space with a large array of complementary probes. Here, we achieve this by constraining a model in the Effective Field Theory of Dark Energy (EFTofDE) framework by supplementing probes of the expansion history with several probes of large-scale structure: redshift space distortions (RSD) from DESI DR1, $3\times2$pt measurements from DES Y3, and the Integrated Sachs-Wolfe effect from cross-correlating CMB temperature anisotropies with galaxy number counts or CMB lensing. We demonstrate the complementarity of different probes which leads to strong improvements on constraints on DE perturbations. For our most constraining dataset combination that supplements CMB+BAO+SNe probes with DESI DR1 RSD, DES Y3 $3\times2$pt and ISW cross-correlations between CMB temperature and galaxy counts, we find an improvement in the Figure of Merit (FoM) for the DE perturbation parameters $\{c_B, c_M\}$ by a factor of 2.69. We show the phenomenological implications of these constraints by mapping them to the present-day values of the phenomenological functions $\{μ(z), Σ(z)\}$, where we see an FoM improvement by a factor of 3.37. We find a significant interdependence between the posteriors of $\{w_0, w_a\}$ and $\{c_B, c_M\}$, caused by the theoretical prior imposed by the gradient stability condition within the EFTofDE framework. Finally, we compute the significance of deviation from $Λ$CM for the EFTofDE model when constrained with CMB+BAO+SNe datasets, finding it to be at 2.9$σ$. This significance is nontrivially similar to the significance for the $w_0w_a$CDM model for the same dataset combination which we find to be 3.1$σ$.

### [146] [Towards Equations for String Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00071)
*A. Morozov,K. Pushkin,M. Reva*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨弦振幅（string amplitudes）在模空间（moduli space）上的积分满足的方程结构，发现开玻色弦树级振幅（tree-level open bosonic string amplitudes）在运动学变量上满足非平凡的线性差分方程（linear difference equations），而非粒子理论中常见的微分方程（Picard-Fuchs方程），且模空间上的分部积分（integration-by-parts）在弦论树级即可运作。低能极限平滑恢复代数量子场论结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准费曼积分（Feynman integrals）作为参数模空间上Picard-Fuchs方程的解被广泛研究，而弦振幅作为黎曼面（Riemann surfaces）真正非奇异模空间上的积分，其核心难题在于：单个弦振幅包含多个粒子图（particle diagrams）对应同一模空间的不同区域，但不同粒子图通常被认为满足不同方程，缺乏统一描述。作者以此为出发点开展研究。

Method: 从Koba-Nielsen图（Koba-Nielsen diagrams）出发，针对任意n点树级开玻色弦振幅，在运动学变量上构建完整的线性差分方程系统，其独立关系数匹配运动学参数数目。该方法利用了弦论树级模空间上的分部积分（与粒子圈中Picard-Fuchs方程背后的分部积分机制同源）。

Result: 发现对于粒子（particles）层次并无有趣结构，但开玻色弦树级振幅满足非平凡的线性差分方程，且模空间上的分部积分在弦论中早在树级层次就起作用。构建了完整的方程系统，独立关系数与运动学参数数目一致。与粒子情形不同，这些方程是差分方程而非微分方程。

Conclusion: 弦振幅在树级层次即可展现比粒子理论更丰富的方程结构（差分方程而非微分方程），低能极限$α\to 0$平滑恢复代数量子场论（algebraic QFT）的结构，表明弦论可能在更深层次统一不同粒子图的方程描述。

Abstract: Generic Feynman integrals are widely studied as solutions of Picard-Fuchs equations on moduli spaces of their parameters, and this calls for consideration of this phenomenon at a more basic level - of string amplitudes which are integrals over true non-singular module space of Riemann surfaces and their various generalizations. The main puzzle here is that a single string amplitude involves mane different particle diagrams, corresponding to different parts of the same moduli space, but different particle diagrams are usually believed to satisfy different equations, not unified into a common entity. We begin investigation of this problem, starting from Koba-Nielsen diagrams. While there is nothing interesting at this level for particles, the tree-level open bosonic string amplitudes satisfy non-trivial linear difference equations in kinematic variables. Moreover, the integration-by-parts on moduli space, standing behind Picard-Fuchs equations for particle loops, for strings are operative already at the tree level. We construct a complete system of such equations for arbitrary n-point tree amplitudes, with the number of independent relations matching the kinematic parameters. In variance with the particle case equations are difference ones rather than differential. The low-energy limit $α\to 0$ smoothly recovers the algebraic QFT structure.

</details>


### [147] [Holographic Spread Complexity from Branes and Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00074)
*Dimitrios Chatzis,Madison Hammond,Carlos Nunez,Alfonso V. Ramallo,Ricardo T. Santamaria*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过对偶性（AdS/CFT）中利用弦理论探针（D0膜、D3膜、基本弦）分析Krylov扩展复杂性（spread complexity），提出以Routhian替代Legendre变换修正固定荷描述下的短时行为，并验证了复杂度增长与边界场论参数的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在全息对偶理论中，Krylov扩展复杂性（spread complexity）的增长速率由体时空中的适当动量测量，但该方案在探针携带等距方向动量时与Krylov复杂性要求的短时行为产生冲突，需要更精确的固定荷描述（fixed-charge description）。

Method: 基于顶向下（top-down）超引力嵌入，分别在type IIA AdS₄×ℂℙ³背景（对偶于ABJM理论）和AdS₅×S⁵背景中构造D0膜、非BPS D3膜及缠绕基本弦的动力学，通过Legendre变换到Routhian（Routhian）修正固定荷描述，并从正则化单极子两点函数提取Krylov矩（Krylov moments）。

Result: 纯径向运动下，原动量的处方正确给出二次复杂度增长；带等距动量时，Routhian处方修复了短时行为；D3膜的角动量产生离心势垒（centrifugal barrier）并决定径向坠落条件；缠绕基本弦的Noether荷（Noether charges）需用固定荷Routhian处理，而缠绕数据（winding data）通过有效质量进入动力学。

Conclusion: 该工作为点状和扩展激发的全息扩展复杂性提供了弦理论实现，明确揭示了复杂度增长对场论参数（如单极子荷、角动量、缠绕数）的依赖关系。

Abstract: We study Krylov spread complexity in holographic theories using genuine string-theory probes. Building on the proposal that the growth rate of spread complexity is measured by a proper momentum in the bulk, we embed the falling-particle picture in top-down examples. We first analyse a D0 brane in the type IIA AdS$_4\times {\mathbb{CP}}^3$ background dual to ABJM theory, identifying it with a dressed monopole operator in the boundary CFT. For purely radial motion the proper-momentum prescription reproduces the expected quadratic growth of the complexity. When the probe carries momentum along an isometric direction, the naive prescription gives an apparent conflict with the short-time behaviour required of Krylov complexity. We propose that the correct fixed-charge description is obtained by Legendre transforming to the Routhian. We support the D0-brane interpretation through the regulated monopole two-point function, whose survival amplitude determines the Krylov moments, and we show that radial fluctuations give controlled corrections to the effective energy governing the complexity growth. We then extend the analysis to a rotating non-BPS D3 brane in AdS$_5\times S^5$, where angular momentum produces a centrifugal barrier and a sharp condition for radial in-fall. In the falling regime the Routhian prescription again gives the correct short-time behaviour. Finally, we consider a wound fundamental string in AdS$_5\times S^5$, which reduces to an effective massive falling particle. This clarifies the distinction between Noether charges, which require a fixed-charge Routhian treatment, and winding data, which enter through the effective mass. Our results provide a string-theoretic realisation of holographic spread complexity for point-like and extended excitations, making manifest their dependence on field theory parameters.

</details>


### [148] [Localization, Factorization and Dualities for Elliptic Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00076)
*Alessio Fontanarossa,Fabrizio Nieri,Antonio Pittelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了4维 $\mathcal N=1$ 超对称规范理论在环形-圆柱（torus times a cylinder）几何上的精确配分函数，构建了刚性超对称几何，通过等变局域化（equivariant localization）计算了手征多重态（chiral multiplet）的单圈行列式，得到了基于 theta 函数和三次相位（cubic phases）的基本模块，并证明了 Seiberg 型对偶（Seiberg-type dualities）作为 Jeffrey–Kirwan 留数（Jeffrey–Kirwan residues）的恒等式，同时探讨了与全纯块（holomorphic-block）分解及相关降维结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究 4 维超对称规范理论在具有两个边界分量的 Cyl = I × S^1 几何上的精确配分函数，旨在通过边界-边界椭圆核（boundary-to-boundary elliptic kernel）的形式理解边界极化效应，并探讨其与 Seiberg 对偶、全纯块分解及全息框架之间的深层联系。

Method: 采用等变局域化方法计算手征多重态在不同边界极化（Dirichlet 型和 Robin-like 型）下的单圈行列式，构造刚性超对称几何并确定 BPS 位形（BPS locus），利用 Jeffrey–Kirwan 留数验证秩改变（rank-changing）的 Seiberg 型对偶等式，并分析配分函数向全纯块波函数（holomorphic-block cap wavefunctions）的因子化过程。

Result: 得到由 theta 函数被三次相位修饰而成的基本构建模块；将 Seiberg 型对偶表示为椭圆核的 Jeffrey–Kirwan 留数恒等式；实现了降维到 3 维和 2 维的结果；并得到了 4 维 $\mathcal N=4$ 超杨-米尔斯理论（super Yang–Mills）和 Klebanov–Witten 理论的椭圆核，适用于全息应用。

Conclusion: 本文建立的边界-边界椭圆核框架统一处理了带有边界极化的超对称规范理论，揭示了 Seiberg 对偶在椭圆核层面的代数恒等式本质，并为全息对偶（holographic duality）和完整交集规范线性 sigma 模型（complete-intersection gauged linear sigma model）提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We study the exact partition function of 4d $\mathcal N=1$ supersymmetric gauge theories on a torus times a cylinder $\mathrm{Cyl}=I\times S^1$, where $I$ is a finite interval carrying two boundary components. Each endpoint supports an independent Dirichlet or Robin-like boundary polarization, so that the partition function is a boundary-to-boundary elliptic kernel. We construct the rigid supersymmetric geometry, determine the BPS locus, and compute the chiral-multiplet 1-loop determinants for the four possible boundary polarizations via equivariant localization. The resulting elementary building blocks are theta functions dressed by cubic phases. We then prove rank-changing Seiberg-type dualities as identities of Jeffrey--Kirwan residues of these elliptic kernels. We also discuss factorization into holomorphic-block cap wavefunctions represented by elliptic Gamma functions, dimensional reductions to three and two dimensions, complete-intersection gauged linear sigma models, and elliptic kernels for 4d $\mathcal N=4$ super Yang--Mills and the Klebanov--Witten theory, useful for holographic applications.

</details>


### [149] [Escape from Ostrogradsky via Hidden Ghost Parity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00096)
*Sam Bateman,Neil Turok*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过在一个不定内积空间（Krein空间）中量子化四阶导数理论，构造了一个紫外完备且具有一致微扰展开的量子场论，从而推翻了奥斯特罗格拉茨基（Ostrogradsky）通常解释下的“no-go”定理，并证明在该框架下所有树级跃迁概率均为正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对奥斯特罗格拉茨基“no-go”定理在量子场论（quantum field theory, QFT）中的通常解读——即高阶导数理论必然导致鬼态（ghosts）和不稳定性——提出反例，以证明在适当框架下高阶导数理论可以保持因果性、幺正性和正定概率。

Method: 在不定态空间——Krein空间（Krein space）——上采用协变量子化方法，确保微扰因果性（perturbative causality）和光学定理（optical theorem）所表述的幺正性（unitarity）在任意阶成立；推广玻恩规则（Born rule）到Krein空间；引入并利用隐藏的“鬼宇称对称性”（ghost parity symmetry），该对称性在将理论嵌入一个两导数、两场的O(1,1)对称微扰场论时显现。

Result: 尽管存在鬼态，所有树级跃迁概率（transition probabilities）均为正；四阶导数理论具有一致的微扰展开并能描述高能散射过程，从而构成奥斯特罗格拉茨基定理的一个反例。

Conclusion: 奥斯特罗格拉茨基的“no-go”定理在量子场论中的通常解读并非绝对成立；通过采用Krein空间量子化和鬼宇称对称性，可以构建具有正能量概率、因果性和幺正性的紫外完备高阶导数量子场论。

Abstract: We present a counterexample to Ostrogradsky's famous "no go" theorem as usually interpreted in quantum field theory (QFT), namely a four-derivative, UV-complete QFT with a consistent perturbative expansion which describes high energy scattering processes. We carefully quantize the theory on an $\textit{indefinite}$ space of states - a Krein space - using covariant methods which ensure perturbative causality and unitarity (in the form of the optical theorem) to all orders. We generalize the Born rule to Krein spaces and prove that all tree level transition probabilities are positive in spite of the presence of ghosts. A key role in the proof is played by a hidden "ghost parity" symmetry which becomes explicit when the theory is embedded in a two-derivative, two-field $O(1,1)$-symmetric perturbative field theory.

</details>


### [150] [Exploring Line Bundle Standard Models with Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00078)
*Jacky H. T. Yip,Alessandro Mininno,Gary Shiu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于Transformer的强化学习架构LB-Explorer，用于搜索光滑Calabi-Yau三折叠紧化产生的异质线丛标准模型，并构建具有SU(5)对称性的E8×E8真空，可进一步通过离散Wilson线破缺到标准模型规范群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦景观（string landscape）中高效搜索具有大量模量（moduli）的异质线丛（heterotic line bundle）标准模型，传统穷举搜索面临维度灾难，亟需可扩展的智能搜索工具。

Method: 采用基于Transformer的强化学习（reinforcement learning）架构LB-Explorer，结合CP-SAT求解器的混合架构，通过扰动LB-Explorer找到的解来精确施加部分约束条件。

Result: LB-Explorer能够高效学习线丛和（line bundle sums）上的约束条件，保证E8规范嵌入（gauge embedding）、反常消去（anomaly cancellation）、多稳定性（poly-stability，即超对称性）、谱的手征性（chirality）以及无奇异物质（exotic matter）。在CICY（complete intersection Calabi-Yau）流形上测试成功，架构可推广到任何具有光滑单纯形Mori锥（simplicial Mori cone）和自由作用离散对称性的CY流形。

Conclusion: LB-Explorer的通用性和可扩展性使其成为在大规模模量空间中导航弦景观的有力工具，代码已开源。

Abstract: We propose a Transformer-based Reinforcement Learning architecture, "LB-Explorer", to search for heterotic line bundle standard models arising from compactifications on smooth Calabi-Yau (CY) threefolds. We construct $E_8\times E_8$ vacua with $\text{SU}(5)$ symmetry, where the $\text{SU}(5)$ can be further broken to the Standard Model gauge group via discrete Wilson lines. We test the LB-Explorer environment on complete intersection Calabi-Yau (CICY) manifolds, though the neural network architecture naturally generalizes to any CY admitting a smooth, simplicial Mori cone and a freely-acting discrete symmetry. The LB-Explorer efficiently learns constraints on the line bundle sums, guaranteeing the $E_8$ gauge embedding, anomaly cancellation, poly-stability (supersymmetry), chirality of the spectrum, and the absence of exotic matter. Valid configurations can be subsequently filtered by imposing the missing constraints, such as the equivariant structure of the line bundle sum and further requirements on the particle spectrum. In this direction, we introduce a hybrid architecture incorporating CP-SAT solvers that aims to impose some of the conditions exactly by perturbing solutions found by the LB-Explorer. The versatility and scalability of the LB-Explorer make it a powerful tool for navigating the string landscape with a large number of moduli. The code and tools necessary to reproduce our findings are available at https://github.com/alexmininno/LB-Explorer

</details>


### [151] [QFT as a set of ODEs: higher dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00079)
*Fabiana De Cesare,Manuel Loparco*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将AdS₂中描述量子场论数据在相关变形下演化的常微分方程组推广至AdS₃和AdS₄，揭示了边界算符合并湮灭和能级排斥机制，并通过引入交叉方程和Padé近似提高了框架的实用性和收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论（QFT）在反德西特空间（AdS）中的局域算符关联函数完全由QFT数据——边界算符的标度维度Δᵢ、OPE系数Cᵢⱼₖ以及体-边界（BOE）系数b̂ᵢ——确定。此前相关工作仅针对AdS₂推导了QFT数据在体相关变形下的演化方程，本文旨在将该框架推广到更高维度的AdS₃和AdS₄。

Method: 本文推广了原先针对AdS₂的常微分方程组（ODEs），使其适用于AdS₃和AdS₄情形。为提高实用性，提出用交叉方程（crossing equation）替代OPE系数的ODE，并通过Padé近似（Padé approximants）加速边界算符求和的收敛性，至少在自由场理论中得到验证。

Result: 结果表明，这些流方程（flow equations）自然地捕获了边界算符达到边缘性（marginality）时的合并湮灭（merger-annihilation）机制，以及不同标度维度相互靠近时的能级排斥（level repulsion）现象。Paé近似显著改善了自由理论中边界算符求和的收敛表现。

Conclusion: 这些进展为流方程未来应用于AdS中强耦合QFT及其平直空间极限的研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Correlation functions of local operators in Quantum Field Theory (QFT) in Anti-de Sitter space (AdS) are completely fixed by the QFT data: the set of scaling dimensions $Δ_i$ and OPE coefficients $C_{ijk}$ of the boundary operators, and the bulk-boundary (BOE) coefficients $b^{\hatΦ}_i$ encoding how bulk fields decompose into boundary operators. In this work, we generalize the ordinary differential equations (ODEs) that govern the variation of the QFT data under a bulk relevant deformation, originally derived for AdS$_2$ \cite{Loparco:2026fki}, to the cases of AdS$_3$ and AdS$_4$. We demonstrate that these flow equations natively capture the mechanism of merger-annihilation when a boundary operator hits marginality, as well as level repulsion when different $Δ_i$'s approach each other. Furthermore, we address the practical implementation of the framework: we propose substituting the ODE for the OPE coefficients with the crossing equation for greater efficiency, and we observe that Padé approximants dramatically improve the convergence of the sums over boundary operators, at least in free theories. Altogether, these advances lay the groundwork for the future application of the flow equations to the study of strongly coupled QFTs in AdS and their flat space limits.

</details>


### [152] [Toward Hamiltonian simulations of Maxwell-Chern-Simons theory: constant modes and gauge field truncation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00082)
*Andrea Bulgarelli,Maria Cristina Diamantini,Nico Dichter,Lena Funcke,Tobias Hartung,Karl Jansen,Enrique Rico Ortega,Simran Singh,Lorenzo Spera*

TL;DR: 本文研究了(2+1)维Maxwell-Chern-Simons理论的常数模扇区，将其映射为具有扭曲边界条件的广义Harper-Hofstadter模型，并分析了格点截断向连续极限的收敛行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Maxwell-Chern-Simons (MCS)理论是兼具动力学自由度与拓扑自由度的拓扑规范场论（topological gauge theory）的典范模型，但其欧几里得形式存在符号问题（sign problem），使得哈密顿量数值方法尤为吸引人。为开展非微扰哈密顿量研究，需先理解该理论在有限维格点希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）中如何编码拓扑性质。

Method: 在空间环面（spatial torus）上研究常数模扇区（constant mode sector），构建平直联络（flat connections）环面的有限维离散化，将格点问题映射为具有扭曲边界条件（twisted boundary conditions）的广义Harper-Hofstadter模型。识别出有限格点精确再现连续理论的磁平移代数（magnetic translation algebra）和拓扑简并（topological degeneracy）的共度条件（commensurability conditions），并系统分析规范场截断及其向连续极限的收敛性。

Result: 成功将MCS理论的常数模扇区离散化为广义Harper-Hofstadter模型；给出了有限格点精确复现连续理论磁平移代数与拓扑简并的共度条件；展示了规范场截断的收敛性分析结果。

Conclusion: 该工作为MCS理论的非微扰哈密顿量研究奠定了第一步，验证了有限维格点离散化能够编码连续理论的拓扑性质，并提供了截断收敛的系统分析框架。

Abstract: Maxwell-Chern-Simons (MCS) theory in $2+1$ dimensions provides a paradigmatic example of a topological gauge theory with both dynamical and topological degrees of freedom. Its Euclidean formulation suffers from a sign problem, making Hamiltonian numerical approaches particularly attractive. As a first step toward the non-perturbative Hamiltonian study of MCS theory, we investigate the constant mode sector on a spatial torus. Being analytically solvable in the continuum, it provides an ideal benchmark for understanding how the topological properties of the theory are encoded in a finite-dimensional lattice Hilbert space. We construct a finite-dimensional discretization of the torus of flat connections and show that the resulting lattice problem maps onto a generalized Harper-Hofstadter model with twisted boundary conditions. We identify the commensurability conditions under which the finite lattice exactly reproduces the magnetic translation algebra and the topological degeneracy of the continuum theory. A systematic analysis of gauge field truncation and its convergence toward the continuum limit is then presented.

### [153] [From geometry to phenomenology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00187)
*Stefan Weinzierl*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论中的精确计算高度依赖费曼积分，而前沿费曼积分往往涉及复杂的混合几何结构（mixed type geometries），理解这些几何信息对提高计算效率至关重要。

Method: 从费曼积分中提取几何信息，并利用这些几何信息（如K3曲面、特定亏格曲线等）来优化费曼积分的计算方法。

Result: 在两圈级别的2→2散射过程（如Drell-Yan、Bhabha散射和Møller散射）中，已经出现了非平凡的混合几何结构。

Conclusion: 从费曼积分中提取的几何信息可以用于更高效地计算费曼积分，混合几何是当前研究的重点方向。

Abstract: Precision calculations in quantum field theory rely very often on perturbation theory and thus on the computation of Feynman integrals. Feynman integrals are also fascinating objects from a mathematical point of view and show deep connections to algebraic geometry. Cutting-edge Feynman integrals usually have geometries of "mixed" type, for example parts of it may correspond to a K3-surface, other parts may correspond to curves of a certain genus and the simplest parts correspond to points. In this talk I will discuss how to extract the geometric information from a Feynman integral and how this information can be used to compute more efficiently Feynman integrals. Non-trivial mixed geometries already occur in $2 \rightarrow 2$-processes at two-loops, like Drell-Yan, Bhabha and Moller scattering.

### [154] [Leggett-Garg inequality in the massive scalar vacuum: No violation under spacelike-separated measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00314)
*Yang Xiang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过利用量子场论（QFT）的因果结构，提出了一种在Leggett-Garg检验中严格满足非侵入可测性（NIM）要求的协议，并以此证明真空态不违反宏观实在论（macrorealism），突显了类空纠缠与时间宏观实在论之间的根本区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Leggett-Garg检验长期面临非侵入可测性（NIM）这一核心挑战，即无法保证测量不会影响被测量系统的后续演化。本文旨在利用量子场论（QFT）的因果结构克服这一困难，从而在严格满足NIM的条件下检验真空态是否违反宏观实在论。

Method: 作者利用QFT中类空分离事件的因果结构设计协议：使用三个独立的真空态系综，每个系综由不同观测者在类空分离事件处测量，得到三个双时关联子。事件位置设定为(0,0)、(τ,L)和(2τ,2L)，且满足L>τ+2τ_0（τ_0为时间窗口半宽），严格确保任何测量不对另一测量产生影响。研究选取1+1维自由有质量标量场的真空态，采用二分可观测量Q(f)=sign(φ(f))，其中φ(f)为涂抹场算符。在海森堡绘景中，时间演化被吸收为时间窗函数的平移，从而导出双时关联函数C(τ,L)和Leggett-Garg参数K₃=2C(τ,L)-C(2τ,2L)。对于重叠时间窗口的情况，采用矩形时间窗口进行数值计算。

Result: 对于非重叠时间窗口，有质量场的关联函数随τ呈指数衰减。对于重叠时间窗口的数值计算结果，在整个质量范围内均得到K₃<1，即真空态不违反Leggett-Garg不等式（LGI）。

Conclusion: 在严格非侵入条件下，真空态不违反宏观实在论，这与其在空间Bell不等式检验中众所周知的违反行为形成鲜明对比。该协议是QFT中首个严格满足NIM的LGI检验，为未来研究确立了方法学基准，并揭示了相对论量子场中类空纠缠与时间宏观实在论之间的根本区别。

Abstract: We overcome the long-standing noninvasive measurability (NIM) challenge in Leggett-Garg tests by exploiting the causal structure of quantum field theory (QFT). Our protocol uses three independent ensembles of the vacuum state, each measured by a different pair of observers at spacelike-separated events, yielding the three two-time correlators. By placing these events at positions $(0,0)$, $(τ,L)$, and $(2τ,2L)$ with $L>τ+2τ_0$, we rigorously ensure that no measurement can influence another. We investigate the vacuum state of a free massive scalar field in 1+1 dimensions, employing the dichotomic observable $Q(f)=\operatorname{sign}(φ(f))$ where $φ(f)$ is the smeared field. In the Heisenberg picture, the time evolution is absorbed into a translation of the time-window function, allowing us to derive the two-time correlation function $C(τ,L)$ and the Leggett-Garg parameter $K_3=2C(τ,L)-C(2τ,2L)$. For non-overlapping time windows, we find that the correlation function decays exponentially with $τ$ for a massive field. For overlapping windows, our numerical computation for a rectangular time window yields $K_3<1$ across the entire mass range, firmly establishing that the vacuum does not violate the LGI. Thus, under strict noninvasive conditions, the vacuum shows no violation of macrorealism, in stark contrast to its well-known violation of spatial Bell inequalities. Our spacelike-separated protocol provides the first LGI test in QFT with rigorously satisfied NIM, setting a methodological benchmark for future studies and highlighting the fundamental distinction between spacelike entanglement and temporal macrorealism in relativistic quantum fields.

</details>


### [155] [Hidden quantum-informatic symmetries of quasi-de Sitter backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00636)
*Suddhasattwa Brahma,Jaime Calderon-Figueroa,Xiancong Luo,Vincent Vennin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 研究发现，在Wands对偶意义下的准德西特（quasi-de Sitter）背景的简并性会反映在原初扰动的实空间量子关联中。尽管协方差矩阵的各个元素高度依赖于背景，但辛特征值（symplectic eigenvalues）及由其导出的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）、互信息（mutual information）、量子失谐（quantum discord）和对数负性（log-negativity）在Wands对偶实现中完全一致，从而揭示出德西特真空的一种全新“量子信息对称性”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Wands对偶（Wands' duality）意义下准德西特背景的简并性如何体现在原初扰动的实空间量子关联中，即背景的简并是否会在量子关联层面留下可观测的印记。

Method: 采用粗粒化标量涨落的连续变量高斯形式体系（continuous-variable Gaussian formalism），构建暴胀时空中一对局域模的协方差矩阵（covariance matrix），并提取系统的辛不变量（symplectic invariants）。

Result: 对于一般的Wands对偶背景对，协方差矩阵的单个条目高度依赖背景，但辛特征值以及由之推导的纠缠熵、互信息、量子失谐和对数负性在两个对偶实现中完全一致。

Conclusion: 揭示了德西特真空的一种新型“量子信息对称性”（quantum-informatic symmetry）：由粗粒化场构造的局域线性纠缠见证（local linear entanglement witnesses）无法区分Wands对偶的暴胀历史。这一对称性的核心在于Wands对偶是一种局域的、不依赖尺度的正则变换（local, scale-independent canonical transformation）。

Abstract: We investigate how degeneracies in quasi-de Sitter backgrounds, in the sense of Wands' duality, are reflected in real-space quantum correlations of primordial perturbations. Using the continuous-variable Gaussian formalism for coarse-grained scalar fluctuations, we construct the covariance matrix of a pair of spatially localized modes in inflationary spacetime, and extract the symplectic invariants of the system. For a generic Wands-dual pair of backgrounds, we find that while the individual entries of the covariance matrix are highly background-dependent, the symplectic eigenvalues -- and hence the entanglement entropy, mutual information, quantum discord and log-negativity -- all coincide for the two dual realizations. Our results unveil a new ''quantum-informatic symmetry'' of the de Sitter vacuum, according to which local linear entanglement witnesses constructed from coarse-grained fields cannot distinguish between Wands-dual inflationary histories, even though their background trajectories differ. We show that the special nature of the Wands-duality symmetry (of being local, scale-independent canonical transformations) is at the heart of this duality.

Method: 通过分析4维$\mathcal{N}=1$超引力（4d $\mathcal{N}=1$ supergravity）中极值三次耦合（extremal cubic couplings）与实Kähler不变超势（real Kähler-invariant superpotential）三阶导数之间的关系，并将该 formalism 应用于超对称DGKT真空（supersymmetric DGKT vacua）。

Result: DGKT场景中全息约束成立当且仅当Calabi-Yau三折叠是刚性的（$h^{2,1}=0$）；在Kähler+通用CS/dilaton扇区中极值三次耦合始终为零，而复结构扇区（complex structure sector）中则必然存在非零的（超）极值耦合。

Conclusion: DGKT场景下全息约束的有效性严格依赖于Calabi-Yau三折叠的刚性条件（$h^{2,1}=0$），这一结论深化了对全息对偶中几何约束的理解。

Abstract: We show that in the DGKT scenario on a generic Calabi-Yau three-fold, a recently proposed holographic constraint on cubic couplings is satisfied if and only if the Calabi-Yau is rigid, i.e. when $h^{2,1}=0$. More generally, we illustrate how in 4d $\mathcal{N}=1$ supergravity, extremal cubic couplings are determined by the third derivatives of the real, Kähler-invariant superpotential, while the eigenvalues of its Hessian compute the conformal dimensions of the dual scalar operators. These results extend more broadly beyond 4d $\mathcal{N}=1$ supergravity. Applying them to supersymmetric DGKT vacua, we prove that extremal cubic couplings always vanish in the Kähler + universal CS/dilaton sector, whereas non-vanishing (super-)extremal couplings are always present in the complex structure sector. Method: 通过对比边界天球共形场论关联函数与四维体振幅的软展开结构，分析天球代数在体描述中的适用性。具体考察软极限与共线极限在体振幅中的相互作用，并与边界描述进行比对。

Result: 体振幅中并不存在天球代数的平凡推广：仅靠前三个软展开项无法递归确定整个软展开。软极限与共线极限在体振幅中产生了边界描述所没有的微妙效应。

Conclusion: 天球对称代数在边界与体描述中的行为存在本质差异，体振幅中软极限与共线极限的耦合导致无法简单地将边界代数结构移植到体描述中。

Abstract: Soft and collinear limits of "celestial amplitudes" give rise to infinite dimensional symmetry algebras for two-dimensional (2D) "celestial" conformal field theories (CFTs). A small subset of these operators generates the action of the entire set recursively via the commutation relations. Insertion of this subset into celestial CFT correlators gives the boundary version of the first three terms in a soft expansion of the corresponding 4D bulk gravitational scattering amplitude. In this paper, we find that a bulk analog of this, which would allow the entire soft expansion of a gravitational amplitude to be determined via just the first three terms, does not follow trivially from the celestial algebras. We show how the interplay of soft and collinear limits results in subtleties for bulk amplitudes that do not show up in the boundary description.
