<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为拓扑弦自由能中非微扰贡献的Stokes常数与BPS/DT不变量（即D-膜多重数）一致的猜想提供额外证据，并探索该猜想的理论基础。

Method: 利用重求和理论（resurgence theory）分析非微扰贡献的模性质（modular properties）；论证非微扰贡献在稳定性腔（stability chamber）内由奇点诱导的局部单值群（local monodromy group）作用下形成轨道；并依据[DK26]的结果，展示非全纯配分函数（non-holomorphic partition function）的Stokes变换生成元满足Kontsevich-Soibelman李代数（Kontsevich-Soibelman Lie algebra）的李括号。

Result: 论证表明，同一轨道上的Stokes常数必须相同，从而在某些例子中可生成无穷多个Stokes常数并复现完整的BPS谱；同时表明全局Stokes变换可被识别为Kontsevich-Soibelman壁交叉不变量（wall-crossing invariant）。

Conclusion: 上述结果为Stokes常数与BPS/DT不变量一致的猜想提供了新证据，并建立了非微扰拓扑弦理论与Kontsevich-Soibelman壁交叉公式之间的深层联系。

Abstract: Topological string free energy has a rich collection of non-perturbative contributions which are labeled by D-brane charge vectors, and the associated Stokes constants are conjectured to coincide with BPS or DT invariants, i.e. D-brane multiplicities. In this paper, we provide additional evidence to this conjecture by studying modular properties of non-perturbative contributions. We argue using resurgence theory that non-perturbative contributions form orbits of local monodromy group induced by singular points inside a stability chamber, and that the associated Stokes constants must be the same across the orbits. In some examples, this allows generation of infinitely many Stokes constants, which reproduce the entire BPS spectrum. In addition, following [DK26], we also show that generators of Stokes transformations of non-holomorphic partition function satisfy Lie brackets of the Kontsevich-Soibelman Lie algebra, making it possible to identify the global Stokes transformation with the Kontsevich-Soibelman wall-crossing invariant.

</details>


### [160] [${\cal N}{=}\,4$ supersymmetric multiparticle systems based on indecomposable multiplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01107)
*Sergey Fedoruk,Evgeny Ivanov,Stepan Sidorov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过使用不可分解超多重态（indecomposable supermultiplets）(1,4,3)⊃+(4,4,0) 构造了带有自旋自由度的 N=4 超对称力学（supersymmetric mechanics）的新多粒子模型。这些模型是对标准不可约 d=1, N=4 多重态关联模型的形变，并由此得到了新的 N=4 超对称推广的 U(2)-自旋有理 Calogero 系统以及双曲 Calogero 系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 N=4 超对称力学模型多基于标准不可约 d=1, N=4 多重态，缺乏对更丰富代数结构的利用。作者希望引入非线性不可分解超多重态来构造形变模型，从而扩展超对称可积系统的家族，特别是带有自旋自由度的多粒子系统。

Method: 采用非线性不可分解超多重态 (1,4,3)⊃+(4,4,0)，对与标准不可约 d=1, N=4 多重态相关的模型进行形变（deformation），构造新的多粒子模型。通过这种超多重态构造方式，系统地导出超对称推广的 Calogero 模型。

Result: 发现了一个新的 N=4 超对称推广的 U(2)-自旋有理 Calogero 系统（rational Calogero system），该系统在 d=1 超共形群 OSp(4|2) 下保持不变。还得到了另一个形变模型，该模型对应于 N=4 超对称的 U(2)-自旋双曲 Calogero 系统（hyperbolic Calogero system），其哈密顿量相差某些 U(1) 生成元的平移。

Conclusion: 通过可分解超多重态构造方法，成功构建了 N=4 超对称力学的新多粒子模型，为带有自旋自由度的超对称可积系统提供了新的实现，并揭示了有理型和双曲型 Calogero 系统在超对称框架下的统一形变结构。

Abstract: We construct new multiparticle models of $\mathcal{N}=4$ supersymmetric mechanics with spin degrees of freedom by employing nonlinear indecomposable supermultiplets ${\bf (1,4,3){\supset\hspace{-1.1em}+}(4,4,0)}$. These systems are proper deformations of those associated with the standard irreducible $d=1, \mathcal{N}=4$ multiplets. In this way we find a new $\mathcal{N}=4$ supersymmetric generalization of U$(2)$-spin rational Calogero system invariant under $d=1$ superconformal group OSp$(4|2)$. One more deformed model reproduces $\mathcal{N}=4$ supersymmetric U$(2)$-spin hyperbolic Calogero system, up to a shift of the Hamiltonian by some U$(1)$ generators.

</details>


### [161] [Type IIB Axion--Dilaton Wormholes and the BPS Limit Hessian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01221)
*Soo-Jong Rey*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了IIB型轴子-膨胀子（axion-dilaton）欧几里得鞍点解，在特定轴子荷扇区中，BPS瞬子（instanton）与光滑喉部的非BPS虫洞（wormhole）分别对应E=0和E>0的解。通过哈密顿约束、规范商（gauge quotient）、荷扇区边界条件及零模消除，将二次作用量约化为物理Hessian，并证明了其可因式分解性，从而建立了端点定理（endpoint theorem），为虫洞能谱提供了更坚实理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视Type-IIB轴子-膨胀子欧几里得鞍点解的稳定性与能谱问题，澄清BPS瞬子与非BPS虫洞之间在涨落（fluctuation）问题上的差异，并验证虫洞能谱的可靠性。

Method: 在特定轴子荷扇区中，分别研究E=0（BPS瞬子）和E>0（非BPS虫洞）两种解；对瞬子情形，通过施加哈密顿约束（Hamiltonian constraint）、规范商（gauge quotient）、扇区边界条件并移除集体零模（collective zero modes），将二次作用量约化为物理Hessian，并证明该Hessian可因式分解为${\mathcal Q}_ν^\dagger{\mathcal Q}_ν$；此外将两末端虫洞喉部与其长程多极算符项分离，导出系数矩阵$C^{ij}$。

Result: E=0瞬子对应的物理Hessian可因式分解为${\cal H}_ν={\mathcal Q}_ν^\dagger{\mathcal Q}_ν$，这被解释为端点定理（endpoint theorem），超越了E>0虫洞的稳定性定理（stability theorem）。在两末端插入的不同分量与相同分量项均出现在同一二次表达式中，移除任意一项需要真正的投影或相消。

Conclusion: 该研究将Type IIB虫洞能谱建立在更可靠的基础上，并揭示了瞬子与虫洞涨落结构的深层联系，为理解弦理论中的非微扰效应（non-perturbative effects）提供了新的分析框架。

Abstract: I revisit Type-IIB axion--dilaton Euclidean saddles in a specified axion charge sector. In that sector, the solution with $E=0$ is the BPS instanton, while $E>0$ gives non-BPS wormholes with a smooth throat. The two cases solve the same radial equations but define different fluctuation problems. For the $E=0$ instanton, the Hamiltonian constraint, gauge quotient, charge-sector boundary condition, and removal of collective zero modes reduce the quadratic action to a physical Hessian. This Hessian factorizes, $ {\cal H}_ν={\mathcal Q}_ν^\dagger{\mathcal Q}_ν$. I interpret this as an endpoint theorem, beyond a stability theorem for the full $E>0$ wormhole. This puts Type IIB wormhole spectra on firmer grounds. I also separate the connected two-ended wormhole throat from its long-distance two-end multipole operator term. Once the coefficient matrix $C^{ij}$ is derived, the different-component and same-component placements of the two end insertions are terms in the same quadratic expression. Removing either term requires a genuine projection or cancellation.

</details>

### [162] [The Solar Neutrino and Astro-Particle PhYsics (SNAPPY) CubeSat Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00295)
*Brian M. Sutin,Edward Bierens,Brian Doty,Atri Dutta,Jonathan Folkerts,Brooks Hartsock,Kyle Messick,Holger Meyer,Daniel Reichart,Nick Solomey,Mark Crystal,Miguel Rodriguez-Otero,Evgeny Kuznetsov,Robert McTaggart,James Cutler,Joel Steinkraus,Jose G. Rivera*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: SNAPPY CubeSat（2026年5月3日发射）将在太空验证nuSol中微子探测技术，该技术利用镓同位素衰变产生的双脉冲信号区分中微子与宇宙射线。卫星采用3U CubeSat结构，搭载0.1公斤镓铝钆石榴石探测器，运行于极地低地球轨道，收集双脉冲事件数据，同时具备太阳风粒子测量与伽马射线暴探测等附加科学能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NIAC Phase II项目评审（2021年）确认了概念与科学可行性，但建议在推进完整任务研究前完成两项先导研究：表征探测器镓双脉冲信号在深空环境中的真实本底，以及收集具有统计学显著性的双脉冲事件以验证快速电子学器件能可靠地选择并分析该信号。SNAPPY任务正是为在太空中测试双脉冲信号而设计。

Method: 任务采用一颗3U CubeSat，搭载0.1公斤镓铝钆石榴石（gallium-aluminum-gadolinium-garnet）探测器，外部包裹主动反符合屏蔽阵列（active veto array）与屏蔽层。卫星运行于450公里或更高高度的极地低地球轨道，在范艾伦辐射带（Van Allen belts）上方的地球极区采集数据。屏蔽采用主动反符合屏蔽与被动屏蔽相结合的方式，被动屏蔽使用已获专利的钨粉与环氧树脂混合物，该材料在再入大气层时会解体。

Result: 探测器具有约7%的能量分辨率。在为期两年的扩展任务阶段，SNAPPY还能开展附加科学研究，包括：测量太阳风粒子密度与能谱，实现电子、质子、α粒子的粒子鉴别；以及探测来自银河伽马射线暴（galactic gamma-ray bursts）的极低能量伽马射线（无方向性）。

Conclusion: SNAPPY CubeSat将首次在太空条件下验证nuSol中微子探测技术的可行性，通过镓双脉冲信号实现太阳中微子的有效甄别，并为未来深空中微子探测任务奠定技术基础。同时，其扩展任务阶段的多项附加科学观测能力进一步提升了任务价值。

Abstract: The SNAPPY CubeSat, which was launched May 3, 2026, will demonstrate and space qualify the nuSol neutrino-detection technology. The nuSol technology detects solar neutrinos using a gallium isotope which decays by emitting two particles spaced apart in time; this allows differentiating neutrino events from cosmic rays. In the NIAC Phase II project review in 2021, concept and science were determined to be feasible; however, two precursor studies were recommended before pursuing a full mission study. These studies were to characterize the true deep-space background for the detector's gallium double-pulse signal and to collect a statistically significant number of double-pulse events demonstrating that fast electronics can reliably select and analyze this signal. To test double-pulse signals in space, a NIAC Phase III funded building a 3U CubeSat carrying a 0.1-kg gallium-aluminum-gadolinium-garnet detector housed within an active veto array and shielding. Because the detector requires deep-space-like conditions, the CubeSat is designed for a polar low-Earth orbit at 450 km or higher altitude, collecting data over the Earth's poles above the Van Allen belts. The detector is highly sensitive, with roughly 7-percent energy resolution, with active veto shielding and passive shielding using a patented tungsten-powder and epoxy mixture that disintegrates upon atmospheric reentry. SNAPPY enables additional science during the extended mission phase of year two operations. These include measurements of solar wind particle density and energy spectra with particle identification of electrons, protons, and alpha particles; detection of very low-energy gamma rays from galactic gamma-ray bursts without directionality.

</details>

Abstract: The vertex detector upgrade project for the Belle II experiment, based on CMOS depleted monolithic active pixel sensor technology, is planned to be carried out in conjunction with the major modification of the interaction region of the SuperKEKB collider during Long Shutdown 2 from 2032 to 2034. The MAPS sensor, named OBELIX currently under development, is derived from the successor to TJ-Monopix2, with modifications implemented to ensure compatibility with the Belle II trigger system. The new vertex detector consists of two layers of four self-supported consecutive OBELIX sensors, and three layers of discrete OBELIX sensors mounted on mechanical support structures with readout flex circuits attached to the sensors. The detector is arranged cylindrically around the beam pipe at radii ranging from 14 mm to 140 mm. The minimization of the material budget is required in order to enhance physics performance. We present an overview of the project and its latest developments, with particular emphasis on the development of low-material-budget flex circuits employing aluminum conductors.

### [164] [In-Situ Polarimetry in Collimated Magneto-Infrared Spectroscopy System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00689)
*Zeping Shi,Wenbin Wu,Zhiwei Zhang,Yuhan Du,Chenyao Xu,Congming Hao,Xiangyu Jiang,Xin Chen,Guangyi Wang,Mingsen Zhou,Chunhui Pan,Wei Lu,Hao Shen,Haifeng Pan,Zhenrong Sun,Junhao Chu,Xiang Yuan*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文报道了一套集成原位连续偏振测量功能的准直型磁光红外光谱系统，通过凯普勒光学结构抑制多反射导致的偏振退化，实现了线性、圆偏振及任意椭圆偏振态的连续原位调控，在50 mm磁体孔径内支持法拉第和福格特几何构型的透射与反射实验，系统最低均方根噪声为0.0033%，线性偏振消光比达40:1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强磁场下的磁光红外光谱（magneto-infrared spectroscopy）是研究朗道量子化（Landau quantization）和场致集体激发的重要手段，但长期以来由于红外光束在窄光管中经多次壁面反射导致偏振严重退化，缺乏原位偏振控制（in-situ polarization control）能力，限制了该方法潜力的充分发挥。

Method: 系统采用入射与出射准直室构成凯普勒光学架构（Kepler type optical architecture），将大孔径傅里叶变换红外光谱仪（FTIR）输出转换为低发散度光束，有效抑制长镀金光管内的多次反射路径。远程偏振模块由自动线偏振器和可切换菲涅耳菱形棱镜（Fresnel rhomb）组成，全部位于高场区外，无需热循环或手动重调即可实现线偏振、圆偏振及任意椭圆偏振态的连续原位切换。可互换紧凑聚焦模块支持在50 mm磁体孔径内的法拉第（Faraday）和福格特（Voigt）几何构型下的透射与反射实验。

Result: 系统实现了最低均方根噪声0.0033%、平均噪声0.0082%、线性偏振消光比（extinction ratio）高达40:1的性能指标。通过对多种单晶样品的磁光红外光谱进行连续原位线偏振测量和宽带圆偏振测量，验证了系统的实验能力。

Conclusion: 该平台为原位偏振分辨磁光红外光谱（in-situ polarization-resolved magneto-infrared spectroscopy）建立了一个稳健的实验框架。

Abstract: Magneto-infrared spectroscopy under strong magnetic fields provides a powerful probe of Landau quantization and field-induced collective excitations, yet its full potential has long been constrained by the lack of in-situ polarization control, because the highly divergent infrared beam propagating through narrow light tubes undergoes multiple wall reflections, leading to severe polarization degradation. Here we report a collimated magneto-infrared spectroscopy system that integrates continuous in-situ polarimetry. The system employs incident and exit collimation chambers forming a Kepler type optical architecture, which converts the large-aperture FTIR output into a low-divergence beam and strongly suppresses multi-reflection trajectories inside long gold-plated light tubes, thereby enhancing both optical throughput and polarization fidelity. A remotely controlled polarization module, consisting of an automated linear polarizer and a switchable Fresnel rhomb positioned entirely outside the high-field region, enables continuous in-situ tuning between linear, circular, and arbitrary elliptical polarization states without thermal cycling, manual realignment, or breaking vacuum. Interchangeable compact focusing modules further support Faraday and Voigt geometries in both transmission and reflection experiments within a 50 mm magnet bore, providing efficient beam focusing and signal collection while maintaining polarization fidelity. The setup achieves a minimum root-mean-square noise of 0.0033%, an average noise of 0.0082%, and a linear polarization extinction ratio up to 40:1. We demonstrate the capability through continuous in-situ linear polarimetry and broadband circular polarimetry in the magneto-infrared spectroscopy of various single crystals. This platform establishes a robust experimental framework for in-situ polarization-resolved magneto-infrared spectroscopy.

</details>

### [165] [Depth Two Mock Modularity by Eisenstein Series Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00643)
*Kathrin Bringmann,Caner Nazaroglu*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文通过“耦合”一对产生深度一模形式（depth one mock modular forms）的艾森斯坦级数（Eisenstein series），提出了一种构造深度二模形式（depth two mock modular forms）的新方法，为高深度模形式（higher depth mock modular forms）提供了独立于不定 theta 函数（indefinite theta functions）的新途径，并以 Vafa-Witten 不变量中的深度二对象为例进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度二及更高深度的 mock 模形式（mock modular forms）在数学物理和枚举几何中具有重要应用，但此前主要通过不定 theta 函数及其变体来构造，缺乏其他独立方法。本文旨在提供一种基于艾森斯坦级数的全新构造途径。

Method: 通过“耦合”（coupling）一对能够产生深度一 mock 模形式的艾森斯坦级数，构造出深度二的 mock 模形式。该方法区别于已有的不定 theta 函数框架。

Result: 成功证明了艾森斯坦级数的耦合可以生成深度二的 mock 模形式，为高深度 mock 模形式提供了新的独立构造方法。并以 Vafa-Witten 不变量中出现的深度二对象为例进行了说明。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个不依赖不定 theta 函数的、基于艾森斯坦级数的新框架，用于研究高深度 mock 模形式，拓展了该领域的研究工具。

Abstract: The notion of depth two and higher mock modular forms have found important applications in mathematical physics and enumerative geometry since their inception through indefinite theta functions with general signature. These theta functions generalize Zwegers' work on Lorentzian signature lattices and the framework of mock modular forms that emanated from it. Mock modular forms can also be studied through Eisenstein and Poincaré series. The interaction of this second point of view with the indefinite theta function approach yields a wealth of tools to unearth the rich structure behind mock modular forms. For mock modular forms of higher depth, on the other hand, indefinite theta functions and their variants largely remained the only available approach. In this paper, we show that one can indeed get mock modular forms of depth two by "coupling" a pair of Eisenstein series that yield depth one mock modular forms, thereby providing a new and independent approach to higher depth mock modular forms. We exemplify this new perspective on a depth two object that appeared in the context of Vafa-Witten invariants.

</details>

### [166] [Periodic orbits with prescribed negative energy for relativistic Keplerian problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00478)
*Alberto Boscaggin,Guglielmo Feltrin,Duccio Papini*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文通过变分方法（variational approach）研究了相对论方程中具有给定能量的周期解的存在性。该方程包含开普勒奇点（Kepler singularity）和一个低阶扰动势能$W$。主要困难在于该奇点对于 Maupertuis 泛函而言正好处于弱力（weak force）与强力（strong force）临界边界，导致紧致性缺失。作者采用惩罚程序（penalization procedure）和 min-max 方案结合碰撞近邻临界序列的爆破分析（blow-up analysis），证明了在任意维度 $N\geq 2$ 上、给定负能级下非微扰（non-perturbative）周期解的存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究相对论框架下具有开普勒势（Kepler potential）及低阶扰动的动力学方程中，具有预定能量的周期轨道是否存在。该问题中的奇点对泛函紧致性构成临界困难，需要发展新的变分工具加以克服。

Method: 采用 Maupertuis 变分原理将问题转化为对 Maupertuis 泛函的临界点搜索；针对奇点导致的紧致性缺失，引入惩罚程序（penalization procedure）修改泛函，并结合 min-max 方案（min-max scheme）与近碰撞临界序列（near-collision critical sequences）的爆破分析（blow-up analysis）恢复紧致性。

Result: 在任意维度 $N\geq 2$ 上，对于给定的负能量水平，证明了该相对论方程存在周期解。所得结果是非微扰的（non-perturbative），不依赖于小参数或弱耦合假设。

Conclusion: 通过综合惩罚、min-max 与爆破分析等方法，成功克服了开普勒奇点处于弱力-强力临界边界所带来的紧致性困难，在非微扰意义上建立了具有给定负能量的周期解存在性定理。

Abstract: Using a variational approach, we study the existence of periodic solutions with prescribed energy for the relativistic equation \begin{equation*} \dfrac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}\left(\dfrac{m\dot x}{\sqrt{1-|\dot{x}|^{2}/c^{2}}}\right) = -α\frac{x}{|x|^{3}} + \nabla W(x), \qquad x\in\mathbb{R}^{N}\setminus\{0\}, \end{equation*} where $W$ is a lower-order perturbation of the Kepler potential. The main difficulty stems from the fact that the Kepler singularity is critical for the associated Maupertuis functional, lying exactly at the boundary between the weak force and strong force regimes. To overcome the resulting lack of compactness, we use a penalization procedure and develop a suitable min-max scheme combined with a blow-up analysis of near-collision critical sequences. As a consequence, we establish the existence of periodic solutions on prescribed negative energy levels, obtaining non-perturbative results in every dimension $N\geq 2$.

</details>
